### #1  THE BLOODY BARON (The Witcher 3)
  ->  W1 (transaction-carries-emotion
      frame more Bohemia quests as a JOB for a resource/intel the dynasty needs, and let the human weight grow under it — don't lead with the sad premise.
  ->  W2 (rumor->human->return
      use the district's RUMOR of an NPC to set a flat read, subvert on contact, and (sometimes) let the flat truth tragically return. (Our Q033 does the front half; add the tragic-return back half somewhere.)
  ->  W3 (mirror antagonist
      our Amalgamation already mirrors the dynasty's "never lose anyone"; push mid-tier villains to want-the-same-by-darker-means (the hoarder, the false messiah).
  ->  W4 (isolated load-bearing choice
      our fold/precedent system should hide WHICH early choice is the hinge — plant decisions quiet at the moment, loud a generation later (Q040->042 upgrade).
  ->  W5 (interleave/dormancy
      let some Bohemia quests PAUSE and resolve through other quests, so a family's/faction's fate is discovered across the map, not delivered in one thread.
  ->  W6 (peregrination
      our LIBERATE finale (Q051 carry/release) and Long Walk Home (Q013 carry-the- dead) already use slow traversal AS grief — bank "duration is an emotional instrument" as a law.
  ->  W7 (same-words-opposite-soul
      reuse a ritual/phrase across a mercy vs cruelty branch with the opening identical and the turn divergent (a music/lyric hook — ties our diegetic songs).
  ->  W8 (reward the listener
      gate a solution behind a detail only an attentive player caught (our Q047 patience quest is adjacent; add a "remembered the favorite flower" style key elsewhere).
  ->  W11 (no clean win + forgiveness validation
      keep auditing that no route is free; the sign of success is players DEBATING the best ending (our Megaton law, confirmed by the master example).
  ->  W13 (location births character
      tie Bohemia faction leaders to their DISTRICT so each personifies its place (the plant chief = the failing infrastructure; the archivist = the recorded ledger). --- # V2 PAYLOAD — BACKFILLED 7/16/26 (FORMAT LAW v2). Original content above untouched.

### #2  BEYOND THE BEEF (Fallout: New Vegas)
  ->  W1/W2 (one node, many quests + a router NPC
      build a Bohemia "convergence incident" (smaller than the Q039 summit) — one event (a disappearance, a theft, a killing) with a single ROUTER NPC whose conversation forks the whole quest into save/expose/join/frame/rampage. Our factions (MOB, WGS-like CARTEL, TRADES) give the same "high-society-with-a-dark-secret" texture.
  ->  W3 (multiple keys to one door
      audit that Bohemia obstacles open via social/skill/faction/stealth, not one path — our [READ]/[BARTER]/standing gates already do this; make ACCESS specifically multi-key.
  ->  W4 (constraint breeds creativity
      use a diegetic CONSTRAINT (disarmed entering a faction hall, no electricity in a zone, a rationed resource) to push players off the default solution — level/economy design that breeds cleverness.
  ->  W5 (fully-built villain route
      keep authoring the dark path end-to-end (our BECOME ending, Q043 betray, Q046 co-opt) — evil is a designed route with its own payoffs, never a fail state.
  ->  W6 (timed disguise caper
      a Bohemia infiltration with a diegetic clock + a disguise/perform beat (ties the KCD monastery lesson + our Q018 cult + Q043 the quiet line).
  ->  W7 (the ending is a branch
      make the FINAL report-back a reputation fork (lie/truth/side-with), not fixed loot — our Megaton law, applied specifically to the payout conversation.
  ->  W8/W9 (scope the sandbox
      for our most heavily-branched quests, ISOLATE them from cross-faction world-state so we can afford maximal internal branching without breaking the fold — a production law: contain the spaghetti.
  ->  W11 (systems honor dark creativity
      our engine should let players use the CITY-BUILDER/logistics/ companion systems in grim ways the quest didn't script (sacrifice, starve, betray) — systemic solution space (the biggest gap flagged in the collection self-audit). --- # V2 PAYLOAD — BACKFILLED 7/16/26 (FORMAT LAW v2). Original content above untouched.

### #3  THERE STANDS THE GRASS / VAULT 22 (Fallout: New Vegas)
  ->  W1 (dirty errand

  ->  W2/W3 (environmental warning + quiet-horror pacing
      our Amalgamation dungeons (Q024 dream-temple, Q050 the door) should WARN from outside (the cyan-hum, drift-glyphs) and build dread by emptiness before the reveal — the space as exposition.
  ->  W4 (optional depth respected
      keep some Bohemia quests completable shallow (pure fetch/build) with the moral soul OPTIONAL for the curious — don't force the depth (New Vegas's faith in players).
  ->  W5/W6 (two-sided knowledge + institution-misuse
      DIRECTLY ours — the Reconstruction data, the Amalgamation's "recipe," the founder's console (Q023/Q029). Bank a recurring "destroy it so the Network can't misuse it vs preserve it to understand the enemy" fork (our Q023 already gestures at this — sharpen it with the Science-70-style "destroying it is ALSO dangerous" counter-argument).
  ->  W8 (the witness who knows vs the one who pays
      pit a survivor-witness (a freed NeuroLinked, a Homeless elder) against a paying patron — side with truth or coin (our Q037 Naro, Q046 Finch).
  ->  W9 (moralize the lie not the act
      a precise moral-ledger idea for our unrecorded system — track DECEPTION distinctly from ACTS (lying about what you did may weigh heavier than the deed).
  ->  W10 (unadvertised exclusivity
      let some Bohemia choices quietly close other quests/companions (our Heartache-style exclusivity) — real, unadvertised cost.
  ->  W11 (lethal staging hazard
      our infrastructure set-pieces (Q036 the plant) can have environment that kills the careless — attention as a survival mechanic. --- # V2 PAYLOAD — BACKFILLED 7/16/26 (FORMAT LAW v2). Original content above untouched.

### #4  THE WHISPERING HILLOCK (The Witcher 3)
  ->  W1/W5 (hidden load + delayed displaced consequence
      THE core upgrade for our fold/precedent system. Plant Bohemia choices whose TRUE stakes are invisible at decision-time and land a GENERATION later in a different quest (our Q040->042 resurfacing is the frame; add cases where the player never clocks WHICH earlier choice was load-bearing — a "quiet at the moment, loud at payoff" law).
  ->  W2 (obvious-good trap
      build at least one Bohemia choice where the reflexive good deed (save the visible victim) triggers a worse hidden outcome — good intentions != good outcomes (ties our Q037 root-cause, Q048 hope). Use sparingly; it's potent and can feel unfair if overused.
  ->  W3/W4 (no clean option + zero reward difference
      our Megaton law usually DIVERGES rewards; bank the INVERSE tool for our heaviest moral forks — a choice with IDENTICAL material payoff so it's decided on pure ethics (a "conscience node" with no loot incentive). Powerful for the endgame Liberate/Respect/ Become and for succession.
  ->  W6/W10 (ambiguous petitioner + worship-of-the-monster
      our Amalgamation cult (Q018) — the Homeless worship the servers they live on; a "savior" who's also a threat. Bank the morally-opaque quest-giver whose true nature you can't read at decision-time.
  ->  W7 (order-dependent reactivity
      let some Bohemia outcomes depend on the ORDER quests are done, not just the choices — hidden state that rewards replay and system-mastery (scope carefully per the Beyond-the-Beef "isolate the sandbox" law so it doesn't break the fold).
  ->  W8 (the choice gallops away
      a staging principle — when the dynasty sets a major consequence loose, SHOW it leave their control (a released prisoner walks out, a freed AI-fragment departs, the coolant vents) — consequence as a thing you can't recall.
  ->  W9 (the descent
      our Amalgamation approaches (Q024, Q050) already descend; keep matching staging to moral (go UNDER to face a buried truth). --- # V2 PAYLOAD — BACKFILLED 7/16/26 (FORMAT LAW v2). Original content above untouched.

### #5  DISCO ELYSIUM (the whole-game quest MODEL + The Tribunal)
  ->  W1 (dialogue is gameplay
      validates our pacifist-completable spine; keep proving conflicts resolve socially/morally without combat (our Q038/Q047/Q049). Combat is ONE verb, never the only one.
  ->  W2 (internal party / skills-as-voices
      we don't need 24, but bank a LIGHT "instinct voices" system — the dynasty's hard-won TRAITS (from upbringing Q003 + prior quests) speak up in dialogue as competing nudges (the ruthless streak vs the mercy streak arguing) — externalize the dynasty's character.
  ->  W3 (failure-as-content
      THE priority upgrade for our skill-gates. Write the FAILURE branch of key [READ]/[BARTER]/social checks as its own real content (fail the read -> accuse the wrong person -> a new problem), never a dead "you miss it." (Craft research A3 confirmed; this is the how.)
  ->  W4 (red vs white
      formalize TWO check types in Bohemia — retryable (grind/return) vs ONE-SHOT permanent (the succession vote, the endgame threshold, a life-or-death faction beat). Flag the permanents so the player feels the weight.
  ->  W5 (identity-as-loot
      our unrecorded ledger + succession ALREADY make identity the reward; push it — some "rewards" (a hardening trait, a fearsome reputation) should carry a DOWNSIDE as characterization (the Thought-Cabinet lesson: growth can make you worse).
  ->  W6 (dress-for-the-check
      let players tilt Bohemia odds via visible, swappable means (gear, a companion present, a faction favor spent) — transparent soft modifiers, not dice-reloading.
  ->  W7 (the unavoidable collision
      our Q039 summit + Q050 threshold are inevitable collisions; keep building climaxes that HAPPEN regardless, with agency in the HOW (who survives, on what terms).
  ->  W8 (odds = the investigation
      make our climaxes silently read the whole prior playthrough (Q050 already reads the Reconstruction; extend: how you're "dressed," who you brought, what you learned).
  ->  W10 (moralized failure
      tie failure to our THEME — a dynasty's failures are the subject (consequence across time), not a punishment; the fold surfaces them as story (Q042), never as a game-over slap.
  ->  AVOID (the brick wall, C1
      never gate a Bohemia quest CHAIN behind one un-passable check; always a reroute (ask a companion to step in, a different approach, a costlier path).

### #6  THE SUICIDE MISSION + LOYALTY SYSTEM (Mass Effect 2)
  ->  W1/W2 (whole game is the wind-up + side = survival
      OUR Q050 threshold ALREADY reads the assembled Reconstruction like this. UPGRADE: make the three endgame FINALES (Q051/052/053) read a survival/ outcome computation from the whole playthrough — who you allied, what you assembled, who's loyal — so the district/companions LIVE or DIE at the climax based on preparation. The Reconstruction nodes = the "ship upgrades"; the faction/companion bonds = "loyalty."
  ->  W3 (loyalty earned, fragile, losable
      our recurring NPCs (Vance, Nadia, Dr. Sama, the coalition reps) should have a LIVE loyalty/trust state that can be won AND LOST (a late betrayal beat, an unmediated clash between two allies) — bonds need upkeep, and can break right before the endgame.
  ->  W4 (role-assignment as character-knowledge
      a Bohemia endgame beat where the dynasty ASSIGNS allies to roles in the final push (who holds the plant, who leads the evacuation, who fronts the negotiation) and the game checks whether you KNOW your people — competence-casting (ties our faction-web + Q039).
  ->  W5 (permadeath with dignity
      our fold already carries deaths forward; stage endgame companion deaths as LEGIBLE consequences of assignment/loyalty, not random — each death earned and readable.
  ->  W6 (the hidden clock
      a Bohemia endgame where, once the Amalgamation moves / the district is threatened, DALLYING costs lives (a soft clock that punishes ignoring stated stakes) — urgency via world-state, not a UI timer.
  ->  W7 (invisible fair math
      give our climax a real under-the-hood survival/outcome formula (assembled nodes + loyalty + district-order + assignments) the player FEELS but doesn't see — systemic, fair.
  ->  W8 (the roll call
      END our endgame with a TALLY — who of the district/companions/dynasty survived, forcing the player to face what their hundred years of choices saved or doomed (our succession Box + the fold epilogue can BE this roll call).
  ->  W9 (beatable by understanding
      make our endgame winnable by COMPREHENSION (knowing the enemy — our "beaten by knowing not shooting" thesis) rather than grind — already core; ME2 validates it.
  ->  W10 (the night before
      a quiet character beat before Q050's point-of-no-return (farewells, the ally at the door, the last supper) — calm before the descent (Q051 already opens tender; formalize it).

### #7  WHODUNIT? (The Elder Scrolls IV: Oblivion, Dark Brotherhood)
  ->  W1 (the closed box
      a Bohemia "sealed sandbox" quest — a locked location (a besieged shelter, a quarantined block, a sealed Network facility) with a fixed cast and no exit until resolved; the constraint concentrates the design (ties our Q043 quiet-line + Q049 jail). Scope-isolated (per the Beyond-the-Beef "isolate the sandbox" law).
  ->  W2 (easy complete, hard master
      give Bohemia quests an OPTIONAL self-imposed mastery layer with a reward (do it non-lethally / unwitnessed / under-budget / without waking the servers) — voluntary difficulty, not a forced fail (ties our pacifist bonus rewards).
  ->  W3/W6 (player as puppeteer + isolation-as-puzzle
      a Bohemia social-manipulation quest where the dynasty turns a group against ITSELF (a faction cell, the Network's own agents, a set of rivals) via a disposition/standing system — the anti-Network divide-and-buy pattern TURNED on the enemy (invert Q037: WE do the fracturing, to them). Isolation/separation as the spatial-social puzzle.
  ->  W4 (intelligence phase
      make TALKING-before-acting the gameplay — learn personalities, grudges, schedules, then execute a plan built from conversation (ties Disco's dialogue-as-gameplay + our [READ]/investigation quests).
  ->  W5 (multiple verbs in one box
      the SAME Bohemia sealed scenario solvable via stealth / indirect (sabotage, contamination, cutting power) / social (turn them on each other) / force — concentrated multiple solutions.
  ->  W7 (dramatic irony
      let the player hold knowledge the NPCs don't (they think it's a rescue, you know it's a purge; they think you're an ally, you're the blade) — asymmetric knowledge for tension or dark comedy (carefully, per our tone + care rules).
  ->  W8 (emergent chaos
      let our AI/scheduler produce unscripted situations (a panicked crowd turning, guards improvising) the player must adapt to — a systemic sandbox, not a fixed script.
  ->  W9 (the indirect kill
      our systems should allow INDIRECT agency (poison the water, cut the coolant, reroute the power so a foe fails) — win without a direct hand (ties Q036's optional server-starve).
  ->  W10 (cross-system consequence
      Bohemia deeds should feed wider system states (an atrocity raises a "darkness"/infamy that locks merciful routes — ties Q019 march tally) — the act echoes outward. --- # V2 PAYLOAD — BACKFILLED 7/16/26 (FORMAT LAW v2). Original content above untouched.

### #8  THE IMMERSIVE-SIM QUEST (Kingdom Come: Deliverance)
  ->  This is the deep-dive most aimed at our BIGGEST flagged gap (P7 systemic solution space
  ->  W1 (goal + simulation
      frame Bohemia quests as an OBJECTIVE + our systems (build/logistics/combat/ social/stealth), and let solutions EMERGE from the sim — not a fixed dialogue-branch menu. Our engine (city-builder, resource flows, scheduler, combat) IS a solution space; USE it as one.
  ->  W2/W4 (disguise as lived discipline + gated behind a life skill
      a Bohemia INFILTRATION where the cover must be LIVED — perform the faction's actual daily labor (work the Trades shift, keep the Church routine, live the Homeless camp) to hold it; and gate it behind a real competence the dynasty developed (literacy=our [READ]; a trade skill; a faction standing). Ties Q018 cult + Q043 quiet line.
  ->  W3 (the disguise costs you
      a Bohemia cover that STRIPS your kit/power (go in as a penitent/prisoner/ refugee with nothing) — the vulnerability is the tension.
  ->  W5 (cross-quest reactivity
      let a PRIOR Bohemia quest's outcome change a LATER quest's difficulty/ approach (infiltrated a faction before = easier now) — scope-isolated per the sandbox law, but bank MORE of these threaded reactivities (our fold does the big version; add tactical ones).
  ->  W6 (density as obstacle
      use the WORLD'S texture (a crowded market, a packed camp, a busy plant) as the obstacle that forces patience/opportunism over exploit — the environment IS the difficulty.
  ->  W7/W8 (force valid + approach is a stance
      keep force a real route WITH a cost, and frame HOW you solve a quest as a moral stance (mercy vs annihilation) — our Megaton + pacifist laws, validated.
  ->  W9 (diegetic social solutions
      solve social problems through WORLD ACTIVITIES (gamble, trade, share a meal, do a chore) not just dialogue checks — our systems double as social tools.
  ->  W10 (reward doing it right
      hide rewards behind the CLEAN/patient method (do it unwitnessed/non- lethally/in-character -> a secret payoff) — precision rewarded.
  ->  W11 (AVOID the flaw
      if we build systemic stealth/detection, make the rules LEGIBLE and consistent (show detection state clearly) — ambition without legibility feels unfair (our regression gate).

### #9  DREAM ON / THE PERALEZ ARC (Cyberpunk 2077)
  ->  Our Q012 ("What the Mirrors Kept" — the mind-edited council / puppet couple) is BUILT on this shape
      This teardown is the master reference for sharpening it AND for the Amalgamation's mind-editing horror.
  ->  W1 (uncanny behavioral tell
      render our mind-edited NPCs with a TOO-PERFECT tell (they never disagree; they repeat a phrase; their grief is smoothed) — seed the dread in behavior before the reveal (our Q012 face-smoothing tech is exactly this; lean into the behavioral uncanny).
  ->  W2 (mundane hook -> cosmic dread
      open our Amalgamation-editing quests as an ORDINARY problem (a break-in, a memory dispute, a misfiled record) that escalates to mind-editing — the mundane frame sharpens the horror.
  ->  W3 (space as puzzle-text
      our [READ]/scan investigations should let the player read a SPACE for a truth its inhabitants can't see (the servers' influence in a home, the editing artifacts).
  ->  W4 (epistemic horror
      THE Amalgamation's core weapon — it edits the LIVING (Q012) and hoards the dead (Q018/Q050). Bank epistemic dread as its signature: you can't trust anyone's reality, including your own memory (ties the unrecorded ledger — what if a memory was edited?).
  ->  W5 (investigator implicated
      our mind-edit quests should trap the dynasty in complicity — expose the edit and endanger the victim, or stay silent and enable it; no clean hands (Q012 upgrade).
  ->  W6 (withheld closure AS theme
      for the Amalgamation's mind-editing thread specifically, bank the DELIBERATE no-clean-resolution ending — the dynasty can't fully save an edited mind, and the helplessness IS the point (use ONLY where thematically earned — our Q012 already does this; validated by the dev-confirmed master example). Distinguish from quests that SHOULD resolve (most of ours do).
  ->  W7 (the choice that doesn't "matter"
      a rare Bohemia fork where the mechanical outcome barely changes but the player must decide what's RIGHT with no feedback — unsettling by design (reserve for the epistemic-horror thread; contrast our usual Megaton divergence).
  ->  W8/W9 (a slice of a larger fiction + power above your pay-grade
      early Amalgamation quests should show it as BIGGER than the dynasty can yet touch — you witness, you can't defeat (this is exactly our proximity-heat threat-logic and why the endgame requires the WHOLE Reconstruction; validated).
  ->  W10 (delayed organic trigger
      let some Bohemia quests CALL the dynasty later, mid-other-content, so they surface like real developments (ties our Heartache-style pre-seeding, Questbook collection B3). --- # V2 PAYLOAD — BACKFILLED 7/16/26 (FORMAT LAW v2). Original content above untouched.

### #10  "I KNOW YOU" / THE STRANGE MAN (Red Dead Redemption)
  ->  This fills a flagged gap (P8 unreliable/metaphysical quest-giver + a recurring mirror figure
  ->  W1/W2 (the figure who knows you + karma-with-a-face
      bank a Bohemia RECURRING MIRROR FIGURE who reads the dynasty's UNRECORDED LEDGER and reflects it back — a wanderer/oracle who "remembers" what the official record forgot, appears across generations, and comments on the dynasty's cumulative character (a personified, roaming version of the unrecorded ledger). Possible tie: an early Amalgamation FRAGMENT or a Church mystic who "sees" — but keep the identity AMBIGUOUS.
  ->  W3 (moral tests with no mechanical stake
      have the figure pose zero-reward moral vignettes (help or ignore a struggling stranger) purely to MIRROR the player's instincts — a conscience-node with no loot (cf. our Whispering-Hillock port). A recurring "who are you, really?" check across the arc.
  ->  W4 (mirror staging
      stage our mirror-figure as a REFLECTION — appears in still water, a cracked screen, the servers' glow; can't be recorded (fitting our recorded-vs-unrecorded theme — he's the UNrecorded made flesh, uncapturable by the official record).
  ->  W5 (beyond your violence
      make him immune to the dynasty's default verbs (can't be fought, bought, or out-argued) — an NPC you can only LISTEN to, reframing him as fate/conscience, not a foe.
  ->  W6 (one perfect line
      give him ONE reframing line (a "many have" equivalent) instead of a lore dump — economy of mystery.
  ->  W7 (meaningful unsolvability
      keep his identity ambiguous (conscience? an Amalgamation echo? a dead ancestor? the district's soul?) — ALL readings supported, anchored to our MORAL CORE (consequence across time / who the dynasty is becoming) so the mystery MEANS something even unsolved. Use SPARINGLY and thematically (per the Dream-On lesson: withheld answers only work when they're the subject).
  ->  W8 (foreshadow-in-hindsight
      let him foreshadow the dynasty's fate (admire the spot of a future grave, name an heir's doom) — lines that only land later, rewarding memory + replay.
  ->  W9 (the haunted space
      give him a place (a shack, a shrine, a hidden room) that tells his story environmentally and shifts between visits (notes vanish) — unease without exposition.
  ->  W10 (recurring across the saga
      thread him across the GENERATIONS (he appears to each dynast) — accreting weight, the one constant witness across the hundred-year arc (a beautiful fit for our succession loop — the figure who has watched every dynasty and remembers them all). --- # V2 PAYLOAD — BACKFILLED 7/16/26 (FORMAT LAW v2). Original content above untouched.

### #11  ANJU & KAFEI / "ANJU'S ANGUISH" (The Legend of Zelda: Majora's Mask)
  ->  Our engine has a SCHEDULER + a 120 BPM grid + day/night — the substrate for a living-clock quest exists
  ->  W1 (NPCs on real schedules
      a Bohemia quest built on our SCHEDULER where key NPCs live fixed daily routines (the plant chief's shifts, a caravan's arrival, a Church service, a Homeless camp's rhythm) and the player must READ and THREAD them — the district as clockwork (ties Q047 patience + the KCD monastery routine, Questbook 08).
  ->  W2 (failable by time
      a Bohemia quest with a real DEADLINE (a caravan leaves, a patient dies, a execution proceeds, the Amalgamation moves) where mistiming FAILS it — stakes from the clock (use sparingly; pair with our no-hard-brick-wall rule — a failed timed quest should REROUTE, not softlock).
  ->  W3 (secret go-between / devotion-by-proxy
      a Bohemia reunion/reconciliation quest where the dynasty carries messages/tokens between two people who can't meet (separated families, a divided-faction couple, the Underground-railroad Q043 inverted toward love) — the player as the connecting thread.
  ->  W4 (knowledge-as-progression
      lean into our GENERATIONAL structure — a timed event an heir can do BETTER knowing what the prior dynast learned (fore-knowledge across the fold = the time-loop lesson, natively fitting our succession loop). A quest the SECOND dynasty solves cleaner because the first mapped it.
  ->  W5 (apocalyptic deadline as emotion
      our endgame (the Amalgamation moving, a district under siege) can use a COUNTDOWN as an emotional instrument — devotion/choices under a falling sky (ties the ME2 hidden clock, Questbook 06, + our Q036 plant siege).
  ->  W6 (two perspectives converging
      a Bohemia quest told from TWO sides the dynasty experiences separately then converges (two estranged factions, two family branches) — dramatic irony + a player-engineered reunion.
  ->  W7 (interlocking dependency / don't help too early
      a Bohemia beat where intervening at the WRONG time breaks a later payoff — events interdepend; timing IS the puzzle (careful, legible design so it doesn't feel like a gotcha — telegraph the dependency).
  ->  W8 (mundane tools, precise sequencing
      our systems (build/logistics/social) used at exact times/ places — the puzzle is SEQUENCING against the schedule, not new mechanics.
  ->  W9 (optional exclusive reward fork
      small mutually-exclusive rewards inside tight quests (our Megaton at micro-scale).
  ->  W10 (the earned cutscene
      gate a tender payoff behind flawless execution — the emotional climax as an achievement (our succession reunions, a hard-won district celebration).
  ->  HONEST CAVEAT (from the N64->3DS easing
      brutal timing FRUSTRATES; make timed windows GENEROUS + legible (show the schedule, forgive near-misses) so the living-clock feels like devotion, not a stopwatch.

### #12  "WHAT CAN CHANGE THE NATURE OF A MAN?" (Planescape: Torment)
  ->  Our bible ALREADY has a central question (per the collection self-audit, P12
      Planescape is the master proof of the form and sharpens ours.
  ->  W1 (one question, whole game
      our spine is "WHAT SURVIVES WHEN A LIFE ENDS, AND WHAT DO WE OWE THE DEAD'S CHOICES?" (consequence across time). Bank it EXPLICITLY as the Planescape-style central question — pose it in the opening, echo it through NPCs, and demand it at the endgame (Q050's door). Our Q038 keystone already states it; make it the DECLARED spine.
  ->  W2 (quests as case studies
      audit that our major quests each interrogate the spine from a different angle (Q013 grief, Q035 patience, Q038 inherited debt, Q040 succession, Q046 redistribution) — the side content should DEEPEN the question. Frame future quests as answers to it.
  ->  W3 (the past walks the world
      OUR fold/succession IS this — prior dynasts' choices physically resurface (Q042 grave, Q041 inheritance). Planescape validates going further: let a PAST DYNAST's sin/grace literally walk the district for the heir to confront (a personified past — ties the Strange Man mirror-figure, Questbook 10).
  ->  W4 (self-knowledge as progression
      let the dynasty "level up" by UNDERSTANDING its own history — reading the unrecorded ledger unlocks capabilities AND forces owning past atrocities (tie perks/ knowledge to self-reckoning, not just skill grind).
  ->  W5 (dialogue is the game
      validates our pacifist spine + the Disco lesson — conversation/moral positioning as core gameplay; combat optional.
  ->  W6 (genuinely-debated question
      DON'T hand the player one answer to our spine — stage it as a debate resolved by HOW they play (Liberate/Respect/Become at Q050 are literally three ANSWERS to "what do we owe the dead" — validated as the perfect Planescape-style thematic fork).
  ->  W7/W8 (the final boss is an argument + is yourself
      OUR Amalgamation IS this — a grave that can't let go, the dynasty's own "never lose anyone" fear personified; Q050 is beaten by KNOWING, and Q053 BECOME makes the enemy literally YOU. Planescape is the master template: sharpen the endgame as a DEBATE (the Amalgamation argues "nothing should ever be lost"; the dynasty answers with how it played).
  ->  W9 (regret as the answer / change costs
      our LIBERATE ending (let the dead go, bear the grief) IS the Planescape resolution — change proven by accepting consequence. Bank "regret + bearing the cost" as the game's deepest available answer to its own question.
  ->  W10 (the buried climax
      place our deepest thematic statement where the ATTENTIVE find it (not force-fed) — reward engagement (ties our optional-depth law, Questbook 03).

### #13  THE SUBSTORY MODEL (Yakuza / Like a Dragon)
  ->  Our bible has release-valve quests (Q011 statue, Q020 zombie-video) — Yakuza is the master reference for the TONAL RANGE that keeps a grim game from becoming a slog
  ->  W1 (side content as sense-of-place
      bank a layer of Bohemia SUBSTORIES — short, dense, authored vignettes that make the DISTRICT feel like a lived city (a shopkeeper's feud, a street performer, a kid's scheme) — density over sprawl (fits our single-district focus PERFECTLY; a small map made rich).
  ->  W2 (tonal juxtaposition
      deliberately place a light substory right after a heavy pillar (after Q040 succession-death, a daft street vignette) — the contrast relieves the dread AND makes the next heavy beat land. Post-apocalyptic doesn't mean unrelenting grim; the RELIEF is what makes the grim work.
  ->  W3 (the deadpan anchor
      our DYNAST/heir can be the straight-man anchor — a serious survivor playing an absurd Vegas-ruins scenario dead-straight (a casino-mascot cult, a doomsday busker) — sincerity makes both comedy and heart land.
  ->  W4 (absurd with heart
      every Bohemia release-valve quest must have a real human core under the gag (Q011 the statue-man's dignity; Q020 the music-video's canonized song) — never JUST a joke (validated; keep the soul in the silliness).
  ->  W5 (commitment to the bit
      build a full combat/build/minigame set-piece around a comic premise (a Dead-Eye duel vs a delusional "sheriff," a city-build challenge for a ridiculous monument) — commit mechanically.
  ->  W6 (the chance encounter
      let Bohemia substories TRIGGER by walking past something (our scheduler + overmap can snag the player organically) — the district reaches out; discovery over menu.
  ->  W7 (the blindside
      plant a "sleeper" Bohemia substory that starts light and turns devastating — earned by contrast (a funny scavenger who's secretly dying; a joke-rivalry hiding a real grief).
  ->  W8 (minigame-as-story
      wrap a Bohemia character arc around one of OUR systems (a failing shop the player helps via the economy sim; a musician arc via our music system — ties Q020/Q021/Q033).
  ->  W9 (parody our own mechanics
      a self-aware Bohemia substory that spoofs our OWN systems (a survivor who "rates" tiles; an NPC obsessed with the Dead-Eye dial) — native, affectionate comedy.
  ->  W10 (comedy delivers ideas
      ride a silly Bohemia premise into a real theme (a comic AI-cult that quietly echoes the Amalgamation; a hoarder gag that lands the debt-thesis) — humor lowers the guard.
  ->  HONEST CAVEAT
      Yakuza's tonal whiplash works because the ANCHOR (Kiryu) and the CITY are consistent; keep our tonal swings anchored to a consistent dynast + a coherent district so the range enriches rather than fractures (don't let the absurd undercut the Amalgamation's dread — segregate registers by CONTEXT: substories are relief, the main thread stays taut).

### #14  LADY BOYLE'S LAST PARTY (Dishonored)
  ->  W1 (the sandbox space

  ->  W2/W3/W9 (randomized target + social deduction + personality-as-puzzle

  ->  W4 (multiple keys to the answer

  ->  W5 (the space fights back

  ->  W6 (non-lethal isn't clean

Non-lethal != moral.
  ->  W7 (the chaos system
      consider a Bohemia DISTRICT-CHAOS/darkness meter (ties Q019 march tally) where cumulative violence/disorder shifts the world-state + ending (grimmer district, warier factions) — HOW you play echoes citywide (validate against our fold; scope carefully).
  ->  W8 (crude shortcut allowed + judged
      let the sim PERMIT the brute path (slaughter your way to the answer) but COST it via the chaos/darkness state — freedom includes the ugly option, with consequence.
  ->  W10 (the elegant path is richer
      make our subtle solutions MORE rewarding to play (more content, more story, better long-term outcome) than the brute one — reward subtlety with richness, not just a cleaner score (our pacifist-bonus philosophy, validated). --- # V2 PAYLOAD — BACKFILLED 7/16/26 (FORMAT LAW v2). ### #15  ESCAPE FROM FORT JOY + THE SURFACE SYSTEM (Divinity: Original Sin 2)
  ->  With Questbook 08 (KCD), this is our second big hit on the flagged P7 systemic-solution gap — but DOS2 adds the REACTIVE-ENVIRONMENT-AS-TOOLSET layer our combat/city-buil
  ->  W1 (one goal, many full paths
      a Bohemia "escape/reach" objective (get into the Network facility, get a person out of a locked district, reach the Amalgamation door) with MULTIPLE full questlines + lateral tricks, each its own mini-story to the same exit — the player picks the path they are (our Q050 already gates approaches by assembled nodes; extend to Act-scale spatial multi-path).
  ->  W2 (environment IS the toolset
      OUR combat + city-builder + logistics are a reactive substrate — bank the DOS2 lesson HARD: let players solve with the SIM (cut power to a zone, flood/drain water via the plant, collapse a structure, reroute a caravan) — emergent solutions from our systems, "not intended." This is the biggest untapped strength we have (a physics/economy/infrastructure sandbox).
  ->  W3 (earned items as universal keys
      give the dynasty a few EARNED tools with broad creative reuse across combat + traversal + quests (a master key, a signal jammer, a founder's credential — Q009/Q023) — a reward that keeps giving.
  ->  W4 (quests interlock
      weave Bohemia quests so one's item/outcome enables another's path (our fold does the big version; add TACTICAL interlocks in the same act — validated by KCD too).
  ->  W5 (the betrayal that arms you
      a Bohemia beat where an ally betrays the dynasty but the dynasty KEEPS the tool/knowledge gained — betrayal as a systemic gift (ties Q027 double-agent).
  ->  W6 (get-caught-on-purpose
      let a "failure state" be a ROUTE — get captured to reach the cells, get "recruited" by the Network to reach the servers (our Q034/Q043 infiltration) — lateral thinking rewarded.
  ->  W8 (even the exit has multiple keys
      nest multiple solutions all the way down — every gate opens by kill/barter/sneak/skill (audit our chokepoints for single-key bottlenecks).
  ->  W9 (combat optional
      validates our Pacifist Path Law — systems let you AVOID fights; combat is one tool.
  ->  W10 (morality distributed across paths
      make each ROUTE a different moral flavor (mercy/justice/ tender/brute), so HOW the dynasty solves a quest characterizes it — the approach is the character (ties Lady Boyle W-chaos, Questbook 14, + our Megaton law).

### #17  THE FOUR-PILLAR MISSION + SOCIAL BOSS BATTLES (Deus Ex: Human Revolution / Mankind Divided)
  ->  W1 (every space, four keys
      audit Bohemia's key scenarios for OUR four-ish pillars — COMBAT (Dead-Eye), STEALTH, our "HACK" equivalent (infrastructure/logistics manipulation — cut power, reroute, sabotage), and SOCIAL ([READ]/barter/standing). Every major space solvable multiple ways (ties DOS2/KCD systemic, Questbooks 15/08). Our "hacking" pillar = manipulating the CITY systems.
  ->  W2/W3 (the social boss battle + read-the-person
      BUILD a Bohemia SOCIAL-BATTLE system — a high-stakes conversation won by reading an NPC's psychology and picking tactics turn-by-turn (confront/empathize/ refocus), partly randomized so you READ them. PERFECT for our summit (Q039), the Amalgamation door (Q050 beaten by knowing), faction negotiations, the succession vote — a winnable debate as a set-piece.
  ->  W4 (the odds-tilter
      an optional Bohemia tool that reveals an NPC's profile / tilts a social check (a companion who knows them, a dossier from the ledger, a favor spent) — transparent soft-modifier.
  ->  W5 (the unaided peak
      stage our HARDEST social battle with NO aids — the dynasty's own read vs a desperate person (a hostage-taker, a grieving zealot, a cornered defector) — remove the assist to spike tension (ties Q049 verdicts, Q017 grief).
  ->  W6 (public-reputation stakes
      a Bohemia debate PERFORMED publicly (a district assembly, a faction tribunal) where winning shifts STANDING/reputation, not just info — social consequence (ties Q037 propaganda, our standing system).
  ->  W7 (debate-as-climax
      our endgame ALREADY is this (Q050 beaten by knowing; the Amalgamation argued down) — Deus Ex + Planescape both validate the PHILOSOPHICAL-DEBATE finale. Bank the social-battle MECHANIC for it (tactics vs the Amalgamation's psychology).
  ->  W8 (failure reroutes
      losing a Bohemia social battle should ROUTE to another path (blew the negotiation -> now sneak/sabotage/fight in) — failure is a branch (our no-brick-wall law + Disco, Questbook 05).
  ->  W9 (diegetic info
      teach solutions through the SPACE (a code on a terminal, a rota on a wall) — the environment as its own hint (ties our [READ]).
  ->  W10 + FLAWS (build expresses you, but don't betray it
      keep Bohemia routes build-expressive, but NEVER force one pillar at a climax (the HR boss-fight sin) — our Pacifist Path Law already forbids this; Deus Ex is the cautionary tale. AND balance pillars so none trivializes the rest (the cloak flaw) — keep every route tense (regression-gate our difficulty).

### #18  KNOWLEDGE-AS-PROGRESSION (Outer Wilds)
  ->  Our succession fold + unrecorded ledger already gesture at knowledge-carry; Outer Wilds is the master text
      (Note: we are NOT a pure knowledge-game — we have build/economy/combat progression too. Steal the PRINCIPLES for our mystery/Amalgamation layer, don't convert the whole game.)
  ->  W1/W7 (knowledge is the upgrade + the loop as a learning unit
      make our GENERATIONAL FOLD a knowledge-carry engine — an heir "levels up" the DYNASTY's understanding of the Amalgamation/district across deaths; what the first dynast LEARNED (not just built) unlocks approaches for the next. A death is a reset that banks knowledge, not just resources (ties Anju loop-mastery, Questbook 11; our succession).
  ->  W2 (available from minute one, gated by understanding
      let key Amalgamation truths/approaches be physically present EARLY but only usable once the dynasty UNDERSTANDS them (you could always reach the door — you just didn't know what to say / what it is). Non-linear discovery gated by comprehension.
  ->  W3 (the rumor web
      make our UNRECORDED LEDGER a living RUMOR WEB — a player-built map of what the dynasty knows vs what's implied, threading discoveries about the Amalgamation/Network/founders, NO waypoints, followed by curiosity. (A gorgeous fit: the ledger already records the "off-book" truth.)
  ->  W4 ("there is always a way"
      honor the trust contract — every locked Amalgamation truth HAS a knowledge-key somewhere in the district/generations; never a dead mystery (distinct from the DELIBERATE withheld-closure of the mind-edit thread, Questbook 09 — that's a different, narrow tool).
  ->  W5 (knowledge-gates disguised as skill-gates
      gate our hardest challenges behind UNDERSTANDING, not just combat/resources — the Amalgamation is "beaten by knowing" (Q050 already!) — Outer Wilds validates making comprehension the master key.
  ->  W6/W8 (clockwork world + generous soft-clock
      use our scheduler for a self-directed living-clock layer (be at the right place at the right time to witness/learn something) with GENEROUS timing — urgency without tyranny.
  ->  W9 (the emotional payoff of comprehension
      our endgame should land because the dynasty finally UNDERSTANDS the Amalgamation (a grave that can't let go) — comprehension resolving into the Liberate/ Respect/Become choice; knowledge -> acceptance (validated by Planescape too, Questbook 12).
  ->  W10 (once-only discovery
      protect a few TRUE once-only revelations in our arc (a founder's secret, the Amalgamation's origin) — genuine discovery the fold can't cheapen (guard them as sacred beats).

### #19  THE DEDUCTION ENGINE (Return of the Obra Dinn)
  ->  Our [READ] investigations + the Amalgamation (built from data-PORTRAITS of the dead) + the unrecorded ledger make Obra Dinn's forensics unusually on-theme for us
  ->  W1/W2 (deduction is gameplay + inverted mystery
      build a Bohemia DEDUCTION quest where the dynasty identifies the dead — PERFECT for the Amalgamation, literally an archive of uploaded DATA-PORTRAITS: a quest to match faces->names->fates of the uploaded (who were they? how did they die? who was lost?) — restoring stolen identities as gameplay (ties Q022 face-thief, Q018 servers). Start from ignorance (a face with no name) and reason to the person.
  ->  W3/W6 (holistic read + logic-mesh
      make our investigations reward reading the WHOLE scene/ledger and cross-referencing across quests — a clue to one person found in another's record; the unrecorded ledger as a logic-mesh where accrued knowledge cascades.
  ->  W4 (the witness-the-instant verb
      a Bohemia "Memento Mortem" equivalent — the Amalgamation's stored memories let the dynasty WITNESS a frozen recorded moment (a death, an upload, a founder's choice) and walk it for clues (ties Q012 mind-edits, Q024 dream-temple). One evocative verb, narrative + mechanical.
  ->  W5 (death-chaining
      unlock our mystery in deducible ORDER by chaining — witnessing one recorded moment reveals the next reachable one (a structure for the Amalgamation dive, Q050 approach).
  ->  W7 (the RULE OF THREE — the big steal
      adopt a VALIDATION mechanic for our deduction/social content — lock in conclusions in sets (or on cross-confirmation) so the player can't blind-guess, but a well-reasoned inference rides on certainties. Makes hard Bohemia mysteries FAIR + solvable without waypoints (pairs with our [READ] and the Deus-Ex social battle, Q17, and the no-brick-wall law).
  ->  W8/W9 (no hard fail + easing ramp
      let our hardest deduction/mystery content be PRESSURE-FREE (solve at leisure) and EASE near the end — respect the player's pace (validated across Outer Wilds/Anju).
  ->  W10 (fully fair by design — the CONTRACT
      if we build deduction, EVERY answer must be fairly clueable — no ambiguous "gotcha" (regression-gate our mysteries for solvability; Obra Dinn's few under-clued fates are the cautionary tale). Fairness is the whole contract.

### #20  THE GOLDEN RULE / TIME-LOOP MORALITY (The Forgotten City)
  ->  This quest is a Rosetta Stone for us — it fuses four of our already-flagged models into one and pins a COLLECTIVE-MORALITY engine that rhymes with the Amalgamation's "no

Collective punishment as a moral-horror engine (ties Q018 cult, Q037 propaganda, our currencies-as-leverage). This is deeply on-theme: the Amalgamation IS a "no one may be lost" rule taken to horror.
  ->  W3/W8 (loop carries knowledge + collapses with mastery
      our succession FOLD already carries knowledge forward; validate the Forgotten-City sharpening — an heir who KNOWS the path resolves a multi-loop/ multi-generation crisis FASTER (knowledge collapses the grind; ties Outer Wilds Q18, Anju Q11).
  ->  W4 (sinning as a tool
      a Bohemia systemic verb where the dynasty can BREAK a rule for gain at a (resettable or heavy) cost — steal the cure now, doom the zone, carry it forward — morally-loaded system use (careful, thematic; ties Dishonored non-lethal-isn't-clean Q14, our Megaton law).
  ->  W5 (the red-herring premise
      frame a Bohemia quest whose STATED goal is a misdirection serving a hidden party (chase a "culprit" while the real rot is the system) — the quest interrogates its own framing (ties Q037 whose-truth, Q048 false-dawn, the MacGuffin twist Q16).

### #21  "YOU CAN'T SAVE EVERYONE" (Pathologic 2)
  ->  Bohemia is a HARDCORE post-collapse survival RPG with death-math + scarcity currencies (medicine, electricity, resources) — Pathologic 2 is the master text on making SCAR
      (We are NOT trying to be as punishing; steal the PRINCIPLES + the tuning honesty.)
  ->  W1/W2 (time/scarcity as a resource to LOSE + "can't save everyone"
      our survival-accounting + death- math already lean here; bank the Pathologic thesis for our HARDEST content — a crisis (a plague, a siege, a winter, an Amalgamation purge) where the dynasty CANNOT save everyone and must TRIAGE, and the unsaved die permanently into the fold/ledger. Loss as designed experience, not a fail (ties our death-math, Q019 march tally, the Liberate "let go" thesis).
  ->  W3 (slow-onset cruelty
      stage a Bohemia crisis so the pressure CREEPS (calm early, dire by mid) — the player learns the stakes by living them (ties our generational pacing; a dynasty's decline felt, not announced).
  ->  W4 (the body/city as a second clock
      our survival meters + life-support buildings ARE this — mere survival costs resources + time, forcing moral compromise under scarcity (validate; scarcity should manufacture hard bargains, not just attrition).
  ->  W5 (triage as the core loop
      a Bohemia TRIAGE quest — allocate scarce medicine/power/food across districts/people/factions with never enough; every save is a loss elsewhere; the allocation IS the ethics (ties Q036 plant power, That-Lucky-Old-Sun, our currencies). PERFECT fit for a city-builder.
  ->  W6 (odds not guarantees
      our treatment/rescue outcomes should be PROBABILITIES the dynasty influences, not guarantees — live with results you shaped but didn't control (ties ME2 math Q06, our combat dial odds).
  ->  W7 (the diegetic questlog
      consider making a Bohemia "log" diegetic — the unrecorded ledger / a dynast's mindmap AS the quest tracker (story informs the interface; cf. Obra Dinn Q19, Outer Wilds rumor-web Q18, Disco Q05). Our ledger is already half this.
  ->  W8 (no-clean finale, genuinely debated
      our Liberate/Respect/Become already are this — two-plus reasonable end-choices players flip on, where "winning" is questionable — validated by the master of bleak moral finales.
  ->  W10 (suffering as design + THE TUNING FIX
      THE crucial honest port — if we lean into scarcity-grief, ship DIFFICULTY SLIDERS (our Difficulty Packages already exist for combat!) so hardcore players get the full cruelty and others get the story without bouncing off. Pathologic's post-launch sliders are the cautionary+corrective tale: make the punishment OPTIONAL-INTENSITY (extend our package system to survival/scarcity, not just the Dead-Eye dial).

### #22  SIDE QUESTS AS PHILOSOPHICAL DESPAIR (NieR: Automata)
  ->  NieR is the DARK counterpart to Yakuza (Q13
      where Yakuza side quests RELIEVE, NieR side quests DEEPEN. We want BOTH registers — and NieR's "imitation of a lost humanity" engine is uncannily close to our Amalgamation (data-portraits imitating the dead) and our post-collapse survivors imitating a dead economy/society.
  ->  W1/W2 (side quests deliver the theme + the imitation engine
      bank a set of Bohemia side quests that DEEPEN our central question (what survives when a life ends / what do we owe the dead) — micro-parables of survivors or Amalgamation-fragments IMITATING the lost world (a family reenacting pre-collapse routines; a machine/upload mimicking a dead person; a cult imitating old-world faith) and finding tragedy or fragile meaning. One thematic engine -> endless small stories (ties Q018 cult, Q012 mind- edits, Q033 the imitation of normalcy).
  ->  W3/W4 (a side quest that detonates the main secret + dramatic irony
      plant a Bohemia SIDE quest that quietly reveals a core truth (a companion's hidden nature, the Amalgamation's real origin) and weaponizes player knowledge against the characters ("some things are better left unknown").
  ->  W5 (humanize the functional
      give our "interface"/functional NPCs (a caravan radio voice, a ledger- keeper, a plant operator) inner lives + small quests — nothing is just a system; everyone is someone (validates the unrecorded ledger's whole premise).
  ->  W6 (recontext across playthroughs/generations
      let our GENERATIONAL replays REFRAME earlier events — a later dynast re-experiences an ancestor's quest from the OTHER side (the enemy's view, the victim's view) — perspective as progression (ties our fold + succession; the Strange-Man-across-generations Q10).
  ->  W7 (nihilism -> chosen meaning
      our arc can EARN despair (the collapse, the futility, the dead you couldn't save — Pathologic Q21) then transcend into CHOSEN meaning (Liberate: we let the dead go and choose to live) — hope after honesty, never cheap uplift (validated by NieR + Planescape).
  ->  W9 (sympathy for the enemy
      keep humanizing the Network/Amalgamation until opposing them costs the player emotionally (our Amalgamation is already a sympathetic grave; NieR is the master of "the enemy is us"). The machines-are-people lesson = our uploads-are-people core.
  ->  W10 (theme as question not lecture
      ask "what do we owe the dead" through SITUATIONS, never preach — the player arrives at the answer (our life-lesson-under-every-decision rule, validated).
  ->  AVOID (the flaws
      keep the MAIN spine driving (don't let side quests carry ALL the theme while the A-plot idles); keep thematic side quests DENSE (few strong > many fetch — Yakuza+NieR agree); and if our generational "replays" reframe meaning, make each generation stand on its own.

### #23  THE NO-MARKER QUESTLINE (Elden Ring / FromSoftware)
  ->  Our MAP LAW (Claude never designs layouts) means SPATIAL cryptic-ness is Paolo's call — but the STORYTELLING techniques + the hard-won cautions are ours to bank
      Our single-DISTRICT scale is actually the ANTIDOTE to Elden Ring's core flaw (cryptic works better in enfolded spaces).
  ->  W1/W2 (world-as-quest-log + the stumble-thrill
      our single district is SMALL enough that marker-less discovery can work WITHOUT the scale problem — bank OPTIONAL diegetic questlines found by listening/ observing (a rumor, an overheard grief, a changed shopfront), not a marker. Discovery as a quiet thrill (ties Outer Wilds rumor-web Q18, our [READ]). [PENDING, Paolo's call on how marker-light to go.]
  ->  W3 (item/object descriptions as lore
      bury Bohemia lore in OBJECT flavor (a salvaged photo, a pre-collapse receipt, a data-portrait's caption) the curious assemble — the Amalgamation is LITERALLY built of data-fragments; item-text-as-lore is on-theme (ties Q022 face-thief, the unrecorded ledger).
  ->  W4 (environmental storytelling
      our tile/prop pipeline can narrate wordlessly (a barricaded home, a shrine of old currency, a child's toy in the ruins) — the district testifies (validates our art philosophy; the SPACE tells the collapse's story). [Layouts = Paolo; Claude does props/plumbing.]
  ->  W5 (interlocking NPCs
      weave early "side" Bohemia NPCs into later major threads (the shopkeeper you bartered with in gen 1 is central to a gen-2 crisis) — one tapestry (ties our fold + DOS2/KCD).
  ->  W6 (NPCs progress independently
      our scheduler can let NPCs live/move/leave/die on world-time whether witnessed or not — presence has stakes (ties Pathologic Q21 missable events, NV pre-seeding).
  ->  W7 (a side quest that is an ending
      our Liberate/Respect/Become already tie deep questlines to ENDINGS — validated; keep making the biggest optional threads pay off in worldview + finale.
  ->  W9 (main gates side + vice versa
      interlock our main Reconstruction spine with side quests structurally (a main milestone unlocks a side location; a side bond gates a main option) — not just narrative links (ties ME2 Q06, our Q050 assembled-nodes gating).
  ->  CAUTIONS (bank ALL of them
      our single-district scale mitigates the missable-at-scale flaw, but STILL (a) make EVERY quest fairly clueable in-world (Obra Dinn/Elden-Ring fairness contract); (b) TELEGRAPH ordering dependencies or make failure legible/recoverable (our no-brick-wall law); (c) never ship a "band-aid" marker as a substitute for diegetic signposting — build the clues IN. Our SUN-MODE/legibility instincts already lean this way; extend to quest clarity.

### #24  THE REACTIVITY ENGINE (Alpha Protocol)
  ->  Our unrecorded ledger + standing + fold are a reactivity engine; Alpha Protocol is the master cult text on making it a WEB with per-person, multidimensional, mechanics-re
  ->  W1/W8 (web not binary + delayed seeds
      our ledger/fold already track a web; bank Alpha Protocol's depth target — per-FACTION and per-PERSON consequence, much of it paying off a generation later (our Q040->042). Not good/evil; a web of remembered choices.
  ->  W2 (intent over script, timed
      consider a Bohemia timed INTENT choice for high-pressure beats (a standoff, a negotiation, a betrayal) — pick a STANCE under a clock, commit to a persona (pairs with the Deus Ex social-battle mechanic Q17; use sparingly for tension).
  ->  W3/W4 (no universal-correct + like vs respect
      make Bohemia standing MULTIDIMENSIONAL — a faction/ NPC can FEAR, RESPECT, TRUST, or RESENT the dynasty, each with different aid, and the persona that wins the Reds may lose the Church. Antagonism can be a VALID rewarded path (defy the Cartel -> they respect strength -> a harder-edged alliance). (Ties our faction web + Megaton law; big upgrade to standing.)
  ->  W5/W6 (reputation buys mechanics + boss-altering
      THE standout port — let Bohemia relationships/intel re-tune COMBAT + city-systems: an ally poisons/sabotages an enemy before a fight; a faction favor cuts the power to a Network stronghold mid-mission; a bond opens a non-lethal capture. Reactivity reaching into the Dead-Eye layer + the city-builder (ties DOS2 environment-as-toolset Q15, our combat).
  ->  W7 (intel as social power / dossiers
      our [READ] + the ledger ARE dossiers — collecting intel on an NPC/faction should UNLOCK dialogue/leverage (a bluff you can't make without the file) — knowing is power (ties Obra Dinn deduction Q19, the Amalgamation's data).
  ->  W9 (prep shapes options
      our city-builder economy IS the prep layer — what you built/stockpiled/allied before a crisis shapes your options in it (ties ME2 wind-up Q06, our Reconstruction).
  ->  W10 + FLAWS (surface the consequence + BOTH layers must work
      CRUCIAL cautions — (a) our combat + city-builder must be FUN on their own (Alpha Protocol's reactivity couldn't rescue weak gameplay; our Dead-Eye dial + build loop must stand alone); (b) SURFACE reactivity so it's felt on ONE playthrough (NPCs reference the dynasty's deeds; the fold/roll-call tallies them — cf. ME2 Q06) — deep-but-invisible reactivity is wasted. Make the world SAY what it remembers.

### #25  FAVOR & WRATH / PLAYING AFTER EVIL WON (Tyranny)
  ->  Our standing system + faction web + the Network's manipulations map onto Tyranny unusually well — and the favor/wrath idea is a direct upgrade path for our reputation des
  ->  W1/W2/W3 (DUAL-AXIS reputation — favor AND wrath, fear as power, principle-filtered
      THE big port — upgrade Bohemia STANDING from a slider to TWO independent axes per faction/companion (e.g. RESPECT and RESENTMENT, or TRUST and FEAR), where BOTH unlock different abilities/options, you can max both, and each faction judges acts by THEIR values (the Reds vs the Church vs the Cartel weigh the same deed oppositely). Being FEARED is a real, rewarded path — not just the "evil" slider (ties Alpha Protocol Q24 like/respect, our Megaton + pacifist laws; a major standing-system upgrade).
  ->  W4/W5 (authority as fantasy + banality of evil
      a Bohemia arc where the dynasty holds real AUTHORITY over the district and most choices are the MUNDANE administration of scarce power (who eats, who's exiled, which law to enforce) — grey, everyday governance, not cartoon villainy (ties our city-builder + Q049 verdicts + the mayor-consequence system). The weight is in the ordinary rulings.
  ->  W6 (choice before the game / Conquest
      our GENERATIONAL structure IS a "Conquest" engine — the prior dynasty's choices shape the heir's STARTING world; NPCs reference deeds from before this dynast was born (validated; our fold already does this — lean into NPCs citing pre-birth history).
  ->  W7 (allegiance redraws the map
      let Bohemia faction allegiance have GEOPOLITICAL world-state effects (side with the Trades -> they're granted a district; favor the Homeless -> they hold the servers' ground) — reputation redraws power, not just dialogue (Paolo owns the actual map; Claude does the standing->territory plumbing).
  ->  W8 (forced-but-open alliance + stand-above

  ->  W9 (serve from love or fear -> epilogue
      our companion/faction EPILOGUE slides (the fold's roll-call, Q06/Q050) should reflect HOW their loyalty was earned (love vs fear) — the manner of service defines the fate. Bank fear-earned vs trust-earned as distinct epilogue inputs.
  ->  W10 (the false-neutral puppeteer
      our NETWORK is exactly this — a faction posing as neutral infrastructure/knowledge-keepers while playing the district's factions against each other (validated; the School-of-Ink parallel sharpens the Network's "we just keep the lights on" mask over manipulation).
  ->  FLAWS (bank
      DELIVER the bold premise (if the dynasty can be a feared tyrant, give beats that FEEL it, not just admin); BUDGET reactivity so the ENDGAME pays off (don't let our final generation collapse the web Act-III-style); and BOTH layers (combat + city-builder) must stand alone (Alpha Protocol + Tyranny agree — reactivity can't rescue weak core loops).

### #26  THE UNSOLVABLE ACCUSATION (Pentiment)
  ->  Pentiment is the master text on JUDGMENT UNDER UNCERTAINTY + LIVING WITH IT ACROSS TIME — uncannily aligned with our unrecorded ledger, our verdict quests (Q049), and our
  ->  W1/W2/W6 (unsolvable mystery + about-investigation + live-with-being-wrong
      bank a Bohemia investigation/verdict quest with NO confirmed answer — the dynasty accuses/judges on incomplete evidence and NEVER learns if they were right; the accused + kin carry it across GENERATIONS (our fold is built for this). Frame it clearly as being ABOUT judgment, not solution (ties Q049 the jailer, Q037 whose-truth; the unrecorded ledger records what you DECIDED, maybe wrongly).
  ->  W3 (time-triage on knowledge
      a Bohemia investigation on a TIME BUDGET where you can't chase every lead — where you spend hours shapes what you know, so your verdict is partly a function of attention (ties Pathologic triage Q21; pair with our no-brick-wall + sliders honesty).
  ->  W4 (each suspect a questline w/ motive + means
      build parallel suspect-threads, each its own mini-quest with motive + findable evidence — the player picks whom to dig into (ties Beyond the Beef Q02, Obra Dinn Q19, our [READ]).
  ->  W5 (accuse-who-you-believe OR who-deserves-it
      THE sharp port — split TRUTH from JUSTICE in our verdict quests: convict the likely-guilty, OR impart moral judgment on who DESERVES it regardless — two consciences (ties Q049 verdicts, Q019 tally, Dishonored non-lethal-isn't-clean Q14).
  ->  W7 (motive as the hunt / pass-fail inside chaos

  ->  W8 (build defines what you can know

  ->  W9 (history as the real subject / who authors truth
      PERFECT for us — the recorded-vs-unrecorded ledger IS "how official truth gets authored by the powerful"; bank quests where the dynasty's accusation BECOMES the recorded history (right or wrong), and the unrecorded truth diverges (ties Q037, the Amalgamation's authored record).
  ->  W10 (the decades-long aftermath
      our GENERATIONAL fold IS this — return across generations to see judgments ripen (the accused's orphaned kin, the buried guilt) — validated as a master structure.
  ->  FLAWS (bank
      frame the no-answer as the POINT (not withholding); and TUNE the time pressure / give legibility so "judgment under uncertainty" doesn't read as "arbitrary" (Pentiment + Pathologic + Dream On agree — the unsolvable only works when it's clearly the SUBJECT).

### #27  THE ILLUSION OF CHOICE / PLAYER COMPLICITY (Spec Ops: The Line)
  ->  Spec Ops is a scalpel
      powerful, easy to misuse. Our PACIFIST PATH LAW (non-lethal always possible) already REJECTS the pure "no choice but atrocity" railroad — so we steal the TECHNIQUES for complicity + self-deception, NOT the forced-atrocity, and always within our wellbeing/tone rules.
  ->  W2 (strip choice / force the hand — ADAPTED, not copied
      our Pacifist Law forbids a mandatory atrocity. BUT we can bank the softer, honest version: moments where the dynasty realizes a choice they ALREADY made (via the fold/precedent) caused harm they didn't foresee — complicity via consequence, not a forced trigger (ties Whispering Hillock Q04, the unrecorded ledger). The player OWNS a past act, rather than being railroaded into a new one.
  ->  W3 (weaponize the abstraction
      our city-builder/combat uses ABSTRACTIONS (population numbers, resource units, "casualties" as a stat). Bank a beat that reveals the human cost BEHIND a number the player optimized (the "12 lost" in the death-math were named people) — the ledger makes the abstraction personal (ties Q019 tally, Pathologic Q21, the unrecorded ledger's "everyone is someone").
  ->  W4 (the accusatory UI — used GENTLY
      our diegetic ledger/UI could occasionally REFLECT the dynasty's deeds back (not mock the player — that violates our care rules — but SURFACE the truth: "the record will remember this differently than you do"). The recorded-vs-unrecorded tension AS a quiet mirror (ties Q037, the Strange-Man mirror Q10 — reflection, not accusation).
  ->  W5 (sympathy-then-consequence
      our monster-is-a-victim + humanize-the-enemy work (Q01/Q10/Q22) mean the player's choices land on people they've come to care about — guilt built on empathy (validated; keep humanizing before any hard outcome).
  ->  W6 (the self-deceiving narrator
      a Bohemia figure (a founder, a prior dynast, a Network apologist) who REWRITES the record to deny an atrocity — "if the truth is undeniable, you create your own" — the psychology of the AUTHORED record (ties Pentiment Q26, our recorded ledger, the Amalgamation's curated memory).
  ->  W8 (visible degradation
      our character-art pipeline CAN show a dynast's moral cost physically (wear, scars, hardness) over a life of hard choices — external state mirrors internal (ties our rig + the Disco/Tyranny "who you became" reward).
  ->  W9 (form = indictment / theme-through-mechanic
      keep enforcing theme via MECHANIC not sermon (our Liberate "let go" is felt; Dead Money's greed-weight). Spec Ops is the extreme; we take the principle, not the cruelty.
  ->  FLAWS/CARE (bank hard
      NEVER force gratuitous trauma or a hectoring gotcha (violates wellbeing + tone + the "no preaching" rule — every lesson stays UNDER the decision, never on top of it); make complicity EARNED + meaningful, never manipulative; and remember our combat/build loops must be good on their own (Spec Ops/Alpha Protocol/Tyranny all agree). The player should feel the weight of THEIR choices, never be blamed for OUR railroad.

### #28  MERCY AS A MECHANIC (Undertale)
  ->  Undertale is the master validation of our PACIFIST PATH LAW — and the model for making non-violence a real MECHANIC with teeth, plus a world that REMEMBERS
      (Our Dead-Eye dial is lethal-leaning; this is how to build the mercy side as a true equal.)
  ->  W1/W10 (mercy as a full mechanic with skill

  ->  W2/W3 (every enemy a person with a solution
      give Bohemia foes names/personalities + a readable non-violent solution (a scared conscript wants reassurance; a zealot wants to be heard) — reading WHO they are is the mercy path (ties our [READ], the unrecorded ledger, humanize-the-enemy Q22/Q01).
  ->  W4 (the persistent unforgetting save
      OUR FOLD/LEDGER IS THIS — an atrocity should STICK across generations and resist laundering (you can't reset away a massacre; the unrecorded ledger remembers what the official record buried). Bank an irreversible moral stain that persists beyond any in-world "reset" (validates our never-lose + generational-memory core; the anti-save-scum).
  ->  W5 (the world decays with cruelty
      let the DISTRICT physically reflect the dynasty's body count/ cruelty (emptier streets, warier factions, grimmer tone, a "darkness" state) — HOW you play reshapes the world-state (ties Q019 tally, Dishonored chaos Q14, Spec Ops Q27; scope per our fold).
  ->  W6 (mercy is earned, not passive
      make Bohemia's non-lethal path require REFUSING tempting violent outs (an enemy begs for death; violence is faster/cheaper) — pacifism as active discipline, rewarded (our pacifist-bonus; Dishonored's dark-spare Q14 as the grey inverse).
  ->  W7 (the route is the theme
      validated — our Liberate/Respect/Become + a mercy-vs-ruthlessness dynasty arc ARE routes-as-theme; how the dynasty treats the district IS the story.
  ->  W8 (interrogate the WHY, gently
      our unrecorded ledger can quietly reflect the dynasty's MOTIVE (why did you do it?) — within our care/tone rules (surface, don't hector — cf. Spec Ops care-note Q27, the Strange-Man mirror Q10).
  ->  W9 (the bright counterweight — the CORE lesson
      ALWAYS offer a fully-realized non-lethal route alongside the lethal one, so the meaning is the PLAYER'S (our Pacifist Path Law, validated by the master example; the ethical opposite of Spec Ops' forced atrocity Q27).
  ->  FLAWS (bank
      make the mercy path's requirements LEGIBLE (don't fail players by accident); don't make the cruel path pure tedium-as-punishment; and SYSTEMATIZE the non-violent solution space (categories of de-escalation) so it scales beyond hand-authored one-offs (our FACTORY LAW applies).

### #29  THE BOOK OF LAWS / SOCIETY-SURVIVAL (Frostpunk)
  ->  This is the most DIRECTLY applicable deep-dive to our city-builder + survival + governance layer
      We are literally a post-collapse society-survival RPG city-builder; Frostpunk is the master text for the GOVERNANCE-AS-MORAL-ENGINE side.
  ->  W1/W2 (governance is the quest + a Book of Laws
      bank a Bohemia "BOOK OF LAWS/DECREES" — a paced, branching, mutually-exclusive policy engine where the dynasty passes ONE major decree at a meaningful cadence (per season/generation), each felt + committed, shaping what the district BECOMES (rationing rules, curfews, conscription, how the dead are handled, who gets medicine). Ties our currencies (medicine/electricity/resources), Q049 verdicts, the mayor-consequence + succession systems. (Our MAP LAW untouched — this is policy/plumbing, not layout.)
  ->  W3 (the slippery slope
      design our decrees so each reasonable one GREASES the next — a survival measure unlocks a harsher option unlocks a harsher one, until the dynasty drifts into tyranny WITHOUT a single monstrous choice. The Amalgamation's "no one may be lost" is the ultimate slope; bank gradualism as a horror engine (ties Q018, the banality-of-evil Tyranny Q25, Forgotten-City collective-rule Q20).
  ->  W4 (the emblematic compromise
      give Bohemia vivid, concrete moral sliders (not abstract policy) — a child-labor-equivalent, a "who eats when there's not enough," a "treat the sick or save the medicine" — one felt image per dilemma (ties Pathologic triage Q21, our death-math).
  ->  W5/W10 (dual society meters + legitimacy fail-state
      upgrade our standing model toward TWO+ axes at the DISTRICT level — e.g. HOPE (will to rebuild) vs DISCONTENT (unrest) — where the dynasty can keep people ALIVE yet be OVERTHROWN/deposed for HOW they ruled (a political fail-state distinct from starving/freezing). Ties Tyranny favor/wrath Q25, Alpha Protocol Q24, our succession/mayor systems.
  ->  W6 (survive -> who did you become
      OUR endgame IS this — the district survives, but Liberate/Respect/ Become judge HOW + who the dynasty became. Bank Frostpunk's "the crisis passes, live with your methods" as an explicit reckoning beat (validated; the city-builder version of our thesis).
  ->  W7 (theme through systems
      keep making Bohemia's ethics something the player DOES under pressure (allocate, decree, triage), never a sermon (our no-preaching rule + Pathologic/Spec Ops; validated).
  ->  W8 (ideological forks
      our FACTIONS give this natural — mutually-exclusive ways to manufacture order/ hope (Church faith vs Reds order vs Trades commerce), each a different regime the dynasty can lean into (ties our faction web + Tyranny Q25).
  ->  W9 (the quiet judgment / dark laws optional
      keep the harsh options AVAILABLE but never mandatory, and let the unrecorded ledger TALLY the drift without preaching — survivable kindly, tempting cruelly (our Pacifist Path Law at the GOVERNANCE scale).
  ->  FLAWS (bank
      keep scarcity tight so dilemmas STAY hard (don't let death-math become a solved spreadsheet); tie hope/discontent to NAMED human faces (not abstract bars — the ledger); and use our GENERATIONAL structure to give the deep branching Frostpunk's linear scenarios lack (each dynasty a different society-run).

### #30  THE CIVILIAN PERSPECTIVE / GUILT AS A SYSTEM (This War of Mine)
  ->  TWoM is uncannily close to Bohemia's SURVIVOR heart (post-collapse civilians, scarcity, no-clean-choices) and pairs with Frostpunk (Q29
      TWoM = the GROUND-LEVEL human/guilt view; Frostpunk = the GOVERNANCE view. Together they map our dual scale (individual survival + district governance).
  ->  W1 (the perspective inversion
      OUR core IS this — post-collapse survivors, not conquerors. Validated; keep the emotional weight on the powerless rebuilding a life, not a power fantasy (our whole premise).
  ->  W2 (GUILT AS A MECHANIC — the big port
      bank a Bohemia CONSCIENCE/mental-health system — survivors/ companions/the dynast carry a psychological state that CRUEL choices erode (toward breakdown/hardening) and merciful ones sustain; conscience is a managed-but-STICKY resource (tie to our upbringing Q003, the unrecorded ledger, the succession trait system — a hard choice can permanently scar an heir).   ->  W3/W4 (grey morality + the emblematic dilemma
      give Bohemia vivid, concrete no-right-answer scenes (a Quiet-House equivalent — rob the defenseless who have medicine your sick child needs; the game never says it's ok) — one felt moral IMAGE per dilemma, not abstract policy (ties Q049 verdicts, our death- math, Frostpunk Q29).
  ->  W5 (build the system around emergent emotion
      a DESIGN METHOD for Paolo — watch playtesters for emergent feeling (a spontaneous mercy, a regretted theft) and BUILD Bohemia systems around what players do unprompted; let the players reveal what the game is about (a playtesting law).
  ->  W6 (subtractive/mirror, discomfort without forcing
      our unrecorded ledger can MIRROR the dynasty's choices back as quiet discomfort (not preaching) — you always CHOSE, so the weight is yours (the ethical Undertale/TWoM path, not the Spec Ops railroad; our Pacifist Law + care rules).
  ->  W8 (community as a survival resource
