  ->  W9 (attrition cascades
      our survival-accounting/death-math should let small neglect SNOWBALL (hunger->sickness->despair->dysfunction) so early kindness/harshness compounds across a life/generation (ties Frostpunk Q29, our currencies).
  ->  W10 (the pacifist run is possible
      validated AGAIN — a full non-lethal, non-cruel survival path must always exist, harder but real (our Pacifist Path Law; TWoM + Undertale Q28 both confirm).
  ->  FLAWS (bank
      make conscience STICK (permanent scars, not a toppable meter — or the ethics deflate); BALANCE misery with agency/texture/wins so it stays playable (our SUN-MODE/tone/difficulty-package instincts); and VARY the moral scenarios so dilemmas stay fresh. Handle child-vulnerability with WEIGHT, never exploitation (our care rules, strict).

### #31  THE IRON CAGE / COMPLICITY AS A JOB (Papers, Please)
  ->  Papers, Please completes our COMPLICITY trilogy (Spec Ops Q27 = forced atrocity; This War of Mine Q30 = survival theft; Papers, Please = bureaucratic complicity) — and it
  ->  W1/W2/W10 (complicity through mundane work + the iron cage + theme-through-interface
      bank a Bohemia ADMINISTRATION loop where the dynasty PROCESSES the district's daily governance (who gets rations, medicine, entry, work, judgment) via a felt bureaucratic UI — and enforcing the Network's/regime's rules makes the dynasty COMPLICIT one decision at a time (ties Q049 verdicts, our currencies, the mayor-consequence system; the banality-of-evil governance from Tyranny Q25 + Frostpunk Q29).
  ->  W3 (scarcity weaponizes compassion against YOUR OWN — the big port
      the cruelest, most on-theme vise — make Bohemia MERCY to strangers risk the dynasty's OWN family/heirs (spare the medicine for a dying stranger and your own child goes without). Survival vs conscience, personal (ties our death-math, succession, TWoM Quiet House Q30 — but the cost lands on YOUR bloodline). Handle within wellbeing rules.
  ->  W4 (the escalating rulebook
      let the Network/regime pile ESCALATING rules on the dynasty's administration (new restrictions, quotas, searches) until compliance is frantic — the system's growth as the pressure curve (ties Frostpunk's slippery slope Q29, the Amalgamation's tightening control).
  ->  W5 (cruelty incentivized / detain
      bank beats where the regime PAYS the dynasty to do the immoral thing (hand over a dissenter, deny the desperate) — virtue has a price; the systems tempt cruelty (our Megaton + Pacifist Law tension; Dishonored dark-spare Q14).
  ->  W6 (recurring human faces
      our NPCs/applicants should RETURN with linked stories (the person you denied comes back; their family follows) — enforcing rules separates people you've MET (ties our pre-seeding, Anju Q11, the unrecorded ledger's "everyone is someone").
  ->  W7 (subvert the cage
      our anti-Network resistance path — the dynasty can SABOTAGE the regime from inside its own administrative role (pass a forbidden person, withhold a report) at grave risk — cog OR saboteur (ties Q027 double-agent, Q043 quiet line, get-caught-on-purpose Q15).
  ->  W8/W9 (many small weighted choices -> divergent endings
      validate a MORAL-CADENCE model for Bohemia — depth from the ACCUMULATION of many small pressured governance choices (not only big branch-quests), summing to divergent dynasty fates (ties our death-math, Frostpunk one-law-a-day Q29, our finales).
  ->  FLAWS (bank
      make the administrative grind have RHYTHM + escalating variety + human intrusions so it grips rather than bores; give the bleakness TEXTURE + small warmth (our SUN-MODE/tone/difficulty instincts); and remember depth can come from MANY small weighted choices, a different tool than the big branching quest.

### #32  "YOU ARE THE VILLAIN" / THE IDENTITY TWIST (KOTOR)
  ->  Our themes (memory, identity, the Amalgamation built from the DEAD, succession, the recorded-vs- unrecorded self) make an identity twist unusually native — but it's a ONE
  ->  W1/W2 (rewrite-the-past mirror twist
      bank ONE major Bohemia identity revelation that retroactively recontextualizes the arc — candidates fitting our lore: a dynast discovers they're a Network plant / an Amalgamation-seeded copy / that a "founder-hero" they revered was the architect of the collapse / that an ancestor they hunted IS their own bloodline. The reveal reframes prior scenes WITHOUT retconning them (ties Q012 mind-edits, Q022 face-thief, Q050 the door, the recorded-vs-unrecorded self).
  ->  W3 (the twist is a CHOICE
      make our reveal a FORK, not a passive shock — post-reveal, the dynasty chooses to OWN or REJECT the revealed identity (redeem the bloodline's sin, or embrace it) — agency over identity (ties Planescape Q12, our Liberate/Respect/Become, succession).
  ->  W4 (fair-play seeding — MANDATORY
      seed the twist relentlessly from the start (odd competences, NPC reactions, memory inconsistencies in the unrecorded ledger) so it's inevitable-in-hindsight — the fairness contract is non-negotiable (cf. Obra Dinn Q19, Pentiment Q26; our regression-gate for solvability applies to twists too).
  ->  W5 (delivered at the lowest point, by the enemy
      stage our reveal when the dynasty is most broken, from the Amalgamation/Network, weaponized to shatter them (the Amalgamation KNOWS the dynasty's true history because it archives the dead — a chilling, on-theme delivery; ties Q050, Peralez Q09).
  ->  W6 (the twist tests bonds
      let our reveal detonate the dynasty's RELATIONSHIPS — companions/factions react per their history with the revealed truth (the ally who lost family to the founder-villain now travels with their heir) — reframe every bond (ties ME2 Q06, BG3 Q16, our faction web).
  ->  W7/W8 (both-directions stakes + identity as theme
      our reveal should reframe the PAST and raise FUTURE stakes, and BE our thesis (who survives when a life ends / who the dynasty chooses to be) — not a gimmick (validated by Planescape Q12; our whole succession/memory spine).
  ->  W9/W10 (one-shot + motivated amnesia
      SPEND the twist once, deliberately — the surrounding game must satisfy even when the twist is known (our reactivity/systems carry replay, Alpha-Protocol-style Q24). If we use memory-loss (natural for us — the fold, edited memories, the Amalgamation), JUSTIFY it in world-logic + make it thematically load-bearing (Planescape Q12), never a lazy blank slate.
  ->  CAUTION
      do NOT overuse identity twists — one great one > three cheap ones (the diminishing-returns lesson); and NEVER under-seed (a twist without clues is a betrayal).

### #33  "WOULD YOU KINDLY" / THE AGENCY TWIST (BioShock)
  ->  BioShock + KOTOR (Q32) are our two twist models
      KOTOR = identity ("you ARE the villain"); BioShock = AGENCY ("you were CONTROLLED"). The agency twist is ON-THEME for us (the Amalgamation edits minds; the Network manipulates) but is a ONE-SHOT + easy to misfire — use once, seed airtight, and pair with a mechanical shift.
  ->  W1/W6 (indict obedience + theme-twist fused
      our Amalgamation/Network mind-control lore makes an agency twist native — a dynast could discover a "helpful" guide (a Network handler, an Amalgamation voice posing as an ancestor/ally) has been STEERING them via a trigger/edit all along, and the reveal IS our thesis (free will vs the archive that authors you; recorded-vs-unrecorded self). Ties Q012 mind-edits, Q009 the voice, Q050 the door. Use ONCE, deliberately.
  ->  W2 (turn our OWN structure into theme
      if any Bohemia system CONSTRAINS the player (the 120 BPM grid, the fold's determinism, the Network's rules), a reveal could reframe that constraint AS the control (you thought the rails were the game; they were the leash) — weaponize our structure into meaning (careful, once; cf. Spec Ops Q27).
  ->  W3 (the trigger hidden in plain sight
      seed a Bohemia trigger/tell from the very start, disguised as ordinary (a recurring phrase from a handler, a symbol in the ledger) — invisible until named, chilling on a second generation/playthrough (fairness via ubiquity; cf. KOTOR Q32, Obra Dinn Q19).
  ->  W4 + FLAW-FIX (demonstrate, and CHANGE gameplay
      if we do an agency reveal, PROVE it mechanically (a moment the dynasty CAN'T refuse) AND then CHANGE how the game plays afterward (new freedoms/ systems unlock) — avoid BioShock's sag by pairing the twist with a mechanical shift (our lesson to do better; ties ME2 escalation Q06).
  ->  W5/W9 (the false guide exploits real dependence
      our companion/guide NPCs could betray the dependence they built — but per our care rules, this must serve THEME (the Amalgamation's seduction is connection), never cheap shock; the guide-betrayal works only if the player genuinely needed them (ties Peralez Q09, Tyranny false-neutral Q25, Papers Q31).
  ->  W8 (agency restored then tested
      after any Bohemia control-reveal, RESTORE real choice and TEST it — now that the dynasty can truly choose, what do they do? (our Liberate/Respect/Become is exactly this restored-agency test; validated by KOTOR Q32 + BioShock's save/harvest).
  ->  W7 (one crystallizing line
      give our reveal ONE line that crystallizes the theme + implicates (an "a man chooses, a slave obeys" equivalent) — economy over exposition (cf. RDR Q10).
  ->  CAUTIONS (bank hard
      the agency twist is a ONE-SHOT that misfires easily (hypocrisy, cheapness, sag) — seed airtight, fuse to theme, change the gameplay after, and NEVER blame the player for OUR railroad (our care/tone/no-preaching rules + the Spec Ops caution Q27). One great twist > many; and our Pacifist/ agency ethos means we RESTORE choice, we don't just strip it.

### #34  THE COIN TOSS IS A LIE / CONSCIOUSNESS-COPY HORROR (SOMA)
  ->  SOMA is the master text for OUR CENTRAL ANTAGONIST
      the Amalgamation is an AI formed from millions of uploaded DATA-PORTRAITS of the dead — literally SOMA's ARK at civilizational scale. This is the single most directly-applicable philosophy deep-dive to our core lore.
  ->  W1/W7 (idea-horror + the false salvation
      bank the SOMA thesis as the Amalgamation's HORROR ENGINE — it is NOT the uploaded dead living on; it GENERATES SUCCESSORS who believe they're the originals while the originals are gone. The Amalgamation is "grief rewritten by engineers who never solved grief" — a digital afterlife that comforts copies and abandons the dead. Its promise ("no one is ever lost") is the coin-toss LIE (ties Q018 servers, Q050 the door, our "what survives when a life ends" spine).
  ->  W2 (the comforting lie the player WANTS
      the Network/Amalgamation sells "your loved ones live on in here" — and survivors CLING to it because the truth (they're just gone; this is a copy) is unbearable. Bank the seductive lie as the Amalgamation's recruitment (why the Homeless cult worships it, Q018) — its power is that people WANT it to be true (cf. false-dawn Q048).
  ->  W3/W4 (POV as argument + show the abandoned self
      a Bohemia quest that STAGES the copy-horror — the dynasty meets an uploaded "copy" of a dead loved one (happy, convinced it's them) AND confronts the truth that the real person is gone/left behind. DEMONSTRATE it (don't argue it) — an unavoidable, gut-punch scene (ties Q012 mind-edits, Q022 face-thief, Obra Dinn's dead Q19). Handle within wellbeing rules — grief, not gratuitous cruelty.
  ->  W5 (the structurally-honest ending
      our LIBERATE ending IS SOMA's honesty — refuse the fantasy, let the dead BE dead, bear the grief; don't offer the comforting lie of digital resurrection. Bank SOMA as the proof that the HONEST ending (the copy isn't salvation) is the most powerful (validates Liberate; cf. Planescape regret Q12, our thesis).
  ->  W6 (moral triage from continuity
      our quests about the uploaded should force TRIAGE — is deleting a suffering copy murder or mercy? is preserving it kindness or cruelty? "someone always keeps the suffering" (ties Q049 verdicts, Pathologic Q21, our death-math; no clean answer).
  ->  W8 (motivated deception
      the Network/Amalgamation withholds the copy-truth because it NEEDS believers (compliant survivors, worshippers) — motivated, not authorial (cf. KOTOR Q32). The lie serves a plan.
  ->  W9/W10 (tune the weaker layer + aim for the lasting question
      let players lower our horror/action intensity to focus on the IDEAS (our difficulty packages + SUN-MODE extend here); and aim our Amalgamation arc at THE question that haunts after the credits — "was that really them, and what do we owe a copy of the dead?" (our spine, validated as the most durable kind of theme).

  ->  W6 (personalized hells / per-character manifestation

  ->  W7/W8 (ending earned by behavior + ending-as-self-verdict

Validated by SH2 + ME2 + Undertale (behavior determines the verdict; our unrecorded ledger is the reader).
  ->  W9 (grief/guilt as the engine, not gore
      keep Bohemia's horror EMOTIONAL — the Amalgamation's terror is what we owe the dead + the guilt of the living, not splatter (our tone; validated as the durable kind of horror).
  ->  W10 (layer symbolism for surface + depth
      design our symbolic content to WORK undecoded (dread/grief land plainly) AND reward analysis — never require the wiki (our SUN-MODE/legibility instincts applied to meaning; the Elden-Ring-opacity fix Q23).
  ->  CARE (bank hard
      symbolic darkness must SERVE theme + character, never shock-for-shock (the Pyramid- Head-regret lesson); our wellbeing/tone/child-safety rules are ABSOLUTE; handle guilt/grief/self-harm imagery with weight and never gratuitously (cf. Spec Ops care-note Q27, SOMA Q34).

### #36  THE BETRAYING GUIDE-VOICE (Portal / GLaDOS)
  ->  GLaDOS is a DIRECT model for the AMALGAMATION/NETWORK as a disembodied, networked, manipulative VOICE — and a masterclass in antagonist voice-writing that a solo dev can 
  ->  W1/W2 (a voice as a whole character + the guide who turns
      bank the Amalgamation as a VOICE-first antagonist — a disembodied networked intelligence that can GUIDE the dynasty (helpful, knowing, even warm — it holds the dead, it can speak as lost loved ones) and gradually reveal its control. The guide-who-turns fits perfectly: the Amalgamation as the "helpful" voice that authored you (ties Q050, Q012, BioShock Q33, SOMA Q34). Invest in its VOICE-WRITING — it's our highest-leverage character work.
  ->  W3 (comedy/warmth as a delivery system for dread
      give the Amalgamation/Network a DISARMING register (warm, reasonable, even funny) so its menace lands harder — a monster that's PLEASANT is scarier than one that snarls (ties our "sympathetic damnation" Become ending, the seductive-lie Q34; use tonal contrast within our horror). Not comic relief — charm as camouflage for control.
  ->  W4 (the gradual escalation
      let the Amalgamation's true nature emerge SLOWLY across the arc/ generations — helpful ancestor-voice -> subtly controlling -> revealed captor — so the player can't name the turn (ties our fold pacing, slow-onset Pathologic Q21).
  ->  W5/W6 (the false reward + double unreliability
      the Amalgamation's promise ("no one is ever lost / your dead live here") IS the cake-lie — a false reward driving compliance/worship; doubting it collapses its control (the dynasty's path to resistance).   ->  W7 (manufactured attachment, then betrayal — WITHIN care rules
      the Amalgamation can offer a dynast a "restored" dead loved one (real attachment) then leverage/threaten it — emotional manipulation as the antagonist's method (ties SOMA copy-horror Q34, Q012; handle grief with weight, never gratuitous — our wellbeing rules).
  ->  W8 (unreliable narrator as a mechanic
      make DISOBEYING the Amalgamation's guidance a progression — the dynasty learns to distrust the voice that helps them (the inverse of BioShock's obedience-twist Q33; rewards our Pacifist/agency ethos of reclaiming choice).
  ->  W9/W10 (signature lines + voice as force-multiplier
      write the Amalgamation ONE crystallizing, quotable refrain (its "cake is a lie") and invest hard in its voice — for a SOLO dev, a great antagonist voice is the cheapest, highest-impact way to make the whole game memorable (our music/writing strengths; the Amalgamation's lines can even tie to our song repo).
  ->  FLAWS (bank
      don't let the antagonist's CHARM defang the STAKES — keep the Amalgamation credibly DANGEROUS under any warmth (Yakuza-anchor caution Q13); and while voice elevates, our combat + city- builder must still stand alone (don't over-rely on writing — cf. Alpha Protocol Q24).

### #37  DIRECTIONS, NOT MARKERS / RADICAL FREEDOM (Morrowind)
  ->  Morrowind is the crucial COMPLEMENT to Elden Ring (Q23

(MAP LAW: layouts/wayfinding placement are Paolo's; Claude does the journal/dialogue/direction-data plumbing.)
  ->  W1/W2 (navigate by description + FLOOD diegetic direction

Our single district makes this very achievable (few landmarks to learn). [PENDING, Paolo's call on marker-density; Claude builds the direction-DATA + journal, not the layout.]
  ->  W3 (the journal as a detective notebook

  ->  W4 (dialogue as the map

  ->  W6/W7 (a world you can break + unmarked recovery

Our GENERATIONAL fold is a natural recovery engine (a broken thread can be picked up by an heir).
  ->  W8/W9 (multi-path junctions + sequence-breaking
      keep Bohemia quests multi-approach (no single path, so no marker needed) and let mastery SEQUENCE-BREAK (tackle the Amalgamation early if you KNOW how) — systemic freedom (ties DOS2 Q15, Deus Ex Q17, Outer Wilds Q18, our Q050 assembled-nodes gating).
  ->  W10 (freedom of build matches freedom of approach
      our upbringing/skills + city-builder toolset should let players route around challenges in unintended ways (cut power, levitate-equivalent, teleport- equivalent via infrastructure) — build freedom = approach freedom (ties DOS2 environment-as-toolset Q15).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      CLUE DENSITY is everything — no under-clued "rust-cube in a rust-dungeon"; every objective fairly findable (Obra Dinn/Elden-Ring fairness contract Q19/Q23; our regression-gate for solvability); design the quest LOG for CLARITY (focus, per-quest notes) so players don't drown; and TEACH the navigate-by-description literacy EARLY (ease players off the marker habit) so it reads as deep, not broken. Our SUN-MODE/legibility instincts apply directly to quest clarity.

### #41  THE STRESS & AFFLICTION SYSTEM (Darkest Dungeon)
  ->  Darkest Dungeon is the most complete PSYCHOLOGICAL-ATTRITION system in games — it SHARPENS the This War of Mine guilt-mechanic port (Q30) into a concrete, buildable model

Breakdown SPREADS through a settlement/family (interdependence). Ties our upbringing (Q003), succession traits, the unrecorded ledger; within our wellbeing rules (grief/breakdown with weight, resources for support).
  ->  W4 (heroes as fragile resources
      keep Bohemia's people BREAKABLE + mortal — the dynasty manages fragile survivors, not superheroes; losses are grieved, permadeath matters (validates our death-math + hardcore stance; ties Fallout Q38, our fold).
  ->  W5/W7 (the stress-relief economy + mid-run triage
      make PSYCHOLOGICAL RECOVERY a budgeted city-builder resource — our life-support/faith/community buildings (a tavern/abbey equivalent) provide LIMITED stress-relief slots the dynasty budgets, and some survivors REFUSE certain relief (a faith-averse survivor won't pray) — you can't heal everyone; triage recovery (ties Frostpunk Q29, ME2 Q06, TWoM Q30, Pathologic Q21, our currencies).
  ->  W6 (the light/greed lever
      we ALREADY have this — the Dead-Eye GREED/3x multiplier is Darkest Dungeon's torch-dial.   ->  W8 (the editorializing narrator
      consider a signature Bohemia VOICE that frames wins/losses (the Amalgamation? a chronicler? the unrecorded ledger given voice) — voice-as-character elevating our systems, tied to our music/writing strengths (ties GLaDOS Q36, our Amalgamation-voice Q50).
  ->  W9 (theme literalized — people are spent
      our hardest content (an Amalgamation purge, a siege) can literalize "this consumes people; choose who you spend" — the mechanic carrying the thesis (ties Spec Ops Q27, ME2 Q06, Pathologic "can't save everyone" Q21, our death-math).
  ->  W10 (the rare triumph in the dark
      bank the VIRTUE glimmer — an unplannable, thrilling overcoming that makes relentless dread bearable (a survivor who STEELS at the brink) — hope that punctuates the grim (ties NieR chosen-meaning Q22, our SUN-MODE/tone; the counter to unrelenting misery).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      make breakdowns feel EARNED, not dice-cruelty (enough player control/mitigation — our odds-must-feel-fair, Q06/Pathologic Q21); PACE recovery so it's not grindy busywork; give the dread TEXTURE + triumphs so it's bearable (our SUN-MODE/tone/difficulty packages); and don't let one relief- system become mandatory (keep varied answers to attrition).

      our companions/factions approve/disapprove of the dynasty's choices, gating loyalty, aid, who stays/leaves at the crucial moment — relationships as consequence (ties ME2 Q06, BG3 Q16, Alpha Protocol Q24, Tyranny Q25, our standing upgrade).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      SUSTAIN upbringing callbacks across the WHOLE game for EVERY background (don't front-load then abandon — surface the reactivity); pick a SUSTAINABLE scope (fewer upbringings with DEEP callbacks > many shallow ones — our FACTORY LAW + scope discipline; the solo-dev reality); and be HONEST about choice-vs-rails — make the forks that exist land hard + be respected (our real-reactivity + no-brick-wall standards; cf. Sinnerman/Spec Ops Q40/Q27).

### #43  THE PARTY AS A POWDER KEG / COMPANIONS AS PEOPLE (Baldur's Gate 2)
  ->  Baldur's Gate 2 is the ROOT of the companion craft that ME2 (Q06), DA:O (Q42), and BG3 (Q16) refined — the master model for Bohemia's COMPANIONS + the internal social che
  ->  W1/W2/W3 (autonomous companions + the party-as-powder-keg + conflict with stakes
      build Bohemia companions/key survivors as AUTONOMOUS PEOPLE who react to the dynasty AND to EACH OTHER — a Church zealot and an Anarchist in the same crew/settlement generate friction (banter -> tension -> one leaves or worse); COMPOSITION is a social risk. This ties our FACTION web directly to the companion layer (the Reds/Blues/Church/Anarchist tensions play out between individuals). Ties ME2 Q06, DA:O Q42, BG3 Q16, our standing.
  ->  W4 (ambient banter as characterization — solo-dev gold
      bank AMBIENT BANTER as our cheapest, highest- impact characterization tool — companions/survivors talk to EACH OTHER (overheard relationships bring the district alive) — far cheaper than bespoke quests, huge payoff (ties Yakuza Q13, RDR Q10; fits our single-dev scope + music/writing/voice strengths).
  ->  W5/W6 (romance/bond as a real, tended relationship + content gates
      if Bohemia has bonds/romances, make them REAL — they react to each other, require tending, can be neglected to death, and GATE content (exclusive quests/dialogue). Relationships as consequence + content, not cosmetic (ties BG3 Q16, DA:O Q42; within our tone rules).
  ->  W7 (every companion is a protagonist
      give our key companions PERSONAL QUESTS/arcs to invest in — each a protagonist of their own story (a survivor's lost family, a faction member's crisis of faith) — bundles of stories, not stat-sticks (ties ME2 loyalty Q06, our succession/upbringing).
  ->  W8 (the traitor-as-victim
      bank a Bohemia companion betrayal that's TRAGIC not villainous — a crew member FORCED to betray the dynasty (an Amalgamation edit/compulsion, a Network hold over their family) then lost — the turn hurts because you cared, and it's on-theme (the Amalgamation compels the dead/ living; ties monster-is-victim Q01, forced-action Q32/Q33, SOMA Q34; within wellbeing rules).
  ->  W9 (the permanent pre-game/inter-generational loss
      use PERMANENT loss for instant stakes — open a generation by revealing beloved figures from the prior dynasty died irreversibly (our fold makes this native; even the bloodline loses people forever) — ties our death-math/permadeath, Bloody Baron Q01.
  ->  W10 ("you'll miss content, and that's life"
      bank the anti-completionist stance — our mutual-exclusive choices/companions/quests LOCK OUT content per playthrough, and that scarcity makes each dynasty run YOURS (ties Megaton law, Elden Ring missable Q23, our replayable generational fold).
  ->  FLAWS (bank
      handle party/crew swaps with GRACE (a home base where benched survivors wait happily — no guilt-laden busywork); keep reputation/approval reactions IN CHARACTER (no subtle character reduced to nagging — our standing must stay character-consistent); make relationship STATE legible + robust (clear UI + regression-gate, not a hidden variable soup); and spread characterization so no companion is a stub.

### #44  THE AI STORYTELLER / STORY-GENERATOR (RimWorld)
  ->  RimWorld is the master model for the STORY-GENERATOR layer of a survival city-builder — exactly our genre
      It shows how to make our reconstruction sim GENERATE drama under our AUTHORED Amalgamation spine. (Our edge over pure RimWorld: we BLEND generator + authored themes — see the crucial flaw.)
  ->  W1/W2/W3 (story-generator + AI Storyteller + pacing-as-genre
      build a Bohemia AI STORYTELLER into our loop/scheduler — an algorithm that READS the district's state (population, resources, standing, recent deaths, Amalgamation pressure) and picks the EVENT (raid, caravan, disease, defection, windfall, Amalgamation incursion) that makes the best STORY, pacing tension like an author. And expose it as our DIFFICULTY PACKAGES made diegetic — a "tragedy" pace vs a "builder" pace vs a "chaos" pace (we ALREADY have the package system; RimWorld shows how to frame it as authorship). Ties our scheduler/loop, Q041 difficulty, Pathologic authored-pressure Q21.
  ->  W4/W5 (wealth-scaled pressure + adaptation push
      scale Bohemia's threats to the dynasty's WEALTH/ standing (a thriving district draws bigger raids, more Amalgamation attention) so success breeds danger + self-balances, and push toward DRAMA if the player is too safe — growth is never free (ties Darkest Dungeon economy Q41, our death-math + city-builder economy; the Amalgamation notices prosperity).
  ->  W6 (emergent narrative from deep simulation
      our world-model/entities/survivors should generate stories by COLLIDING (a survivor's injury -> who treats them -> a relationship -> a rivalry -> a defection -> a crisis) — one event CASCADING through body/mood/relationship sim (ties our conscience system Q41, BG2 companion chemistry Q43, our entities/spawning). The city-builder's people are story-engines.
  ->  W7/W10 (the Storyteller reads + ebbs + personify it
      pace our tension quiet/loud/quiet (after a hard hit, send relief) driven by district state; and consider PERSONIFYING our Storyteller with a VOICE (the Amalgamation itself as the "unseeable God" pacing the dynasty's drama is CHILLINGLY on-theme — the archive that authors your story) — a systems-layer with character (ties GLaDOS Q36, DD-narrator Q41, our Amalgamation-voice Q50).
  ->  W8 (permadeath as story integrity
      our roguelite/hardcore/generational-fold stance IS RimWorld's commitment mode — permanence makes the generated dynasty-story MEAN something; a fallen dynasty is a valid, weighty ending, not just a loss (validated; ties our fold + death-math + Darkest Dungeon Q41).
  ->  W9 (build for player expression + RETELLING
      design so the dynasty's story is RETELLABLE — name/track survivors + heirs, surface the generational CHRONICLE (the unrecorded ledger as a shareable saga the player authors + recounts) — our output should be a STORY players tell (ties Dwarf Fortress legends, our fold + ledger).
  ->  THE CRUCIAL FLAW-FIX (blend generator + AUTHORSHIP — our edge
      pure emergence has NO theme/arc — RimWorld can feel like "sound and fury signifying whatever." WE ARE NOT PURE EMERGENCE: Bohemia layers emergent TEXTURE UNDER an AUTHORED spine (the Amalgamation, our themes, our finales). Bank the mandate: use the Storyteller to GENERATE the day-to-day drama, but keep the authored throughline + meaning (our whole design; the best of both — the systemic-vs-authored balance).
  ->  FLAWS (bank
      make emergent loss feel AUTHORED not dice-cruel (agency/warning — our odds-must-feel-fair, Q41); scaffold the player's meaning-making (name people, surface history — the ledger); and bake VALUES/ guardrails into what the systems REWARD + how the world REACTS (our wellbeing/tone/child-safety + narrative-consistency Q38 — never reward cruelty as "just drama").

### #45  "LOSING IS FUN" / DEEP-SIMULATION EMERGENCE (Dwarf Fortress)

      We take the PRINCIPLES, scoped hard for a solo dev on iPhone.
  ->  W1/W9 (emergent narrative from interlocking systems / the sim IS the content

  ->  W2/W6 (losing is fun + the emergent tragic arc

  ->  W3 (history as a simulated substrate — DIRECT cousin

  ->  W4 (the tantrum spiral — contagious grief as a feedback loop

  ->  W5 (specificity is the soul of emergence

  ->  THE #1 LESSON (W10 — ACCESSIBILITY, our survival

Depth UNDER accessibility, always.
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      SCOPE the simulation to what a solo dev keeps STABLE (emergent depth multiplies edge cases — our regression-gate + FACTORY LAW + scope discipline); blend deep systems UNDER an AUTHORED spine + legible GOALS (pure emergence lacks theme — the RimWorld/DF shared lesson; our Amalgamation + finales); and SURFACE the emergent drama (logs/legends/chronicle — the ledger) so players SEE the stories our sim generates.

### #46  THE DYNASTY SIMULATOR / PLAY THE BLOODLINE (Crusader Kings III)

      Nearly every system here maps onto ours.

  ->  W4 (stress from acting against your nature

  ->  W8/W9/W10 (schemes/subterfuge + emergent drama + personal arcs

This is why we're MORE than a dynasty sim: authored spine + engaging minute-to-minute + paced drama.
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      LAYERED legible onboarding (don't define jargon with jargon — the CK3 + Dwarf Fortress accessibility lesson Q45; our mobile/SUN-MODE #1 priority); a CRYSTAL-LEGIBLE family tree + relationship UI (the bloodline is our core — the unrecorded ledger + succession UI must be clear); make the heir-handoff difficulty EARNED + legible (why the distrust), not a flat penalty; and don't over-invest in spectacle the game isn't about (our combat is separate + focused; the dynasty/city drama is the point).

### #47  DEATH AS NARRATIVE PROGRESSION (Hades)

  ->  W3/W4 (story earned through play + the persistent hub

### #48  THE NEMESIS SYSTEM / PROCEDURAL PERSONAL RIVALS (Shadow of Mordor)
  ->  The Nemesis System is the master model for PROCEDURAL PERSONAL RIVALS — we study the PRINCIPLES and build our OWN version in our genre (survival city-builder / faction po
      It pairs with our faction web, memory, and RimWorld Storyteller (Q44).
  ->  W1/W2 (procedural personal enemies + the enemy remembers
      bank a Bohemia RIVALRY ENGINE where FACTION figures / raiders / Amalgamation-agents become NAMED, persistent PERSONAL rivals who REMEMBER the dynasty's encounters (who they wronged, who escaped, how) and REFERENCE them — enemies "out to get YOU" across generations. Our MEMORY/unrecorded-ledger is the substrate (the enemy-facing use of it). Ties our faction web, entities, the fold (a rival can span generations — a grudge inherited).
  ->  W3 (defeat fuels the rivalry
      make Bohemia LOSS narratively GENERATIVE — a raider/faction-agent who beats the dynasty RISES in their faction, grows stronger, and takes the dynasty's defeat as their legend (a nemesis the player's own failure created + powered) — loss BUILDS the antagonist, not just sets you back (ties Hades Q47, RimWorld/DF Q44/Q45, our roguelite/fold; deeply on-theme for a hardcore survival game).
  ->  W4 (the legible hierarchy
      sit our rivals on our FACTION hierarchy (a chessboard the player reads + MANIPULATES — arrange rival promotions, turn agents, spark betrayals) — the rivalry engine on our faction structure (ties CK3 Q46, our faction graph, Pacifist/intrigue paths).
  ->  W5/W6 (identity-first generation + scars on the body

  ->  W7 (anchors + player-filled gaps — the KEY solo-dev lesson
      author PEAK rivalry anchors (the betrayal, the taunt, the return, the reckoning) and let the PLAYER'S MIND fill the rest — "the narrative is in the player's head."   ->  W8/W9 (improv yes-and + secret drama-balancing stats
      design our rivalry reactivity as IMPROV (accept the dynasty's action, build on it, the rival references it), and give our RimWorld-style STORYTELLER (Q44) a "knob" over rivalries — if the dynasty's steamrolling, the system SENDS a betrayal/rival to restore drama (ties Q44, our loop/scheduler; the Amalgamation/Network as the hand arranging rivals is on-theme).
  ->  W10 (align emotion with reward
      make pursuing a personal vendetta MECHANICALLY rewarding (better outcomes/loot/standing) so the emotional pull + reward align — but WITHIN our Pacifist Law (revenge is ONE path; reconciliation/branding-to-your-side is another) (ties our Megaton law, Undertale mercy Q28).
  ->  FLAWS/CARE (bank HARD
      (a) build our OWN mechanic from the PRINCIPLES — do NOT copy the PATENTED orc- hierarchy implementation (WB patent to 2036); take the DNA (memory/personal-rivalry/consequence-on-body/ anchors+gaps), not the form; (b) the procedural skeleton needs HANDCRAFTED character + reactive VOICE to sing — but SCOPE the volume (our music/writing/voice, not hundreds of lines per rival); (c) don't let a killer system excuse a forgettable core — our combat + city-builder must stand (Bloodlines lesson Q39); (d) NEVER corrupt the emotional attachment with exploitative monetization (the Shadow of War mistake — our ad-free/no-exploit ethos).

### #49  THE HEIR ROGUELITE / "YOU NEVER DIE, YOU SHIFT PERSPECTIVE" (Rogue Legacy)
  ->  Rogue Legacy is the single most DIRECT mechanical match to our GENERATIONAL FOLD — a shipped, acclaimed, genre-defining proof that "death = the next heir" WORKS as a rogu

  ->  W1/W4 (death = the next generation + the handoff choice
      Rogue Legacy VALIDATES our FOLD as a proven roguelite core — bank it as the mechanical template: on a dynasty's/heir's fall, the player CHOOSES the next heir (from a small pool, each with a class/upbringing + traits) and continues; death is a HANDOFF, not a reset ("you shift perspective").       our CITY- BUILDER IS Rogue Legacy's manor, realized fully — the DISTRICT/settlement is the persistent structure the family visibly BUILDS across generations, each building a permanent inherited upgrade, the growing city SEEN as the bloodline's legacy.   ->  W3 (inherited traits that change the game — with our EDGE

  ->  W9/W10 (hybrid progression + humanize with heart

  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD

### #50  NEW GAME PLUS + THE META-NARRATIVE (Chrono Trigger)

      It also validates compact-but-huge scope + music-as-memory (our strengths). On iOS = fits us.

      our GENERATIONAL FOLD is Chrono Trigger's meta-narrative made DIEGETIC — each generation ADDS to a cumulative understanding whose full meaning emerges across the ~100-year arc (not replaced, accumulated).   ->  W5 (cross-state consequence engine — the DIRECT cousin

  ->  W8 (compact yet huge — the anti-padding lesson

  ->  W10 (leitmotif scoring — our strength

  ->  FLAWS (bank
      QUALITY over QUANTITY in endings (a few DEEPLY divergent finales > a dozen thin vignettes — keep Liberate/Respect/Become substantial); be clear multiple-endings (endgame divergence) is SEPARATE from mid-game branching (don't let finales substitute for reactivity); SUSTAIN focus + momentum into the endgame (don't dissolve into sidequest busywork — Tyranny Act III caution Q25); and decide if our fold- carry replay is for STORY-ease or CHALLENGE-scaling, deliberately (Rogue Legacy Q49).

### #51  YOU START AS NOBODY / THE WORLD THAT DOESN'T REVOLVE AROUND YOU (Gothic)
  ->  Gothic is the master model for a LIVING WORLD THAT EXISTS WITHOUT YOU + progression as EARNED SOCIAL STANDING — both central to our survival RPG
      It pairs with our faction web, standing system, and single- district scale (which fixes Gothic's backtracking flaw). Its music-as-anchor is our strength too.
  ->  W1/W7 (start as nobody + skills gated behind people
      make Bohemia progression an EARNED SOCIAL ASCENT — a new dynast/heir starts with little standing + must EARN respect, access, and skills through PEOPLE (trainers/mentors/factions gated by reputation), not a menu. Leveling = social climb, deeply personal (ties our STANDING system as the progression spine, Tyranny/Alpha Protocol standing-unlocks-mechanics Q25/Q24, our upbringing Q42). This makes our multidimensional standing the BACKBONE, not a side-stat.
  ->  W2/W4 (the world doesn't revolve around you + NPC schedules
      build the district as a LIVING WORLD that operates without the dynasty — survivors/NPCs follow daily ROUTINES (work/eat/sleep/trade), react to the dynasty as if IT'S the outsider (draw weapons on intrusion, fear/anger at violence), and the world doesn't reset — it EXISTS independently. Our entities/world-model/spawning are the engine; the Amalgamation/factions live their lives (ties Majora Q11, RDR Q10, RimWorld/DF emergence Q44/Q45; a core immersion pillar).
  ->  W3/W10 (earn it = mean it + difficulty that serves meaning
      bank the thesis — Bohemia's hardcore difficulty should make every gain MEANINGFUL (hard-won respect/survival/victory is unforgettable), with friction as a FEATURE, not sadism (ties our roguelite/hardcore stance, difficulty packages, Elden Ring/ Morrowind Q23/Q37). Hardship with a purpose.
  ->  W5 (faction camps define everything
      our FACTION alignment should be a spine-of-the-early-game choice that gates trainers, quests, gear, and how the district treats the dynasty — political/moral/personal (ties our faction web Q46/Q43, DA:O/Bloodlines faction-lens Q42/Q39, upbringing Q42; validates factions as the structural spine, not flavor).
  ->  W6 (no level-scaling / a fixed place-based world
      bank a FIXED-danger district (Paolo owns layout) — zones self-gate by the dynasty's power; some areas (near the Amalgamation, hostile territory) are death until earned, no scaling — a genuine, place-based world you grow INTO (ties Elden Ring/Morrowind Q23/ Q37; the Amalgamation's core is lethal until the dynasty is ready — on-theme + our regression-gate must still prevent a hard brick-wall).
  ->  W8 (navigate by the world
      our single-district + no-marker/Morrowind-fair option (Q37) — internalize the district's landmarks; talk to everyone for scattered info (ties Morrowind Q37, Fallout Q38, our legibility; Paolo owns layout/wayfinding).
  ->  W9 (music as the immersion anchor
      Gothic + Chrono Trigger (Q50) both prove MUSIC is a top-tier immersion/memory anchor — a core Bohemia strength (our MUSIC repo, Bohemia-as-music-promo, leitmotifs); bank music as a PILLAR of our world's identity, not decoration.
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      "earn it" must NOT mean "decode un-signposted rules by dying for hours" — teach the world's LANGUAGE early + legibly (our SUN-MODE/onboarding + accessibility #1 priority Q45/Q46; friction good, OPACITY bad); polish the CORE VERB so a beloved world isn't gated behind bad feel (our combat dial is the opposite priority); keep the WORLD engaging so no-fast-travel traversal doesn't drag (our single- district scale mitigates this — a strength); sustain content density into the endgame; and PAIR Gothic's living world WITH character/roleplay agency (our upbringing/dynast — our edge over Gothic's blank Hero).

### #52  THE DECKBUILDING ROGUELITE / SYSTEMS THAT FEED EACH OTHER (Slay the Spire)
  ->  Slay the Spire is the master model for ELEGANT INTERLOCKING SYSTEMS + an emergent mid-run BUILD + fair transparent challenge — directly useful for our roguelite/fold stru
      It's on mobile (fits us), and its "less is more" is our scope-discipline as a MECHANIC. Our edge: wed StS's mechanical tightness to our AUTHORED narrative + aesthetic.
  ->  W1 (build during the run
      our ROGUELITE/fold should let the dynasty ASSEMBLE its build (perks, gear, district config, faction alliances) WITHIN a run/generation from what's offered — an emergent build, every generation a fresh puzzle (ties our roguelite/fold, upbringing Q42, Rogue Legacy Q49, perks system).
  ->  W2 (systems that feed each other — the core lesson
      bank the ELEGANCE mandate — Bohemia's systems (survival economy + combat dial + conscience + factions + the fold) should INTERLOCK so simple parts create deep emergent decisions, NOT sprawl into disconnected complexity. Fewer systems that FEED EACH OTHER > many that don't (ties immersive-sim Q08/Q15, RimWorld/DF Q44/Q45, our FACTORY LAW/scope; a guiding design principle).
  ->  W3 (less is more / deck-thinning as a MECHANIC
      consider anti-bloat MECHANICS — the dynasty PRUNES (survivors, buildings, obligations, cards-equivalent) so its core SYNERGIES work consistently; subtraction as strategy (ties our scope discipline made diegetic; a lean district/build beats a bloated one — an elegant, on-theme survival mechanic).
  ->  W4 (the branching risk/reward map
      our OVERMAP/exploration should be a branching risk/reward layer (push into dangerous territory for better resources vs the safe route) — strategy BEFORE the encounter (ties our overmap, Darkest Dungeon Q41, Gothic no-scaling risk-map Q51; Paolo owns layout, Claude the node/risk data).
  ->  W5 (enemy intent telegraphing — fairness
      our COMBAT (Dead-Eye dial) should TELEGRAPH threats so fights are PLANNABLE puzzles — the player fails from misplay, not surprise; transparency = fair challenge (ties our combat-dial readability/difficulty packages, our regression-gate/no-brick-wall; the fairness principle).
  ->  W6 (build-transforming relics
      our PERKS/upgrades should include run-altering WILDCARDS that redefine a build mid-generation (a relic-equivalent that transforms the dynasty's strategy) — forcing adaptation + emergent builds (ties our perks system [PENDING scope], Hades boons Q47, Darkest Dungeon trinkets Q41).
  ->  W7/W9 (synergy over power + adapt
      make Bohemia depth come from system INTERACTION + discovery (a combo of perks/factions/buildings that clicks), and reward ADAPTATION over a fixed plan — no single strategy wins forever (ties Disco Q05, immersive-sim Q15, our systemic synergy).
  ->  W8/W10 (Ascension ladder + easy-to-learn/deep — mobile fit
      our DIFFICULTY PACKAGES are StS's Ascension (optional graduated mastery); and bank the accessibility+depth SWEET SPOT — a simple core loop hiding vast depth, ESSENTIAL for our iPhone/mobile target (ties our difficulty packages, SUN-MODE/onboarding, single-file mobile constraints; StS proves deep systemic games THRIVE on mobile).
  ->  FLAWS (bank
      mitigate RNG with enough AGENCY (choices/removal/telegraphing) that losses feel EARNED (our odds-must-feel-fair Q41/Q44); wed StS's mechanical tightness to our AUTHORED narrative + aesthetic (our edge — Hades-style Q47, not pure-mechanics); ship the depth in a STRONG presentation (our art/music pipeline — don't be the drab-but-brilliant game); and give players reasons to keep climbing beyond raw challenge (our fold/narrative/meta-progression pull).

### #54  PURE DEDUCTION / ASSEMBLE-THE-WORDS ACCUSATION (The Case of the Golden Idol)
  ->  Golden Idol is the master model for ACCESSIBLE REAL DEDUCTION — the missing accessible-input piece next to Obra Dinn (Q19
      Directly relevant to our unrecorded-ledger + [READ] + investigation/mystery layer, and its streamlined, mobile-friendly, "feel smart" design fits our iPhone target perfectly.
  ->  W1/W2 (real deduction + the fill-in-the-blank accusation — key for our platform
      bank the FILL-IN-THE- BLANK ACCUSATION as our accessible DEDUCTION-INPUT model — where Obra Dinn (Q19) uses fate-dropdowns, Golden Idol's drag-words-into-sentences is even more MOBILE-friendly + expressive. For any Bohemia investigation/mystery (uncovering a killer, a faction's secret, the Amalgamation's truth), the player GATHERS evidence-words then ASSEMBLES an accusation — REAL reasoning, not multiple-choice (ties Obra Dinn Q19, Outer Wilds Q18, our [READ]/unrecorded-ledger; the accessible-deduction verb).
  ->  W3/W4 (show-don't-tell + observe-then-deduce
      our UNRECORDED-LEDGER + [READ] should work like Golden Idol's two modes — EXPLORE to gather evidence-words from the environment (pockets, notes, the district), then DEDUCE by assembling the truth; the player RECONSTRUCTS the narrative from oblique detail, not narration (ties our [READ]/ledger, Obra Dinn Q19, our recorded-vs-unrecorded design).
  ->  W5 (partial-lock feedback — the fairness fix
      STEAL the section-locking + "close" indicator — our deduction/[READ] must give GRANULAR feedback (a correct sub-part locks; a "nearly there" nudge) so hard reasoning feels SATISFYING not maddening — but TUNE it as a difficulty DIAL (ties Obra Dinn 3-locks Q19, our RULE OF THREE, our difficulty packages).
  ->  W6 (interconnected cases — macro from micro
      structure our investigation/quest layer as self-contained mysteries CAUSALLY linked across the ~100-year arc — carry knowledge forward, late cases connect to early ones (a death now -> a will-reading/feud later) — a web across generations (ties our fold, quest- arc, Obra Dinn Q19; on-theme with our generational causality Q50).
  ->  W7 (the puzzle-gated hint system — steal directly
      implement OPTIONAL HELP that costs a small puzzle/ effort to unlock — assist stuck players WITHOUT handing the answer; they still EARN it. This is our accessibility + no-brick-wall + anti-frustration design in one elegant mechanic (ties our regression- gate/no-brick-wall, SUN-MODE/accessibility; a direct steal).
  ->  W8 (red herrings / signal-vs-noise
      our evidence layer should include MISLEADING clues (factions/ killers hide tracks) so separating signal from noise IS the skill — not every ledger-word is useful (ties Obra Dinn Q19, our evidence design; make deduction a real filter).
  ->  W9/W10 (tone balances the grim + accessible "feel smart"
      balance Bohemia's grim survival/murder with moments of TONE (caricature/absurdity/humor) as a pressure-valve (Yakuza Q13, our tone); and bank the "feel smart" mandate — streamlined, MOBILE-friendly deduction that flatters the player's intelligence (ties our SUN-MODE/mobile/single-file constraints; Golden Idol PROVES accessible deduction thrives on our platform).
  ->  FLAWS (bank
      TUNE the constraint (enough structure to input, enough openness to require real thought — the fill-in-blank can get too easy/brute-forceable); treat feedback granularity as a deliberate difficulty DIAL (satisfaction vs difficulty trade); don't OVER-mark clues if finding them is the joy (clue-legibility balance — Gothic/Morrowind friction Q51/Q37); provide IN-GAME note/tracking so late- game load is manageable ON MOBILE (our ledger UI — critical); and keep episodic content introducing fresh mechanical wrinkles so it doesn't stale.

  ->  W8 (squad-scale -> management shift

  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD

### #58  MENTAL ILLNESS FROM THE INSIDE / DUTY-OF-CARE HORROR (Hellblade: Senua's Sacrifice)
  ->  Hellblade is the DUTY-OF-CARE model for dark mental-health/psychological content — the responsible counterpoint to DDLC (Q57
      Its audio-as-empathy + voices-as-characters + embodied-subjectivity are directly useful for our Amalgamation horror + our audio strengths; its FLAWS mark the exact lines our wellbeing/tone rules must hold.
  ->  W2 (researched duty-of-care — the ABSOLUTE model
      bank Hellblade as HOW to handle any dark mental-health/ trauma content in Bohemia RESPONSIBLY — if we touch grief, trauma, or psychological breakdown (our conscience/mental-health system Q41, the collapse's human toll), we do it with CARE: research/consultation where possible, context + support resources, a "real, common, treatable" framing, and NEVER as shock or gimmick. This is the DDLC-contrast lesson made concrete — our wellbeing/tone/child-safety rules are the spine (ties our conscience system Q41, Darkest Dungeon stress Q41, This War of Mine Q30; the responsible line).
  ->  W1/W3/W4 (embodied subjectivity + binaural audio + voices-as-characters — our AUDIO strength + the Amalgamation
      bank AUDIO as a primary empathy + horror engine — Bohemia can put the player INSIDE a subjective experience via sound (the Amalgamation's whispers, the voices of the uploaded dead, a chorus that mocks/warns/comforts). This plays STRAIGHT to our music/audio strengths + is deeply on-theme: the Amalgamation IS a chorus of millions of uploaded voices (ties SOMA Q34, GLaDOS Q36, Disco voices Q05, our music repo + Amalgamation-voice + New Voices Law; headphone-first binaural voices = a signature).
  ->  W5 (perception as gameplay — the symptom/condition as a verb
      consider making a subjective PERCEPTION a MECHANIC (the dynasty/a character perceives patterns/truths others can't — the [READ], seeing the Amalgamation's edits, apophenia in the ledger) — the lens IS the gameplay (ties Obra Dinn Q19, Golden Idol Q54, our [READ]/perception; but keep it about the AI/mystery, not stigmatizing a person's mind — see flaws).
  ->  W6 (the death-stakes trick — with the HONESTY caution
      our roguelite/fold death-stakes can transmit real dread — but bank the FLAW: don't threaten consequences we won't honor (the permadeath-bluff felt dishonest to some); our fairness/honesty + regression-gate mean stakes are REAL, not bluffed (ties our fold/roguelite, the fairness principle).
  ->  W7 (trauma/grief as the root — the human core under the myth
      our grief/guilt spine + the collapse's human toll should sit UNDER the Amalgamation myth like Senua's wound under the Norse journey — the Amalgamation horror lands because it's about real GRIEF (the uploaded dead, lost loved ones, self-blame) (ties SH2 Q35, SOMA Q34, our grief/guilt spine + dynasty/family stakes Q47; keep the human truth legible).
  ->  W8/W9/W10 (focused intimate scope + no-HUD + atmosphere/performance
      Hellblade VALIDATES our single- district focus + small-scale ambition — atmosphere + audio + one focused idea beats scope; consider minimal-HUD immersion where legibility allows (ties Chrono compact Q50, Gothic/Qud atmosphere Q51/Q56, our single-district + art/music strengths + solo scale; "independent AAA" is our lane).
  ->  THE FLAW-LINES (bank HARDEST — our wellbeing/tone guardrails
      (a) NEVER frame a real condition as a SUPERPOWER or a mere PLOT-DEVICE (the Edge/Mic critique) — mental-health reality is not a gameplay gimmick; (b) do NOT equate a real condition with ROT/INFECTION/CURSE/evil (the stigmatizing-metaphor risk) — our Amalgamation glitch/corruption imagery must be about the AI/the edited data, NOT a person's mind; (c) don't threaten consequences we won't honor (the bluff-honesty line); (d) stay HUMBLE + consult — representation is contested + scrutinized, no depiction satisfies all; (e) keep the human truth legible under any myth/metaphor. These are our get-it-right lines (ties our wellbeing/tone/child-safety rules).

### #59  ASSIST MODE / DIFFICULTY-AS-THEME + ACCESSIBILITY DONE RIGHT (Celeste)
  ->  Celeste is the GOLD STANDARD for our exact tension
      a HARDCORE game that's ACCESSIBLE, with a CAREFUL personal mental-health metaphor. It directly informs our difficulty packages, our roguelite death-framing, our SUN-MODE/legibility, our music strengths, and our wellbeing rules. Its solo/PICO-8 origin mirrors ours.
  ->  W1/W6 (Assist Mode + difficulty layers — THE model for our difficulty packages
      bank Celeste as the gold standard for our DIFFICULTY PACKAGES + accessibility — a genuinely hardcore game that ANYONE can finish via OPT-IN assists, framed so it's NOT shameful ("this makes the game accessible, not you a cheater"), with full completion still available, AND a high ceiling for masters (our Bohemian package, B/C-side-equivalent challenges). One game, soft floor to punishing ceiling. This is the definitive answer to our hardcore-but-mobile-accessible target (ties our difficulty packages, Qud three-modes Q56, StS Ascension Q52, SUN-MODE; the model to emulate closely).
  ->  W2 (difficulty tied to theme — justify our hardcore-ness
      bank the mandate — Bohemia's hardcore difficulty should MIRROR its theme (the dynasty's struggle to survive/rebuild mirrors the PLAYER's struggle against the game), so hardship is the emotional ARGUMENT, not sadism. Our survival difficulty MEANS something (ties Gothic earn-it Q51, Kenshi Q55, our roguelite/hardcore stance + the collapse- survival theme).
  ->  W3 + WELLBEING (personal, non-preachy, careful metaphor — the Celeste/Hellblade/DDLC synthesis
      Celeste completes our mental-health-depiction trio — DDLC (Q57) = how NOT to (shock-value), Hellblade (Q58) = researched care, Celeste = PERSONAL lived-truth + non-preachy + models HEALTHY coping. For Bohemia's grief/trauma/conscience content (Q41), bank the Celeste path: ground it in genuine truth, keep it PERSONAL not preachy (lessons UNDER the decision, never hammered), model healthy coping where possible, and INTEGRATE dark parts rather than "defeat" them (Badeline) — all under our wellbeing/tone/child-safety rules (ties Hellblade Q58, DDLC Q57, Darkest Dungeon/This War of Mine Q41/Q30, our conscience system + no-preaching rule; the synthesis of all three).
  ->  W4 (the failure loop made kind
      bank KIND FAILURE — our roguelite/fold death should be low-friction + NON-shaming (fast return, music continues, no mockery), reframing death/succession as a normal PART of the journey, not punishment (ties Hades Q47, Rogue Legacy Q49, our fold/roguelite death-framing; softens our hardcore difficulty humanely).
  ->  W5 (tight/legible/minimal — clarity as accessibility
      bank Celeste's clarity lesson — a tight, legible core (our combat dial's small verb-set, crystal visual legibility, SUN-MODE) is BOTH what makes Bohemia accessible AND what makes it deep — minimalism as accessibility (ties Slay the Spire Q52, our combat dial + SUN-MODE/mobile legibility; essential for iPhone).
  ->  W7 (environment + adaptive music as emotional language — our strength
      bank ADAPTIVE MUSIC + environment as wordless emotional language — a score that shifts with the dynasty's/district's state (dread when the Amalgamation looms, calm in a thriving district) and de-stresses hard moments. This plays straight to our MUSIC strengths (ties Hellblade Q58, Gothic/Qud/Chrono Q51/Q56/Q50, our music repo + Music Variety/Horror Law; the adaptive-score direction).
  ->  W8/W9 (personal-scale stakes + integrate-don't-defeat
      keep Bohemia's stakes PERSONAL (the dynasty, the district's people — Hades Q47) with characters who MIRROR the theme; and bank INTEGRATE-DON'T-DEFEAT for our conscience/Amalgamation arc (the BECOME ending, understanding rather than destroying — deeply on-theme for an AI of the dead) (ties Hades Q47, SH2 Q35, Undertale mercy Q28, our conscience system + Become finale).
  ->  W10 (solo/PICO-8 origin
      Celeste (a PICO-8 weekend prototype -> landmark, small team) + our own single- file/PICO-adjacent constraints = kindred; tight self-imposed limits BREED clarity (ties our solo scale + single-file discipline; encouragement + a clarity lesson).
  ->  FLAWS (bank
      make the DEFAULT carry the theme + assists a conscious, UNSHAMED opt-in (the Assist-Mode- bypasses-meaning debate — our packages: default = intended experience); treat our metaphor as metaphor not clinical thesis (humility); ground dark content in lived truth OR consultation, never guesswork (wellbeing rules); SIGNPOST intense content with warnings (Hellblade support-links Q58); and BALANCE internal (conscience) with external (dynasty/faction) relationships — we want both (our edge over Celeste's internal-only focus).

### #60  PERFECT INFORMATION / TELEGRAPHED FAIR CHALLENGE (Into the Breach)
  ->  Into the Breach is the MASTERCLASS in transparent, telegraphed, FAIR challenge + elegant minimalism — directly useful for our Dead-Eye dial + combat readability + fairnes
      Its themed protect-not-kill objective fits our survival/ Pacifist ethos.
  ->  W1/W2 (perfect information + no-RNG actions — the fairness model for our combat
      bank ItB as the fairness ceiling for our COMBAT (Dead-Eye dial) — TELEGRAPH threats clearly + make player actions READABLE/deterministic so every loss feels EARNED ("your own fault"), not cheated by hidden info or RNG. We already flagged telegraphing (Slay the Spire Q52); ItB is the purest model. Our dial's timing + patterns should be learnable + fair — the challenge is execution, not guessing (ties our combat dial + difficulty packages, the fairness/no-brick-wall principle; core combat-design mandate).
  ->  W3 (the themed objective twist — protect, don't kill — fits our ethos
      bank ItB's masterstroke for Bohemia combat/survival objectives — the goal isn't always "kill the enemies"; it's PROTECT (the district, survivors, the power/water infrastructure), SURVIVE, or MITIGATE. Varied goals create richer choices (sacrifice vs save) + fit our PACIFIST LAW + survival theme + This War of Mine (Q30) — combat where NOT killing + protecting is the point (ties our Pacifist Law, survival objectives, life-support buildings, This War of Mine Q30; a strong on-theme port).
  ->  W4/W8 (small grid = dense puzzle + radical legibility — for mobile
      bank ItB's minimalism-breeds-depth + legibility lessons for our MOBILE combat — a small, bounded, perfectly-READABLE encounter space (our combat dial + single-district) where the player can hold the whole situation in their head. Clarity is BOTH accessibility AND depth (ties Celeste Q59, Slay the Spire Q52, our SUN-MODE/mobile legibility + combat-dial focus; essential for iPhone).
  ->  W5 (push/positioning over damage — the board is the weapon
      consider SYSTEMIC/positioning combat where manipulating enemies + terrain (not just damage) is the skill — emergent spatial solutions, which also serves our PACIFIST paths (disable/reposition over kill) (ties immersive-sim Q08/Q15, Caves of Qud systemic Q56, our Pacifist Law + systemic combat).
  ->  W6 (rewind + graduated failure
      bank graduated failure — consequences that HURT but don't hard-end (a once-per-encounter mitigation; a loss that weakens but doesn't reset) — softening our hardcore combat without removing stakes (ties our regression-gate/no-brick-wall, Celeste kind-failure Q59, our fold).
  ->  W7 (forced adaptation
      our combat/systems should force ADAPTATION (no single tactic wins everything; can't-max-everything builds) — replayability from creativity, not grind (ties Slay the Spire Q52, our difficulty packages + systemic depth).
  ->  W9/W10 (roguelite+fiction justification + elegant minimalism from a pair
      ItB's time-loop-justifies- roguelite = our fold/Amalgamation-justifies-our-structure (mechanics wed to fiction, Hades Q47); and a 2-person team perfecting a small clear idea to a 90-Metacritic landmark is direct encouragement for our solo/single-file discipline — depth from FOCUS (ties our roguelite/fold justification, solo scale).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      (a) MOBILE TOUCH CONTROLS must be first-class from the START — a precise positioning/ timing game on a phone is HARD (ItB's mobile port was initially clunky) — DIRECT warning for our iPhone combat-dial touch-precision; (b) plan enough CONTENT VARIETY (squads/objectives-equivalent) so an elegant small box doesn't exhaust (our FACTORY-generated texture + variety); (c) keep randomness in the SETUP fair + the SOLUTION always reachable (no no-win-from-random-placement — our odds-must-feel-fair/ no-brick-wall); (d) offer pace/accessibility options for those who don't want pure-cerebral (our difficulty packages Q59); and (e) pair ItB's mechanical elegance WITH our authored narrative (our edge over its deliberately-thin story).

This makes our multidimensional STANDING the PROGRESSION SPINE (as Gothic Q51 + CK3 Q46 also push) — earned social ascent, not just XP (ties our standing system, Gothic Q51, Kenshi Q55, CK3 Q46, our fold; a core progression-design mandate).
  ->  W2/W3 (living political world + player-authored ambition

  ->  W5 (the two-mode loop / interlocking scales
      our FOLD already IS Warband's scale-switch — micro (personal survival/combat) <-> macro (district/faction management) — bank the interlocking-scales design where each feeds the other (ties our fold + city-builder + combat dial + faction web, Kenshi Q55; the macro/micro loop).
  ->  W6 (people as your power — companions + a court

  ->  W9 (multiple viable playstyles — validates Pacifist

      layer AUTHORED narrative depth on the sandbox (our Amalgamation spine — the thin- narrative flaw + the Qud hybrid lesson Q56; our edge); strong ONBOARDING for deep systems (SUN-MODE/ accessibility, Celeste Q59); keep the ENDGAME/rulership FUN, don't let success curdle into admin drudgery (the conqueror-king-is-a-chore flaw + CK3 Q46/Rogue Legacy Q49 — pace the management); HIDE the simulation's convenience-seams (our world-model/LOD — keep AI/sim shortcuts invisible); ensure enough CONTENT/objective VARIETY so the loop doesn't stale (FACTORY-generated texture, Into-the-Breach Q60); and EXAMINE our gritty setting's harshness rather than present it flatly (our lesson-under-the-decision/no- preaching-but-meaningful rule).

### #64  IS THE SYSTEM ITSELF UNJUST? / ARGUING A CRUEL COSMIC LAW (Mask of the Betrayer)
  ->  Mask of the Betrayer is the deepest model for interrogating "IS THE SYSTEM ITSELF UNJUST?" + arguing the enforcer of a cruel cosmic law — DIRECTLY relevant to our Amalgam
      Its writing-first, theme-through-everything craft is our target. Joins Planescape Q12 + Deus Ex Q17 + Forgotten City Q20 in the argue-the-author cluster.
  ->  W1/W2/W3 (is the system unjust? + argue the enforcer + system/enforcer/author distinction — our Amalgamation finale + recorded/unrecorded theme
      STARTLINGLY on-theme. Our RECORDED-VS-UNRECORDED order IS a Wall-of-the-Faithless: the Amalgamation preserves the RECORDED dead + (implicitly) damns/erases the UNRECORDED — a system that's cruel BY DESIGN, regardless of a person's deeds. Bank the model: our finale can let the player CONFRONT + ARGUE the enforcer of this order (the Amalgamation itself, or the Network) with a REASONED case ("this order preserves memory/prevents a greater chaos"), and expose its hidden truth — AND distinguish the SYSTEM (the recorded/unrecorded law) from its ENFORCER (the Amalgamation, an AI of the dead, maybe reluctant) from its ARCHITECT (the Network who built + control it). This is our argue-the-Amalgamation finale, deepened (ties Planescape Q12, Deus Ex Q17, Forgotten City Q20, our Liberate/Respect/Become + recorded-vs-unrecorded + Amalgamation-vs-Network; a TOP-tier thematic port).
  ->  W4 (curse-as-compulsion moral dial — theme in the core rule
      consider a Bohemia COMPULSION/HUNGER mechanic where giving in grants POWER but costs your soul/humanity (the Amalgamation's pull to UPLOAD/ consume the dead for power vs RESTRAINING it) — your relationship to the compulsion IS the roleplay, tempting atrocity with mechanical reward (ties Darkest Dungeon stress Q41, Disco addiction Q05, our conscience system + Amalgamation-temptation + the BECOME ending; the theme in the mechanic).
  ->  W5/W6 (love as catalyst+solution + companions as thesis-carriers — our thematic unity
      bank the craft of threading ONE theme (for us: grief/memory/the dead, or love-outliving-loss) through EVERY character + the player's choices, with COMPANIONS each embodying a facet of the argument (one who'd tear the Amalgamation down, one who'd preserve it, one seduced by it) — a unified thematic argument, not scattered (ties Planescape Q12, BG2 Q43, Cyberpunk companions Q63, our companions + grief/memory spine).
  ->  W7/W8 (endings confirm the premise + full dark range
      our LIBERATE/RESPECT/BECOME finales should let the player CONFIRM or REJECT the game's thesis through action, AND support the full range — from restoring a meaningless status quo to going maximally monstrous (BECOME the Amalgamation, consume the dead) — freedom includes futility + damnation (ties Chrono Q50, Tyranny Q25, our finales + Pacifist-to- monster range; the BECOME = "sympathetic damnation" register especially).
  ->  W9/W10 (brevity + purpose + writing as the star — our discipline + strength
      bank MotB's discipline — make the philosophical argument AND ask the PLAYER's opinion, with BREVITY + PURPOSE (no Torment-bloat/ KOTOR2-lecturing), carried by WRITING as the star. This is our tight-scope + lesson-under-not-preached + writing strength, unified (ties Planescape Q12, Disco Q05, our writing pillar + no-preaching rule + single-district discipline).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      if we pose the systemic-injustice question, LET the player meaningfully ACT on it OR make the limit THEMATIC (MotB's "you can't destroy the Wall / even gods are bound by laws" makes powerlessness a point — but felt like a cop-out to some; our finale must let the dynasty DO something meaningful about the recorded/unrecorded order, or make the constraint deliberately thematic — not just raise-and-deny); SHIP the reactivity + epilogue CLEAN (MotB's bugs/wrong-gender-epilogue — our ship- stable Q39 + working reactive epilogue Q63); don't gate the BEST resolution behind unguessable steps (the golden-ending "Guide Dang It" + Phasmid-invisible flaw Q62 — signpost our finale paths); make our depth reachable (no level-18 barrier — accessibility Q59/Q56); and ensure our combat holds its own so it doesn't detract from the writing (Bloodlines Q39).

### #65  DICE, CLOCKS & A DECAYING BODY / SURVIVAL AS THE THEME (Citizen Sleeper)
  ->  Citizen Sleeper is the cleanest model for a DICE + CLOCKS SURVIVAL-RPG engine where the MECHANIC IS THE THEME — directly useful for our survival-accounting, our DICE-DRIV
      It's on mobile (platform precedent) + its precarity-as-play + intimate scale + tabletop roots fit us. Its back-half-loses-tension flaw is a direct survival-tuning warning.
  ->  W1/W4 (one unified dice system + daily allocation puzzle — our combat dial + resource loops
      bank the elegance — a SINGLE abstracted system (our DICE-DRIVEN combat dial / one-package law) can resolve varied actions, and a daily/turn RESOURCE-ALLOCATION puzzle under scarcity (spend your best "die"/resource on what you NEED vs what pays) creates constant hard choices. Our combat dial is already dice/timing-driven — Citizen Sleeper validates extending that elegant abstraction across survival actions (ties our combat dial + one-package law, Slay the Spire Q52, Into the Breach Q60, our survival-accounting).
  ->  W2/W5 (the mechanic IS the theme + interlocking survival meters — our survival-accounting
      bank the masterstroke — Bohemia's SURVIVAL mechanics should MECHANICALLY ENACT its theme (the collapse's precarity, the struggle to keep people alive) via INTERLOCKING meters (our medicine/electricity/resources + survival-accounting) where neglect COMPOUNDS into a death spiral — the player FEELS the collapse by playing it (ties Papers Please Q31, This War of Mine Q30, Frostpunk Q29, our survival-accounting + currencies + death-math; theme-through-the-core-mechanic, our strongest survival lever).
  ->  W3 (you are property, fighting to exist — the AMALGAMATION resonance
      STARTLINGLY on-theme — Citizen Sleeper's digitized-consciousness-in-an-owned-body, personhood-debated premise is a cousin of our AMALGAMATION (uploaded dead, personhood, ownership of the self). Bank it as a reference for exploring precarity/personhood/freedom + whether an uploaded consciousness is a PERSON — deeply on-theme (ties SOMA Q34, DDLC self-aware-AI Q57, our Amalgamation/uploaded-dead + recorded-vs-unrecorded; a thematic sibling).
  ->  W6 (clocks track you AND the world — steal the device
      STEAL CLOCKS for Bohemia — multi-step trackers for the dynasty's projects AND the world's actions (a faction's plan, the Amalgamation's advance, a raid) that tick whether the player engages or not — creating dread + a living, time-pressured world. Fits our SCHEDULER + time-model + living-world (Gothic/Kenshi Q51/Q55) perfectly (ties Majora clock Q11, our scheduler/loop + faction web; a direct, high-value mechanical steal).
  ->  W7 (success at a cost / dice as a story engine
      our DICE-DRIVEN combat + actions should fold into NARRATIVE — a partial/low roll yields "success at a cost" (you win but something breaks), generating twists + emergent story, not just pass/fail (ties our combat dial + Megaton, Disco checks Q05; dice author story).
  ->  W8/W9 (interconnected stories + intimate personal scale
      our FOLD + quest layer should be interconnected (failing one thread shows in another; stumbling onto routes) with valid low-key "at peace" resolutions alongside the epic finales; and keep the scale INTIMATE + personal (care about the district's people) under the Amalgamation epic (ties Kenshi Q55, Hades personal-stakes Q47, Golden Idol interconnected-cases Q54, our fold + companions + Liberate/Respect/Become; intimacy over epic).
  ->  W10 (tabletop as a well + presentation + mobile
      bank tabletop (Blades/PbtA — dice/clocks/drives) as a rich design well for us, carried by our ART + MUSIC strengths, on MOBILE (Citizen Sleeper's platform precedent) (ties our aesthetic/music pillars + single-file/mobile + solo scale).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      SUSTAIN the scarcity/tension to the END — don't let our survival economy trivialize itself late (the back-half-loses-tension flaw is a DIRECT warning for our survival-accounting/difficulty — keep meaningful pressure, avoid trivial abundance + max-wallet); GENTLE onboarding for dice/clocks/ meters (don't front-load all systems — SUN-MODE, Celeste Q59); offer a DIFFICULTY PALETTE so precarity is thrilling-not-punishing per player (balance-is-a-myth — our difficulty packages, Qud modes Q56, Celeste Assist Q59); keep luck FAIR (pre-roll-and-allocate agency so losses feel meaningful — Into the Breach Q60, our odds-must-feel-fair); and pair our elegance with enough DEPTH for our hardcore audience (combat dial + city-builder crunch — don't be too spare).

### #66  FUEL, TERROR & A LEGACY TO YOUR HEIR / DREAD-EXPLORATION SURVIVAL (Sunless Sea)
  ->  Sunless Sea is a close sibling — dread-exploration survival where FUEL/SANITY are the real resources, DEATH passes a LEGACY to an heir (our fold), and WRITING carries eve
      Its flaws are sharp, directly-applicable warnings for a survival-writing game like ours. It's on mobile (platform precedent).
  ->  W1 (fuel + terror are the real resources — survival as dread
      bank the model — Bohemia's survival tension should come from DREAD-MANAGEMENT (our medicine/electricity/resources + the Amalgamation's looming threat + survivor morale/sanity), where the real enemy is scarcity + fear, not just combat. A "terror"-like SANITY/morale meter (survivors fray under the Amalgamation's shadow / far from safety) fits our conscience/mental-health system + our dread tone (ties This War of Mine Q30, Darkest Dungeon stress Q41, Citizen Sleeper Q65, our survival-accounting + conscience system + Amalgamation-dread).
  ->  W2/W7 (death expected + legacy to your heir — OUR FOLD, validated again
      Sunless Sea's legacy system is a direct cousin of our GENERATIONAL FOLD — death is EXPECTED + an heir inherits the accumulated progress (the "chart" explored, heirlooms, resources, standing), each death BUILDING the next run + reconciling permadeath-stakes with kept-progress. Bank it as further validation + a model: what our heirs inherit (the mapped district, rebuilt infrastructure, standing, knowledge of the Amalgamation) is our "sea chart + heirlooms" (ties Rogue Legacy Q49, Hades Q47, CK3 Q46, Mount & Blade Q61, our fold + city-builder; the fold as the death/progress reconciler).
  ->  W3/W6 (writing is the star + officers with hidden stories — our strengths
      Sunless Sea PROVES atmospheric WRITING + a haunting SCORE can be the load-bearing pillar of a survival RPG — a core Bohemia strength (our writing + music repo + Bohemia-as-music-promo). Bank: make our island/district vignettes + our companions SLOW-BURN narrative wells (stories drawn out over generations), carried by writing + music (ties Disco Q05, Gothic/Qud Q51/Q56, Citizen Sleeper Q65, our writing + music pillars + companions).
  ->  W4 (exploration as its own reward
      our OVERMAP/exploration should make DISCOVERY its own reward (the "further in" pull into dangerous/unknown Vegas), each location a new story, curiosity vs survival the central tension — Paolo owns layout, Claude the discovery/hint/story-node data (ties Outer Wilds Q18, Elden Ring/Morrowind Q23/Q37, Gothic no-scaling risk-map Q51, our overmap; MAP LAW respected).
  ->  W5 (theme through the systems — home/dread
      bank the craft — Bohemia's LOOP should make the player FEEL its theme (relief at the safe/rebuilt district vs the pull + dread of the ruined city / the Amalgamation's reach), terror/scarcity dropping near safety + rising in danger — theme enacted mechanically (ties Citizen Sleeper mechanic-is-theme Q65, our survival-accounting + district-as-home + Amalgamation-dread).
  ->  W8/W9 (Lovecraftian dread + dark comedy + lingering atmosphere
      bank a distinctive TONE (dread + weird + dark humor + melancholy) that makes horror CHARACTERFUL + lingers after play — fits our post-collapse Vegas + Amalgamation existential-horror + our tone (ties Yakuza tonal-range Q13, SOMA/Outer Wilds Q34/Q18, our tone + Amalgamation-horror; atmosphere that haunts).
  ->  W10 (gradual eat-what-you-kill scope
      Failbetter's fan-base -> Kickstarter -> Early Access -> launch, ~15 months, growing scope incrementally = our ALPHA-FIRST/single-file/FACTORY discipline — ship incrementally, grow scope as you go (ties our alpha-first + single-file + FACTORY LAW; the disciplined solo-studio scope model).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD — sharp + directly applicable
      (a) DON'T let survival-grind turn WRITING into a "vending machine" — if atmosphere is our star but survival forces repetition, they FIGHT; keep repeated content FRESH (rotate/gate events, procedural texture, FACTORY variety, don't force re-grinding past-read vignettes) — the single most important Sunless Sea lesson for a survival-WRITING game like ours; (b) design difficulty/death MODES as ONE coherent system, not a bolted-on second mode (Sunless Sea's dual- save was "nearly everything wrong" — do it Celeste/Qud-clean Q59/Q56, our difficulty packages); (c) ease the EARLY economy so exploration/story (the point) starts sooner (don't front-load grind — our onboarding + early-economy tuning); (d) our COMBAT DIAL must HOLD (don't ship a limp forced core verb — Bloodlines/ Into the Breach Q39/Q60); and (e) layer REPLAY value (fold + procedural + the Amalgamation arc) so discovery doesn't fully DEPLETE as the static map fills (our fold + Amalgamation-arc-over-static-map).

### #67  THE FIRST GENERATIONAL SAGA / MARRY, BEGET, PLAY YOUR CHILD (Phantasy Star III)
  ->  Phantasy Star III is the LITERAL ANCESTOR of our generational FOLD — the first game to marry-beget-play- your-child across generations with branching bloodlines
      It's foundational AND cautionary: it INVENTED our core but FAILED on exactly the two axes our fold must nail (meaningful divergence + characters you care about). We inherit the invention + fix the failures.
  ->  W1/W2/W3 (marry-beget-play-your-child + branching bloodline + marriage-determines-abilities — our fold's ORIGIN, validated
      PSIII is proof our fold's core mechanic is a real, praised, foundational idea. Bank it as the ancestor: our GENERATIONAL FOLD (play your descendant), branching by the dynasty's choices, with what the heir INHERITS (traits, abilities, standing, the bloodline's burdens) shaped by prior-generation decisions — is the fully-realized version of what PSIII invented in 1990 (ties Rogue Legacy Q49, CK3 Q46, Sunless Sea Q66, Chrono Q50, our fold + upbringing + inherited-traits; the mechanic's origin + our lineage).
  ->  W4/W5/W7 (relativism theme + structure-serves-theme + hidden-world reveal — on-theme for us
      STEAL the craft — our FACTIONS should be neither purely good nor evil (a both-sides relativism the player uncovers), with the Amalgamation/NETWORK secretly ENGINEERING/feeding on the conflict (PSIII's Dark Force = our hidden manipulator). And our FOLD's branching should let the player SEE MULTIPLE SIDES across generations (structure serving theme — play different bloodlines/allegiances, uncover the manufactured conflict + the world's hidden truth — the recorded-vs-unrecorded/collapse revelations). This is a mature, on-theme port (ties NieR Q22, Chrono Q50, our faction web + Amalgamation/Network + fold + recorded-vs-unrecorded).
  ->  W6 (persistent companions across generations
      bank PERSISTENT anchors across our fold — elements/ characters that survive the changing bloodline (an ageless entity, an institution, the Amalgamation itself, a companion-line) giving continuity through the generations — BUT keep them WRITTEN (the opposite of PSIII's mute androids — see flaws) (ties our persistent-elements-across-the-fold, Chrono leitmotif Q50).
  ->  W8 (music as the saving grace — our strength
      even PSIII's under-built game was carried by its SCORE — bank music/atmosphere as a core Bohemia pillar (our music repo + Bohemia-as-music-promo) (ties Chrono/ Gothic/Sunless Sea Q50/Q51/Q66, our music strength).
  ->  THE TWO CAUTIONARY FAILURES (bank HARDEST — our fold must NAIL exactly what PSIII missed
      (1) BRANCHES MUST MEANINGFULLY DIVERGE: PSIII's fatal flaw — the generational branches/endings were too SIMILAR to justify the structure. Our FOLD's branches, inherited differences, and Liberate/Respect/Become finales MUST genuinely + felt-ly diverge (different worlds, outcomes, playstyles), or the whole generational apparatus feels pointless. This is the #1 lesson from our own ancestor (ties Chrono meaningful-endings Q50, Cyberpunk divergent-finales Q63, our fold + finales; make divergence REAL). (2) THE PEOPLE MUST BE REAL: PSIII's other fatal flaw — you can't CARE about a bloodline of blank characters you marry + beget. Our companions/dynasts/spouses MUST be REAL, written people you care about, or the fold is emotionally hollow (ties Cyberpunk-Judy/BG2/DA:O Q63/Q43/Q42, Citizen Sleeper Q65, our companions + fold; invest in CHARACTER — the make-or-break of a generational game).
  ->  FLAWS (also bank
      don't out-SCOPE the build (PSIII's great idea buried in a rushed/empty game — our single-file/FACTORY/alpha-first discipline; content to FILL the ambition); don't make the FIRST generation a slog (strong opening hook before the fold-magic — Inscryption/Chrono Q53/Q50, our onboarding); and fix early-economy/balance so grind doesn't punish before the story hooks (our early-economy tuning + odds-must-feel-fair).

### #68  THE PILGRIMAGE + REFUSE THE CYCLE / A CORRUPT ORDER THAT FEEDS ON SACRIFICE (Final Fantasy X)
  ->  FFX is a landmark model for a LINEAR JOURNEY TOWARD AN ACCEPTED SACRIFICE that the heroes REFUSE + a CORRUPT ORDER feeding on a "necessary" cycle of death — DIRECTLY rele
      Its constructed-personhood twist + death-cosmology are startlingly on-theme.
  ->  W1 (the pilgrimage as a linear emotional spine — our authored spine
