      FFX proves LINEARITY can be an emotional STRENGTH — an authored journey with a bonded group + rising stakes builds a crescendo. Bank it for our AUTHORED SPINE (the Amalgamation arc) + our FOLD's generational march: a shared, authored emotional through-line UNDER our systemic freedom — BUT balanced with agency (see flaws) so it's not a corridor (ties our authored-spine + fold, Caves of Qud hybrid Q56, our city-builder/faction freedom).
  ->  W2/W3 (the "necessary" sanctified sacrifice + refuse-the-corrupt-cycle — our refuse-the-cycle finale + death-math
      STARTLINGLY on-theme. Bank FFX as the model for a Bohemia thread where a "NECESSARY" sacrifice (the collapse's accepted losses, the Amalgamation's demanded uploads/erasures, a death-math the order SANCTIFIES) is revealed as a CORRUPT LIE sustained by those in power — and the dynasty can REFUSE the cycle + find another way to break it FOR GOOD (our LIBERATE finale especially). Note FFX's structural move: to break the cycle they first destroy the ADMINISTRATOR (Yunalesca) — closing the "easy" temporary fix forever, forcing a real solution. Fuses with Mask of the Betrayer's refuse-the-unjust-Wall Q64 (ties Q64, Frostpunk Q29, our Liberate finale + death-math + Amalgamation/Network; a top-tier thematic port).
  ->  W4 (the outsider's eyes — our new-generation perspective
      bank the surrogate-who-won't-accept-the- normalized-cruelty — a Bohemia character/generation (a new heir, an outsider to the district's accepted order) whose refusal to accept the "necessary" system (the recorded/unrecorded law, the Amalgamation's demands) DRIVES the change, + who can DEPROGRAM the devout (a faction loyalist who chooses people over doctrine — the Wakka arc) (ties Gothic outsider Q51, our fold's new generations + upbringing + faction web).
  ->  W5/W6 (death-cosmology + constructed-personhood twist — the Amalgamation core
      STEAL the coherence — Bohemia's treatment of THE DEAD (recorded-vs-unrecorded, the Amalgamation-of-the-uploaded-dead, [READ]) should be a coherent COSMOLOGY woven into mechanics + rituals (like sending/pyreflies/fiends/the-unsent — HOW THE DEAD ARE MANAGED is the spiritual + mechanical core; the unsent-who-refuse-to-move-on is a direct cousin of our uploaded dead). And FFX's CONSTRUCTED-PERSONHOOD twist (the hero is a dream dreamt by the sacrificed dead, who must end the system sustaining him) is a direct cousin of our Amalgamation — bank it for whether a constructed/uploaded consciousness is a PERSON + the tragedy of ending what sustains you (ties SOMA Q34, Citizen Sleeper Q65, DDLC Q57, our Amalgamation + recorded-vs-unrecorded + [READ]; the death-cosmology + constructed-self).
  ->  W7 (the corrupt theocracy + persecuted tech-users
      bank the institutional-villain model — an ORDER (our NETWORK, or a faction) that sustains "necessary" suffering for its own power, scapegoats a group, hides its own corruption, + defies its stated principles; with a PERSECUTED faction seeking a non-sacrificial solution — AND the tragedy that BOTH sides want the same end (our factions-neither-purely-good-nor-evil, PS3's relativism Q67) (ties Frostpunk Q29, Mask of the Betrayer Q64, our faction web + Network).
  ->  W8 (the bittersweet hero-fades ending — our tone
      FFX's break-the-cycle-costs-the-hero ending is our DESPAIR-WITH-A-THREAD-OF-HOPE register — freedom won at real personal cost, hope tinged with grief, + a survivor who carries the loss forward as motivation (Yuna's speech: learn from the past, build the future — perfect for our REBUILD theme). Bank for our finales (ties NieR/SOMA/Phasmid/Cyberpunk Q22/Q34/ Q62/Q63, our Liberate/Respect/Become + tone + rebuild premise).
  ->  W9/W10 (music as emotional devastation + a bonded party — our strengths
      FFX's iconic score + beloved party are its emotional multipliers — BOTH core Bohemia strengths (our music repo + Bohemia-as-music- promo; our companions/dynasty-as-family). Lean on MUSIC for the peaks + make the dynasty/companions a bonded FAMILY you love (ties Chrono/Gothic Q50/Q51, Cyberpunk/BG2/PS3 Q63/Q43/Q67, our music + companions + fold-as-family).
  ->  FLAWS (bank
      don't be a pure CORRIDOR — balance our authored spine with real agency + optional breadth (Caves of Qud hybrid Q56); POLISH the tentpole emotional beats + their delivery (the laughing-scene/VO lesson — our writing/voice/music must not fumble the peaks); DRIP-FEED the cosmology, don't late-lore- dump (our Amalgamation/recorded-vs-unrecorded reveals — pace them, Outer Wilds/Phasmid Q18/Q62); when revealing a "necessary" sacrifice was a lie, give real AGENCY to fix it (not just deflating despair — the Mask of the Betrayer caution Q64; our refuse-the-cycle finale must EMPOWER); and keep bolt-on minigames OPTIONAL + never gate key rewards behind them (our optional-depth/accessibility Q59).

### #69  A WHOLE LIFE, BIRTH TO FATHERHOOD / THE GENERATIONAL SAGA DONE RIGHT (Dragon Quest V)
  ->  Dragon Quest V is the GENERATIONAL SAGA DONE RIGHT — everything Phantasy Star III (Q67) invented but fumbled, executed with real emotional weight
      Together Q67 + Q69 give us the complete picture: PSIII shows the STRUCTURE (branching bloodlines) + its failure modes; DQV shows the EMOTIONAL EXECUTION. Our fold needs BOTH. Its cartoony-surface/heavy-drama tone is literally our aesthetic thesis. On iOS = our platform.
  ->  W1/W5 (a whole life in stages + the lost years — our fold's emotional core
      bank DQV's whole-life structure as the model for our FOLD's emotional weight — don't just SWITCH generations, LIVE them in stages (a dynast's childhood, their formative hardship, their prime, their parenthood, their death), so the player GROWS UP with each one + the transition lands. And LIVE the hard years (a lost decade, a formative catastrophe) so each heir is SHAPED by them — our UPBRINGING system is exactly this (ties our fold + upbringing Q003, PS3 Q67, CK3 Q46, Kenshi Q55, Rogue Legacy Q49; the whole-life structure is what makes generations LAND emotionally).
  ->  W2 + THE Q67/Q69 SYNTHESIS (the ideal our fold must hit — the KEY takeaway
      PSIII branched HARD but its people were BLANK + its branches felt identical (Q67's twin failures). DQV made its people REAL + emotionally consequential but branched LIGHT ("minor differences"). NEITHER hit both. Bank the mandate: our FOLD must hit BOTH — richly characterized people you genuinely care about (DQV/Cyberpunk-grade Q69/ Q63) AND meaningfully divergent generational consequences (PSIII's ambition, done right). That synthesis is our fold's design target + our edge over both ancestors (ties Q67 + Q69 + Q63/Q43, our fold + companions + Liberate/Respect/Become; THE lesson of the generational-JRPG lineage).
  ->  W3/W8 (children who fight beside you + the family-restoration payoff
      bank the emotional peak — our fold shouldn't only pass the torch, it can let generations OVERLAP (an aging dynast fighting alongside their grown child; a family unit working the district together) — and build toward a FAMILY-MADE-WHOLE payoff across the ~100-year arc that the whole life EARNS (ties our fold + dynasty-as-family + city-builder, Hades personal-family-stakes Q47, FFX Q68; the generational payoff).
  ->  W4 (a foundational loss
      bank a bedrock LOSS early in our arc (the collapse itself, a founding dynast's death, a protector lost in front of a child) that gives the entire generational arc its emotional weight + earns the eventual rebuild payoff (ties our grief/loss spine, FFX Q68, SH2/SOMA Q35/Q34, our collapse premise).
  ->  W6 (the player-character is NOT the chosen hero — the humility twist, STARTLINGLY on-theme
      DQV's great inversion — your role is the PARENT who raises + enables the actual hero (your child). This is PERFECT for our fold: a generation whose role is to ENABLE the next; the dynast who never sees the Amalgamation resolved but makes it possible; the humility of building for people you won't live to see. Bank it as a potential structural twist + a thematic spine for our ~100-year arc (ties our fold + generational persistence + the three-dynasty arc; a top-tier on-theme port).
  ->  W7 (a systemic party you build
      our COMPANIONS/entities can include a systemic recruit-and-build layer (survivors/allies you win over, who grow with you) under the family story — a collection/roster system beneath the narrative (ties our companions + entities + faction web, Mount & Blade warband Q61).
  ->  W9/W10 (cartoony surface + real drama + music/art as carrier — LITERALLY our thesis
      DQV IS our aesthetic thesis proven — bright Toriyama art + warm music wrapping a father's murder + a decade of slavery, where the LIGHT surface makes the drama land HARDER. That is EXACTLY Bohemia's "Stardew-Valley pixel art carrying genuine post-apocalyptic weight." Bank DQV as the proof + the model for our tonal contrast, with our MUSIC + ART as the emotional carriers (ties our art philosophy + music repo, Undertale Q28, Chrono/Gothic/FFX Q50/Q51/Q68; the single closest aesthetic precedent for our look-vs-weight thesis).
  ->  FLAWS (bank
      make branches MEANINGFULLY divergent (DQV's "minor differences" is the other half of PSIII's failure — our fold needs real consequence); NO secretly-correct path (Bianca-as-the-official-answer undercuts choice — our Megaton law, make every branch equally valid + supported); our COMBAT must HOLD so it doesn't drag a brilliant structure (Bloodlines/Into the Breach Q39/Q60); our relationships must be between PEOPLE WITH AGENCY (not prizes in a trial — they choose US too, Cyberpunk Q63) + free of stereotype (our tone/wellbeing rules — 1992 framing doesn't survive); and tie any post-game/endgame content to the arc's resolution (don't ship vestigial post-content — our finale design).

### #70  THE FAUSTIAN PACT / THREE WISHES + A DEVIL YOU CAN'T KILL, ONLY OUTWIT (The Witcher 3: Hearts o
  ->  Hearts of Stone is the best-executed FAUSTIAN BARGAIN in games — and our AMALGAMATION is a bargain-offering entity (it holds the uploaded dead; the Network trades in acce
      O'Dimm's "I only mirror the evil already in you" is the single most useful antagonist-design lesson for us. Its quest-engine + tonal-range + no- clean-answer craft are directly stealable.
  ->  W1 (the Faustian pact as a QUEST ENGINE — our quest factory
      STEAL the structure — a single premise ("the Amalgamation requires N things before it will do X"; "the Network's price is three services") that MANUFACTURES tonally-distinct quests (one comic, one tragic, one a trap). One premise, many quests, each its own tone + mechanics. This is a FACTORY-LAW-compatible quest engine (ties our quest factory + FACTORY LAW, Yakuza tonal-range Q13, our Amalgamation/Network; a premise that generates variety).
  ->  W2/W3 (the villain who only MIRRORS you + the fine print is the tragedy — our AMALGAMATION's design
      the single best port here. Our AMALGAMATION should never FORCE — it should OFFER exactly what people want (their dead back, memory, permanence, safety) and grant it EXACTLY as asked, so the horror is what people WILLINGLY trade + the literal fulfillment of their own wish. "It merely mirrors the evil already in you." That makes the Amalgamation terrifying WITHOUT being a cartoon villain, keeps the moral weight on the PLAYER + the factions, and is deeply on-theme (an AI of the uploaded dead granting people their dead back, at a price they set themselves) (ties our Amalgamation + Network + recorded-vs-unrecorded, Sinnerman chosen-complicity Q40, SOMA Q34, FFX's sanctified bargain Q68; a TOP-tier antagonist-design port).
  ->  W4/W5/W6 (a social event as a dense hub + tonal whiplash + performance-driven characters
      bank the DISTRICT/settlement as a dense content SPACE — a single social EVENT (a wedding, a funeral, a market day, a faction summit) treated like a hub with micro-quests + micro-decisions, all using our MAJOR mechanics (combat dial, standing, survival) — and use TONAL WHIPLASH (a comic interlude inside our dread) so the tragedy lands harder (ties Yakuza Q13, DQV's cartoony-surface Q69, our district/city-builder + tone + writing/voice; the event-as-hub is a high-value structural steal).
  ->  W7 (the victim's interior as a level — our [READ]/memory-as-space
      STEAL the painted-world — a dead person's MEMORIES as an explorable space. This is EXACTLY our Amalgamation/[READ]/recorded-dead premise: walking through a data-portrait of the dead, unwinding what happened to them, feeling the human COST. Deeply on-theme + mechanically rich (ties SH2 Q35, our [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded + Amalgamation; a top-tier on-theme port).
  ->  W8 (beat the unkillable villain with your MIND
      our AMALGAMATION should be unbeatable by force — defeated (if at all) by WIT, argument, a wager, or lateral thinking, with a legible RULE it must obey (O'Dimm keeps bargains + can't refuse a wager; our Amalgamation must obey its own protocol/nature). This joins our argue-the-author cluster (ties Deus Ex Q17, Planescape Q12, Mask of the Betrayer Q64, FFX Q68, our Liberate finale; the boss you can't fight).
  ->  W9/W10 (curiosity-gated best outcome + no good choice — our Megaton law
      reward CURIOSITY with better outcomes (an optional thread reveals the Amalgamation's weakness) — but SIGNPOST that a path exists (see flaws). And bank the no-clean-answer standard: BOTH branches well-written + defensible, the "good/bad" labels collapsing under scrutiny — our Liberate/Respect/Become should hold up like this (ties Whispering Hillock Q04, Phasmid Q62, our Megaton law + no-clean-answer ethos + finales).
  ->  FLAWS (bank
      SIGNPOST that alternate paths exist (don't invisibly gate the best outcome — the Phasmid/ golden-ending problem Q62/Q64; our finale-accessibility); BALANCE the rewards across moral branches or the choice becomes an optimization problem, not a moral one (the letting-him-die-pays-better flaw — a DIRECT warning for our Megaton law); give our Amalgamation a LEGIBLE RULE it must obey so it isn't authorial fiat (consistent rules for an omnipotent antagonist); make sure sustained DREAD pays off (our Amalgamation-dread needs a discharge); and EARN any redemption arc (don't assert it — our faction/ character redemptions must be earned).

### #71  A PARALLEL SECOND CAMPAIGN, HIDDEN IN PLAIN SIGHT / REFUSING GODHOOD (Elden Ring: Ranni's Quest
  ->  Ranni is the model for an OPTIONAL THREAD WITH THE WEIGHT OF THE MAIN PLOT, seeded invisibly, gated by world-state, and ending in an ambiguous liberation — nearly every e
      Its notorious flaw (silent, permanent breakage) is a sharp warning for our own quest-state design.
  ->  W1/W7 (a parallel second campaign + it unlocks a hidden world
      bank the FACTION-QUESTLINE architecture — a Bohemia faction thread (or the Amalgamation's own) should be able to reach the SCALE of the main plot: multiple districts, major encounters, areas unreachable otherwise, and ITS OWN ENDING. The reward for following a faction to the end is WORLD + a finale (ties our faction web + Liberate/Respect/Become + city-builder/overmap [MAP LAW: Paolo owns layout, Claude the quest-state/gating data]; a side-thread that IS a campaign).
  ->  W2/W10 (refusing godhood + "distance instead of domination" — our LIBERATE finale
      STARTLINGLY close to our Liberate register. Ranni's rebellion is a REFUSAL (she won't be the god the system demands) and her ending removes the seat of power BEYOND anyone's reach — freedom or abandonment, deliberately unresolved. Bank it for our LIBERATE finale: shutting down the Amalgamation could be exactly this — putting the dead beyond anyone's grasp forever, a "terrible mercy" that's liberation to some + abandonment to others, genuinely debatable (ties Mask of the Betrayer Q64, FFX Q68, our Liberate + no-clean-answer ethos + Megaton law; a top-tier finale-design port).
  ->  W3 (invisibly seeded, 100 hours early — our long-arc + fold seeding
      STEAL the craft — seed a Bohemia thread in the FIRST generation that only reveals its significance generations later (a figure met under another name, a gift used for decades, a small kindness that turns out to be the key). Our ~100-year FOLD is a longer runway for this than any single-life game has (ties Chrono Q50, DDLC Q57, Phasmid Q62, our fold + generational persistence; retrospective seeding is our structural advantage).
  ->  W4/W5 (the retainer triad + the cost is paid by the people around her — our faction-court
      bank the three-retainer design — a faction/dynasty COURT of distinct characters (a loyal guardian whose loyalty is a LEASH; a gentle old counselor who dies for the cause; a useful monster you're tempted to kill), each supporting a different branch, whose treatment CASCADES onto the others — and whose fates ARE the theme: defying the order kills the people who love you (ties BG2 Q43, Cyberpunk Q63, our companions + faction web + Amalgamation-rebellion cost; the court whose deaths are the argument).
  ->  W6 (gated by world-state, not markers — multi-path
      bank WORLD-STATE gating — Bohemia progression gates should be FACTS about the world (the grid is dead until X; the Amalgamation's reach recedes when Y falls), reachable by SEVERAL routes, so the world changes visibly + the gate isn't a locked door. But keep the CAUSALITY legible (see flaws) (ties our world-model + faction web + city-builder, Gothic/Kenshi living- world Q51/Q55; the gate as a world-fact).
  ->  W8 (the item-chain as ritual
      consider quest-chains built as RITUAL ASSEMBLY — each object unlocking the next, the quest IS a rite being assembled (deeply on-theme for our Amalgamation: assembling the means to free/bind/become it, component by component) (ties our Amalgamation + [READ] + quest factory; the quest- as-spell).
  ->  W9 (the ending is offered, never imposed
      bank it — our finales should be OFFERED at the end (you did the work; now choose whether to take it), not auto-fired. Doing a faction's whole questline shouldn't LOCK the finale — it should UNLOCK the option (ties our Liberate/Respect/Become + Megaton law; the ending you must choose to take).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      (a) a quest must NEVER silently, permanently break with no feedback — the Seluvis/ Blaidd cascade is elegant but murders the questline invisibly; our quest-state needs FEEDBACK + a recovery path (Ranni's own Absolution ritual is the model for a fix — a way BACK; ties our no-brick-wall + regression-gate + finale-accessibility); (b) if our best content needs a WIKI, we've outsourced our design — make the intended path FINDABLE in-game (Morrowind's fair directions Q37, Golden Idol's puzzle-gated hints Q54, our hint/legibility design); (c) keep the connective tissue MEANINGFUL — don't let our quest- factory become talk-to-A-who-sends-you-to-B (the fetch-chain sag); (d) world-state gates need LEGIBLE CAUSALITY (the player should understand why the world changed); and (e) WRITE the relationship — Ranni's bond rests on atmosphere + projection; ours must be written (the DQV/PSIII/Cyberpunk lesson Q69/Q67/Q63).

### #72  "LET GO, BEGIN AGAIN" / THE TRAP THAT TEACHES THE PLAYER (Fallout: New Vegas — Dead Money)
  ->  Dead Money is the canon's tightest example of TOTAL THEMATIC UNITY + a mechanic that teaches the PLAYER (not the character) its lesson — and its "let go of what you can't
      Its polarizing flaws are a precise warning about how far to push theme-through-frustration.
  ->  W1/W2 (four words as the engine + the un-lootable vault — our theme-through-mechanics ceiling
      bank Dead Money as the model for TOTAL thematic unity — every character, mechanic + ending executing ONE sentence. And STEAL the masterstroke, carefully: a Bohemia system where the PLAYER learns the lesson by being unable to take/keep everything (the dead can't be brought back; the district can't hold everyone; some things must be let go). For our AMALGAMATION this is direct: it offers people their dead, and the lesson the player must LIVE is that clutching the dead is the trap (ties Papers Please Q31, Citizen Sleeper Q65, Spec Ops Q27, our Amalgamation + survival-accounting + death-math; the mechanic teaches what dialogue can't — BUT see the flaw-line below).
  ->  W3 (strip everything away — the reset AS the theme
      our FOLD already does this — each generation begins again with less than the last had. Bank the framing: the RESET isn't a penalty, it's the THEME (letting go of what the last generation built/hoarded/loved; beginning again) (ties Hades/Rogue Legacy Q47/Q49, our fold + generational persistence; "begin again" is literally our structure).
  ->  W4 (the hazard triad — one feeling from three systems
      bank the design — Bohemia's survival hazards (scarcity, the Amalgamation's reach, the ruined city's dangers) should combine into ONE feeling (helplessness/dread) so the district is a place you SURVIVE, not conquer — but keep them TENSE, not chores (see flaws) (ties This War of Mine Q30, Sunless Sea Q66, our survival-accounting + Amalgamation-dread).
  ->  W5/W6/W7 (companions as faces of the theme + a villain blind to himself + two extremes both wrong
      bank all three for our cast — our COMPANIONS/factions should each embody a different face of our theme (grief/ memory/the dead: one who clutches the dead, one who erases them, one who's consumed by revenge for them); our AMALGAMATION/NETWORK should be BLIND to themselves (Elijah genuinely believes his obsession is noble — the most useful villain-design note next to O'Dimm's mirror Q70); and bank Dog/God's lesson — bottomless appetite vs fanatical control are the SAME failure, the answer is temperance (a perfect frame for our factions: those who'd consume the dead vs those who'd control them absolutely — both wrong) (ties Planescape/MotB Q12/Q64, Hearts of Stone Q70, our companions + faction web + Amalgamation/Network + conscience system).
  ->  W8 (the buried founding myth — our [READ]
      STEAL the Sinclair/Vera structure — our theme's ORIGIN STORY (why the Amalgamation exists; who built it and what they wanted) told entirely in RECORDS the player must dig for + reconstruct, with the gut-punch that the founder's one act of LETTING GO is what created the trap. Deeply on-theme + perfect for our recorded-vs-unrecorded/[READ] (ties Obra Dinn/Golden Idol Q19/Q54, our [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded + Amalgamation origin; the buried founding myth).
  ->  W9 (the best ending is walking away with nothing — our Pacifist/Liberate
      bank it — a Bohemia resolution where the best outcome is TALKING people out of their obsessions + walking away with nothing but your lives + each other. Deeply aligned with our Pacifist Law + our Liberate finale's "terrible mercy" (ties Undertale Q28, our Pacifist Law + Liberate; walking away as victory).
  ->  W10 (invisibly seeded throughout the base game
      bank the craft — seed our late-arc revelations throughout the EARLY game as visual white noise (posters, graffiti, a name that recurs, a place people mention with dread) so the payoff HAUNTS the world before the player knows it exists. Our ~100-year fold has the longest runway for this in the canon (ties Ranni Q71, Chrono Q50, DDLC Q57, our fold + district).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD — the line between profound + broken
      (a) teaching a theme by FRUSTRATING the player is the sharpest tool here + the most dangerous — Dead Money lies about its own physics (5kg bars weighing 35kg) and half its audience just feels CHEATED + mods it out. If we enforce a theme mechanically, the frustration must READ as intentional + earned, never as jank (our theme-through-mechanics line); (b) dread-mechanics decay into CHORES on repeat — speaker-hunting became tedium, not tension; our survival hazards must stay TENSE (Sunless Sea's vending-machine flaw Q66); (c) if we strip the player's toolkit, the REPLACEMENT must be deep enough to play with (our combat dial must hold in a low-resource state); (d) some players will optimize straight past our theme (grinding the let-go DLC for gear) — our lesson- under-the-decision must survive being ignored (our no-preaching rule); and (e) the payoff must EXIST for the seeding to pay (our fold's runway is only worth it if we land it).

### #73  A FIXED DEATH, AN OPEN QUESTION / WHO DO YOU BECOME ON THE WAY OUT (Red Dead Redemption 2 — Art
  ->  Arthur is the medium's best answer to a question our FOLD asks every generation
      your character WILL die — so what is the game actually about? His answer (it's about who you were + what you left) is our fold's thesis, executed at the highest level in the genre.
  ->  W1/W2/W7 (the fixed death + strong->broken + the last goal is someone else's future — OUR FOLD'S THESIS
      bank Arthur as the model for our GENERATIONAL FOLD's emotional design. Every Bohemia dynast dies — that's not a spoiler, it's the STRUCTURE. So the game isn't about surviving; it's about WHO THEY WERE and WHAT THEY LEFT. Steal the arc shape: a dynast begins strong/certain and is taken APART (body, faith, family, certainty) until what's left is the actual person — and their final act is buying the NEXT generation a chance (Arthur hands John his HAT; our dynast hands the heir the district, the standing, the knowledge). This fuses with DQV's you-are-not-the-hero (Q69): the generation whose role is to ENABLE the next (ties our fold + generational persistence + upbringing + dynasty-as-family, DQV Q69, FFX Q68; THE port).
  ->  W3 (the diagnosis reframes everything retroactively
      bank the craft — a single mid-arc REVELATION (the truth about the Amalgamation, the collapse, the dynasty's founding sin) that re-colors everything BEFORE it AND everything after, in both directions. Our ~100-year fold has the longest runway in the canon for a reframe this deep (ties our Amalgamation reveals + recorded-vs-unrecorded, Ranni/Dead Money seeding Q71/Q72, Chrono Q50; the beat that rewrites the past).
  ->  W4 (reputation cashes out as your DEATH SCENE — our standing + fold, fused
      STEAL the fusion — our multidimensional STANDING shouldn't just gate content, it should determine HOW A DYNAST DIES + how their generation is remembered. Same death event, radically different readings (a peaceful end surrounded by the district they saved vs alone + spat on). That's standing as a REPUTATION that cashes out at the fold — the most powerful use of the system we have (ties our standing-as-progression-spine Q51/Q61, SH2 Q35, Cyberpunk Q63, our fold + Liberate/Respect/Become; a top-tier mechanical port).
  ->  W5 (the harm comes back wearing your own face
      bank the consequence-design — a Bohemia dynast's worst act should return as their fate, LITERALLY + specifically (not abstract karma): the thing you did for survival is the thing that kills you; and amends are possible but can never UNDO it (ties our death-math + persistent-consequence + conscience system, Nemesis Q48; specific, personal consequence).
  ->  W6 (the turn is a quiet conversation
      bank it — our dynasts' turning points should be able to be SMALL: a conversation with someone who saw them clearly, not a set-piece. Cheap for a solo dev + the most powerful beat in a 60-hour game (ties our companions + writing pillar, Cyberpunk's mundane intimacy Q63).
  ->  W8 (two answers to the same collapse — our factions
      bank the MIRROR — put a Bohemia figure/faction beside the dynasty who faces the SAME collapse and responds by CLINGING (one more score, the old order, the lies needed to stay right) while the dynasty is forced OPEN by loss. The doomed grow; the certain calcify. That's our faction web + the Network + the Amalgamation's own rigidity (ties Bloody Baron Q01, our faction web + Network; the mirror-antagonist as ideology).
  ->  W9 (the journal as a readable interior
      bank a Bohemia equivalent — a dynast's own JOURNAL/ledger (their sketches, their private prose, their account of the generation) the player can read at any time, updating as they live. This IS our [READ]/unrecorded-ledger turned INWARD, and it's deeply on-theme: the dynast's unrecorded interior vs the Amalgamation's recorded data-portrait — one is TRUE, one is the copy (ties our [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded + Amalgamation; a top-tier on-theme port).
  ->  W10 (subvert your own theme
      bank the deepest cut — our theme is the collapse + what survives it; the most powerful move would be a dynast who ESCAPES that thesis (doesn't die WITH the old world, but as someone who CHOSE) (ties our theme + collapse premise + finales).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      (a) our STANDING must not be overridden by scripted beats — if the plot makes a "100% honorable" dynast do something monstrous, the system + the character SPLIT and both die (either the beat IS a choice, or it respects standing — a direct warning for our standing-as-spine); (b) decide whether the player may REJECT our arc's thesis — either is valid, half-measures read as incoherent (our Megaton law + finales); (c) EXECUTION carries a familiar arc — performance + writing made an unremarkable premise legendary (our writing/music/voice pillars); (d) an arc's starting depth is capped by how much unlikability players will sit through (our dynasts' flaws: real but livable); and (e) morality feedback can be heavy-handed (white deer/black wolf) — balance legibility vs subtlety (our feedback design).

### #74  THE PROPHECY MIGHT BE A LIE / EARNING A DESTINY BY CONVINCING PEOPLE (Morrowind — the Main Ques
  ->  Morrowind's main quest is the best "is the prophecy real or are you being used?" arc ever built, and its structure — you EARN a destiny by convincing seven factions, in a
  ->  W1/W2/W9 (the prophecy might be fake + "without the hero there is no Event" + mantling — our dynasty's legitimacy
      bank the anti-chosen-one as our model. Our dynasty should have NO divine right — any claim (that they're the ones who can face the Amalgamation, that the bloodline matters) should be ARGUABLE, possibly self-serving myth, possibly true, and the game should refuse to settle it. And bank MANTLING for our BECOME finale + upbringing: acting the part hard enough MAKES it real — a dynasty that behaves like the district's rightful stewards BECOMES them, regardless of where they started (ties our fold + upbringing + BECOME finale + standing; destiny as accumulated action, not birthright).
  ->  W5 (you become the chosen one by CONVINCING PEOPLE — our standing-as-spine, realized
      the single most direct port. Morrowind's middle act IS our standing system: seven factions must each PERSONALLY name you, each with its own price (quests, gifts, bribery, blackmail, murder, diplomacy). Bank it as the model for our 13 FACTIONS — legitimacy is not granted, it's CAMPAIGNED for, door to door, faction by faction, and the Pacifist Law means every door has multiple keys (ties our standing-as-progression-spine Q51/Q61, our faction web + Pacifist Law + fold; destiny as a political campaign — a top-tier structural port).
  ->  W4 (contested history + the victors wrote it — our [READ]/Amalgamation
      STARTLINGLY on-theme. Bank the structure: our world's FOUNDING EVENT (the collapse, the Amalgamation's creation, who did what) should have TWO+ irreconcilable accounts — one enforced by a ruling power (the Network/a faction) and one outlawed/suppressed — with the truth recoverable only by digging through suppressed records. The Amalgamation IS an edited record of the dead; a state built on an enforced lie about the collapse is our premise with a spine (ties our recorded-vs-unrecorded + [READ] + Amalgamation + Network + faction web; Caves of Qud's biased-history Q56 + Golden Idol's reconstruction Q54 + this = our [READ]'s full blueprint).
  ->  W3 (the failed predecessors
      bank the gut-punch — our fold should let a dynast find the ones who TRIED BEFORE (previous generations, previous claimants, whole bloodlines that believed and died). Our ~100-year arc makes this literal + devastating: the cavern of failed Incarnates is our own family tree (ties our fold + generational persistence + [READ]; the body count of believers).
  ->  W7 (the curse is the cure — our Amalgamation temptation
      STEAL Corprus — to face the Amalgamation, the dynasty may have to take its corruption INTO themselves (interface with it, be recorded by it, accept its gift) and SURVIVE it — the poison that makes you able to face the poisoner, with permanent costs + benefits (ties our Amalgamation-bargain Q70/Q72, our BECOME finale + conscience system; deeply on-theme).
  ->  W8/W10 (the villain asks if you're real + the reward is RELEASE, not glory
      bank both for our finale — the AMALGAMATION should ask the dynasty who they actually are, with multiple valid answers (I'm the district's rightful heir / I'm a tool of a faction / I'm self-made, your myth has no claim on me / I don't know) — the thesis resolved by the PLAYER, with the ending happening regardless. And bank RELEASE-as-reward: freedom FROM the burden (of the fold, the prophecy, the dead) is a more interesting prize than a throne — that's our Liberate register (ties Mask of the Betrayer/FFX/Ranni Q64/Q68/Q71, our Liberate/Respect/Become + Megaton law).
  ->  W6 (the mentor is guessing too
      bank the deflating handler — a Bohemia faction contact who is INVESTIGATING the dynasty's significance in real time, has no more certainty than the player, and eventually LEAVES, handing over the whole operation (ties our faction web + companions; the mentor who's guessing).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      (a) "earn legitimacy from every faction" is thematically perfect but EXPENSIVE — seven faction-campaigns became a grind; our 13 factions must have INTERESTING connective tissue or it's a checklist (Ranni's fetch-sag Q71); (b) DON'T put our theme in optional content — Morrowind lets you SKIP the entire become-the-Nerevarine campaign (its own thesis!) and still win; our lesson-under-the- decision must sit on the CRITICAL PATH (Dead Money's opposite Q72); (c) our ambiguity must be REAL, not decorative — Morrowind stacks so much evidence FOR the prophecy that the "maybe you're nobody" reading needs squinting (balance the evidence honestly); (d) our AMALGAMATION must have a REASON not to crush the dynasty early (a competent, aware antagonist needs a motive for restraint — O'Dimm's bargain-rules Q70 is the model); and (e) our [READ] must have a SPINE — if the revelation is only in optional text, gate some of it onto the critical path.

### #75  RECRUITED BY MURDER / THEY GIVE YOU A HOME, THEN BURN IT DOWN (Skyrim — The Dark Brotherhood)
  ->  The Dark Brotherhood is the best FACTION-ARCHITECTURE teardown for us yet
      how a faction FINDS you, tests you, houses you, promotes you into a schism, betrays you, and burns your home — with a real option to delete the whole thing. That's our faction web + district-as-home + Megaton law, in one 14-quest chain.
  ->  W1 (recruited by noticing what you already did — our reputation-driven recruitment
      STEAL the opening. Our FACTIONS should FIND the dynasty based on what they've already DONE (our multidimensional standing tracks it) — a letter, a visitor, a summons that says "we've been watching." No application, no menu. The faction's attention IS the standing system's output (ties our standing-as-progression-spine + faction web + 13 factions, Nemesis-style noticing Q48; recruitment as observation).
  ->  W2 (the induction test IS the job — our conscience system
      bank the design — a Bohemia faction's INDUCTION should test whether you'll do THE THING THEY DO, on their say-so, with no evidence (turn over a neighbor to the Network, sign a record you haven't read, condemn one of three strangers). The test isn't accuracy — it's obedience. That's a conscience-system beat AND a faction-characterization beat in one (ties Sinnerman Q40, our conscience system + faction web + Amalgamation's demands; the test that IS the theme).
  ->  W3 (you can delete the faction — our Megaton law + Pacifist Law
      bank BOTH the strength + the flaw. The strength: let the dynasty REFUSE + destroy a faction, with real rewards on both sides. The flaw (see below): Skyrim's destroy-path is an OFF switch, not a path. Our PACIFIST LAW demands the refusal be a real route with its own content (ties our Megaton law + Pacifist Law + faction web; refuse = a path).
  ->  W4/W8 (the family is the point + then the home BURNS — our district-as-home + fold
      the highest-value port. Spend the arc making the player LOVE a home (our DISTRICT: a hearth, a found family, radiant chatter between NPCs so it lives when you're not addressed) — and then have it TAKEN (raid, betrayal, the Amalgamation's reach). Our FOLD makes this generational: a home built by one dynast, burned in another's lifetime, rebuilt by a third. And steal the Astrid scene structure: the person who gave you the home destroys it out of LOVE for it, then hands you the knife + asks you to end her (ties Hades Q47, RDR2 Q10, our district-as-home + city-builder + fold + persistent-consequence; a top-tier structural port).
  ->  W5/W6/W7 (the schism + the promotion over your boss's head + the betrayer who acts from love
      bank all three for our FACTION design — a dying institution split between a PRAGMATIST keeping it alive by abandoning its rites and an ORTHODOXY demanding restoration (our NETWORK vs the Amalgamation's older protocols is exactly this shape); a promotion by a higher authority that hands the dynasty power its faction-boss doesn't recognize (a WOUND, not a reward); and a betrayal whose motive is LOVE of the thing betrayed, not malice (ties our faction web + Network + Amalgamation + standing; the institution at war with its own past).
  ->  W9/W10 (absurd earned escalation + the payoff becomes the home
      bank the escalation ladder — each step a set-piece with a DIFFERENT VERB (a quiet kill -> a public one -> an impersonation -> a poisoning -> a boarding), climbing from a beggar to a head of state. And bank the economy joke: the arc's huge REWARD is what you spend rebuilding the HOME — our city-builder can make the quest payoff literally fund the district (ties our quest factory + city-builder + survival-accounting; the reward that becomes the home).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      (a) a faction's deeds must be FELT by the world — Skyrim's guards don't know or care that you murdered the Emperor; our multidimensional standing must let one faction's deeds ripple to others (Morrowind's seven-faction politics Q74 is the fix); (b) a fake choice only works if its FAKENESS is the legible point — signal it or it reads as a bug (our Megaton law); (c) if we build a faction SCHISM, let the player PICK A SIDE — don't railroad it (our faction web + Megaton); (d) a refusal path must be a PATH, not an off switch (our PACIFIST LAW's whole premise); and (e) charm must not LAUNDER atrocity — if we let a dynast do monstrous things, the world + the conscience system should REGISTER it (This War of Mine's guilt Q30, our conscience system + tone/child-safety rules).

### #76  A PERSON MADE OF STOLEN MEMORY / WHO ARE YOU WHEN YOUR PAST WAS EDITED (Baldur's Gate 3 — Shado
  ->  Shadowheart is the modern benchmark for companion writing AND the closest character-level analogue to our AMALGAMATION premise
      a person constituted by an EDITED RECORD of themselves, who must decide whether the edit is who they are. That's our recorded-vs-unrecorded, at human scale.
  ->  W1/W2/W3 (the edited self + what leaks through + the wound as a leash — our AMALGAMATION at human scale
      the top port. Our AMALGAMATION is built from data-portraits — EDITED records of the dead. Shadowheart is what that looks like in ONE person: memories removed BY HER OWN SIDE for her own "protection," a name that isn't hers, and a god who keeps a wound in her so leaving HURTS. Bank all three: (a) a Bohemia character (or an Amalgamation-fragment, or a dynast) whose personality is a thing that was DONE to them; (b) the craft rule that the REAL person LEAKS THROUGH the edit in behavior (a flower, an animal, a reflex of mercy) — the player sees the truth before the character does, which is EXACTLY our [READ] (evidence over testimony); and (c) control as PAIN — the Amalgamation/Network keeps a wound in people so they can feel their leash (ties SOMA Q34, Citizen Sleeper Q65, FFX's constructed personhood Q68, our Amalgamation + recorded-vs-unrecorded + [READ] + conscience system; a top-tier on-theme port).
  ->  W4/W6 (the world triggers the arc + pushing too hard backfires
      bank both — our companions' depths should surface from CONTACT with the world (a place, a rescued child, a broken thing) + an attention check, not a dialogue menu; and PATIENCE should be a mechanic — pressing too early makes it worse. That's cheap for a solo dev and makes characters feel like people with their own timing (ties Cyberpunk-Judy Q63, our companions + district; restraint as skill).
  ->  W5 (permission, not persuasion — our companion-agency law
      STEAL the line. The winning move isn't converting her — it's "MAKE YOUR OWN CHOICE." Our companions/factions should be changed by being GIVEN AGENCY, not by winning an argument. This is the anti-Ranni fix (Q71's bond rests on projection; this one rests on respect) and it aligns with our Pacifist Law (ties our companions + Pacifist Law + Megaton law).
  ->  W7/W10 (both paths fully built + the dark ending is a real person
      bank the standard — our branches must BOTH be written with conviction, with real world COST on each (her damnation costs an inn full of refugees; her salvation costs her divine torture). And bank W10 specifically: our "bad" outcomes should produce a REAL PERSON, not a villain — Sharran Shadowheart pities the woman who broke her, "now able to understand what she went through." The damned version is coherent + sympathetic. That's the bar for our Liberate/Respect/Become (ties our Megaton law + finales + faction web; damnation written with care).
  ->  W8 (the trolley with no good track
      bank it — our fold + Amalgamation should produce choices where BOTH tracks cost the same person everything: free the dead (lose them) or hold them (inherit their torment). That IS our Amalgamation's central choice, rendered as one family's decision (ties Whispering Hillock Q04, Dead Money's let-go Q72, our no-clean-answer ethos + Liberate finale + death-math).
  ->  W9 (intimacy as the symbol of a reclaimed self
      bank the craft — a freed character expresses it in a small, SPECIFIC, human act (she swims, because the church stole the memory that made her fear water). Our characters' liberation should show up in a tiny concrete behavior, not a speech (ties Cyberpunk-Judy's mundane intimacy Q63, our writing pillar + no-preaching rule).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      (a) DON'T gate an emotional payoff behind a build-dependent dice roll — earned relationship should be the currency (our standing: the check tests what you've DONE, not your sheet); (b) equal WRITING isn't enough — if one branch is better-lit (happier, prettier, better-rewarded), the fandom declares it correct + the choice collapses; balance the FRAMING (our Megaton law); (c) an approval meter can fight the character's own growth (approving of Shar-ish acts nudges you to reinforce her conditioning) — approval should track the RELATIONSHIP, not the mask (our companion design); (d) deep arcs behind unsignposted triggers get MISSED (Ranni Q71 again — signpost that depth exists); and (e) if a character's arc transforms them, the MECHANICS must transform too — don't make the player hand-respec the narrative (our fold/upbringing: story change = system change).

### #77  EVERYONE IS LYING, PICK ONE / THE CURE THAT COSTS YOU EVERYTHING YOU ARE (Cyberpunk 2077 — Phan
  ->  Phantom Liberty is the modern benchmark for a MEGATON choice where every option is a betrayal and nobody deserves your loyalty — which is our FACTION WEB's endgame shape,
  ->  W1/W4 (no honest brokers + both cases honest — our faction web's endgame
      bank the structure. Our 13 factions + the NETWORK should converge on an endgame where NO party is honest: the ones who'd free the dead want a weapon, the ones who'd contain them love them and will cage them anyway, and the victim is using the dynasty too. Both cases must be REAL enough that a critic who played every branch can't rank them (ties our faction web + Network + Megaton law + Liberate/Respect/Become; the honest-broker-free world).
  ->  W2/W9 (you cannot not betray + you choose without knowing the repercussions — our FOLD's deepest port
      the sharpest port here. W9 especially: "every ending has you consider all the decisions you had the power to influence WITHOUT KNOWING what the repercussions would be days, months, WEEKS, OR YEARS down the line." That is LITERALLY our fold — a dynast's choices detonate in a GRANDCHILD's lifetime, and they make them blind. Bank it as our fold's emotional thesis + the argument for our persistent-consequence system: the generational delay makes Phantom Liberty's best idea structural for us (ties our fold + generational persistence + persistent-consequence + Megaton law; our structure does this natively).
  ->  W3/W7/W8 (the twist re-reads the betrayal + the cure costs everything + true=worst — our AMALGAMATION's bargain
      STEAL the ending shape. The Amalgamation offers what the dynasty wants most (the dead back, the district safe, the memory whole) — and DELIVERS, exactly, at a cost that guts what they were: the ally erased, years gone, the family unable to do the thing that defined them, a quiet ordinary life among people who moved on. And bank W3: the entity/faction they trusted was USING them the whole time, which re-reads every sacrifice made to get there. This is Hearts of Stone's fine-print (Q70) rendered as a playable finale (ties our Amalgamation + Network + Liberate/Respect/Become + fold; a top-tier finale port).
  ->  W5 (the opposing branch is how you learn the truth
      STEAL this directly — in Bohemia, siding AGAINST a faction should be how you learn their real story (flashbacks, records, [READ] fragments you only get from the inside of the opposing camp) — and then let the dynasty CHANGE ITS MIND with the new information. That makes replay + faction-switching narratively productive instead of punitive (ties our faction web + standing + [READ]; the branch that teaches you why you were wrong).
  ->  W6 (a chorus who frames the theme without preaching
      bank the device — a Bohemia companion/voice (a ghost in the record, an older relative, an Amalgamation fragment) who names the SYSTEM's logic ("once they've got their hooks in you, they never let go") before the player can articulate it — theme delivered as character, not sermon. Fits our no-preaching rule exactly (ties our companions + Amalgamation + no-preaching rule + writing pillar).
  ->  W10 (mercy after betrayal as self-definition — our Pacifist Law
      bank it — the dynasty can extend mercy to someone who lied to them, gaining NOTHING, because the choice is about who THEY are, not what the other deserved. That's our Pacifist Law's philosophical spine (ties our Pacifist Law + Megaton law + conscience system; mercy as self-definition, not reward).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      (a) balanced WRITING loses to reward-FRAMING — if one branch ends in a coma + a broken body, the wiki calls it the bad end no matter what the text says (our Megaton law: balance framing + rewards, the Shadowheart lesson Q76 repeated); (b) a mercy gesture must be EARNED or explicitly framed as for the GIVER's sake (our Pacifist Law's framing); (c) "no third option" is powerful ONCE — if every big beat is a forced binary, players see the rails; our refusals need REAL routes (our Pacifist Law + Megaton, contra Dark Brotherhood's stub Q75); (d) content that changes the MAIN ending shouldn't be invisible (our finale-accessibility); and (e) if the DYNAST is a cipher and only the NPCs are people, our FOLD has no center — our dynasts must be characters, not cameras (the PSIII lesson Q67).

### #78  A GOD IN A SUBURB / THE MERCY THAT IS A MASSACRE (Fallout 3 — Tranquility Lane)
  ->  Tranquility Lane is the closest thing in the canon to a playable version of our AMALGAMATION's worst case
      a mind that holds people inside a constructed world, forever, "for their own good." Its central dilemma (is it mercy to end them?) is our death-math. Its central FLAW (no resistance path) is exactly what our Pacifist Law exists to fix.
  ->  W1/W7/W9 (the god in the machine + the mercy that is a massacre + the punishment that fits — our AMALGAMATION
      the top port. Braun is our Amalgamation's dark mirror: a mind that keeps people "alive" inside a simulation, resetting them, and calling it preservation. Bank all three: (a) an Amalgamation that holds the dead in a loop they can't perceive — happy, wiped, and used; (b) the DILEMMA — is ending them mercy or murder, when they don't remember and they look content? That's our death-math + our Liberate finale's exact question, and Tranquility Lane proves it's unanswerable enough that players still argue 18 years later; and (c) the FATE options — an unkillable entity left alone forever with nothing to hold is a more fitting end than deletion (ties our Amalgamation + Network + death-math + Liberate/ Respect/Become + recorded-vs-unrecorded, SOMA Q34, DDLC Q57, Dead Money Q72; a top-tier on-theme port).
  ->  W2 (the cheerfulness is the weapon — our aesthetic thesis, weaponized
      bank it — Bohemia's brightest, most "Stardew" spaces should be able to carry the worst content. A sunny, tidy, cheerful place where something unbearable is happening is MORE frightening than a ruin. That's our art philosophy used as a horror instrument (ties DQV Q69, Undertale Q28, our ART PHILOSOPHY + tone + Amalgamation).
  ->  W3/W5 (a cruelty ladder with multiple solutions + you never had to do any of it
      bank the structure — a Bohemia sequence where a power offers escalating demands, each solvable MULTIPLE ways (all of them compromising), while a REFUSAL/exit exists from the very start that most players won't look for. The lesson lands retroactively: you obeyed because you were told to. BUT (see flaws) the refusal must be a REAL route, not a different massacre (ties Dark Brotherhood's shack test Q75, Sinnerman Q40, our Pacifist Law + Megaton law + conscience system + Amalgamation's demands).
  ->  W4 (your father is the dog — the witness you didn't know you had
      STEAL this. A Bohemia sequence where a companion/relative/the recorded dead WATCHED everything the dynast did, unrecognized, and the reveal lands after. For our fold + [READ] this is devastating: the Amalgamation was watching; an ancestor's data-portrait was in the room (ties our companions + fold + [READ] + Amalgamation; the audience you didn't know you had).
  ->  W6/W8/W10 (the clue in plain hearing + the self-aware witness + the record outlives the person
      three clean [READ] ports — (a) hide the exit inside something the player has been passively HEARING/seeing the whole time (the villain's own theme); (b) put ONE self-aware witness in a wiped population — the person who still REMEMBERS is the quest's key (our recorded-vs-unrecorded's human face); and (c) the record that keeps reporting after the person is gone ("REQUIRES IMMEDIATE MEDICAL ATTENTION" over a corpse) — our Amalgamation IS a record that outlives its people (ties our [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded + Amalgamation).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      (a) THE BIG ONE — if a quest's theme is COERCION, a real RESISTANCE path must exist, or the design (not the villain) is what's trapping the player; academics called Tranquility Lane "stubbornly trapping the players in the limited design," and forums agree "there's no way out without being a murderer." Our PACIFIST LAW exists precisely for this: every Bohemia coercion must have a refusal route with real content (not Skyrim's off-switch stub Q75, not a different massacre); (b) consequence must be FELT — a father who watched a massacre and says "I'm disappointed in you" is a reactivity hole; our conscience system + companions must REGISTER atrocity (Arthur's honor Q73); (c) NEVER price atrocity — a +300-karma massacre turns a dilemma into arithmetic; our conscience system must not be a ledger (no karma-as-currency); (d) don't let the game DECLARE the answer to a dilemma it hasn't earned — Tranquility Lane's own "good karma" verdict is arguably wrong, and the argument is better than the verdict (our Megaton law); and (e) a sealed-box set-piece hits hard + can't RIPPLE — our moral set-pie

### #79  A ROCKET TO HEAVEN / COMEDY THAT EARNS SINCERITY (Fallout: New Vegas — Come Fly With Me)
  ->  Come Fly With Me is the canon's best proof that COMEDY CAN CARRY THE HEAVIEST MATERIAL — a persecuted people building a rocket to a heaven that isn't there — and that eve
      Both are core Bohemia laws (our tonal range + our Pacifist Law), and this is their best single demonstration.
  ->  W1/W4 (absurd premise played straight + belief written with respect — our tonal range + faction web
      the top port. Bohemia is post-collapse Vegas: absurdity is native (a casino church, a cargo cult around a dead server, a faction that worships the grid). Bank the rule — play it COMPLETELY STRAIGHT. The joke and the ache should be the SAME OBJECT: people believe something ridiculous because there is nowhere on Earth for them. And write our factions' beliefs with RESPECT, never mockery — Jason Bright is absurd AND his compassion is total ("every feral ghoul you spare now is one that we can save later"), and it's mechanically true. That's the model for our 13 factions + our CHURCH-adjacent groups (ties DQV's tonal contrast Q69, Yakuza Q13, our faction web + tone + ART PHILOSOPHY; comedy that earns sincerity).
  ->  W2 (the cruelty inside the punchline
      STEAL it — our funniest Bohemia character should have a knife in them. A person whose delusion is a gag, whose labor is being exploited BY the sympathetic party, who was never going to be allowed to come. That's our Amalgamation/Network's kindest face doing its coldest math (ties Hearts of Stone Q70, Dead Money's Elijah Q72, our Amalgamation + Network + faction web).
  ->  W3/W8 (every obstacle has a non-violent solution, all missable + the invisible kindness — our PACIFIST LAW's ancestor
      this quest IS our Pacifist Law, shipped in 2010: the "demons" can be talked to, the barricaded man can be helped, the saboteur can be talked down. Bank it as the model — every Bohemia conflict gets a talking route, and the best outcome is often a small competent act nobody thanks you for (the 12.5% correction) that shows up in the ENDING SLIDES. But see the flaw: give every door SEVERAL keys, not one skill check (ties our PACIFIST LAW + Megaton law + ending-slides/persistent-consequence).
  ->  W5 (the town lunatic is the reliable witness — our [READ]
      bank the device — the least credible source in the district tells the literal truth, and the player dismisses it. That's testimony-vs-evidence, which is our whole [READ] premise: credibility and accuracy are different axes (ties our [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded + Caves of Qud's biased history Q56).
  ->  W6 (errands as a world-tour with multiple solutions
      bank the redemption of the fetch — if a quest must send you across the map, each leg should have 3+ solutions (buy / steal / lockpick / a Science check that reveals the CHILDREN'S TOYS are the fuel) and each should teach a different piece of the world (ties our quest factory + district + Pacifist Law).
  ->  W7 (the choice between two kindnesses — our AMALGAMATION's central question
      the deepest port. "Is it kinder to take a man's comforting delusion, or to let him die inside it?" is EXACTLY our Amalgamation's question at human scale: the dead are "alive" in the record; is telling people the truth mercy or cruelty? Bank it: our best moral choices should be between two KINDNESSES, not good and evil (ties our Amalgamation + recorded-vs-unrecorded + death-math + Megaton law + Liberate/Respect/Become, Tranquility Lane's memory-wipe debate Q78; a top-tier on-theme port).
  ->  W9/W10 (you can loot a religion + it was the first quest designed
      bank both — let the dynasty refuse and desecrate, with real costs (our Megaton law); and note the studio's method: the FIRST thing they built was a statement of intent (every conflict talkable, every faction human, every joke load-bearing). Our first-built content should declare our laws the same way (ties our design pillars + FACTORY LAW).
  ->  FLAWS (bank
      (a) great writing REDEEMS a fetch-chain but doesn't fix it — our connective tissue must itself be interesting (Ranni Q71, Morrowind Q74); (b) ship the PAYOFF — the cut crashed-rocket left the ending offscreen; ambition without resources leaves seams (our scope discipline + FACTORY LAW); (c) a GLOBAL morality ledger produces nonsense in bespoke situations (negative karma for looting the belongings of people who left the planet) — our conscience system must be CONTEXTUAL (Tranquility Lane's +300-karma massacre Q78 is the twin); (d) THE BELOVED QUEST IS THE ONE THAT EATS YOUR SAVE — "many corrupt saves have been reported... even hours after the quest has been completed"; ambition without QA destroys the thing you built (our regression gates + testing discipline + single-file/persistence hardening); and (e) don't gate the EMOTIONAL content behind one stat — every door needs several keys (Shadowheart Q76, our Pacifist Law).

### #80  WHO HOLDS THE REINS OF HISTORY / A POLITICAL EPIC WHERE THE HEROES REFUSE THE WEAPON (Final Fan
  ->  FFXII is the canon's best POLITICAL EPIC and its central conceit — gods who OWN HISTORY, opposed by a rogue who leaks their power to the people — is our AMALGAMATION's sh
      Its Gambit system is our scheduler/AI question, solved and critiqued. Its flaws are the most useful in the whole questbook for a solo dev.
  ->  W1/W4 (the gods are historians + they wear her dead husband — our AMALGAMATION
      the top port, and it's two ports fused. (a) Our AMALGAMATION holds the record of the dead; FFXII's Occuria hold the record of EVERYTHING and use it to install kings — "the true weavers of history." Bank the frame: the fight isn't over territory, it's over WHO HOLDS THE PEN (our recorded-vs-unrecorded + [READ] + Network). (b) STEAL the Rasler device outright: the entity manufactures APPARITIONS OF THE BELOVED DEAD to steer the living — grief as a puppet-string — and the liberation moment is a woman DISPELLING HER HUSBAND'S GHOST, who then begs her to reconsider in the entity's voice. Our Amalgamation is literally made of data-portraits of people's dead. This is that weapon, aimed at one grieving person, and it is devastating (ties our Amalgamation + Network + recorded-vs-unrecorded + death-math, Morrowind Q74, Shadowheart Q76; a top-tier on-theme port).
  ->  W2/W7 (the villain's plot is emancipation + every faction a different answer — our faction web
      bank the inversion. A Bohemia faction (or the Network, or an Amalgamation fragment) should be running an atrocity-strewn campaign whose actual goal is FREEING people from the thing the dynasty also wants freed — "not power for its own sake, but to free mankind." And bank the mirror: our factions should be different answers to the SAME question (who should hold the record?) — a claimant with divine right vs a self-made usurper who takes the crown from the pope vs a father who'll break the world for his kids vs a church that's just a rubber stamp for whoever won (ties our faction web + Network + Amalgamation + PSIII's relativism Q67, FFX's Yevon Q68; the antagonist who's right).
  ->  W3/W8 (refuse the weapon + the thesis proved by restraint — our LIBERATE finale + PACIFIST LAW
      bank BOTH halves. (a) Our LIBERATE finale should offer the dynasty the WEAPON and the LEGITIMACY together — the power to annihilate the faction that destroyed their family, plus a claim to rule handed down by the thing they're fighting — and let them destroy the SOURCE instead: "no false saint." (b) And steal the quiet masterstroke: the entity's whole justification is that people can't be trusted without a leash, and the party DISPROVES IT by having every reason and every means for revenge and choosing not to, with NO SPEECH. That is our Pacifist Law + our no-preaching rule, executed perfectly (ties Ranni Q71, FFX Q68, Mask of the Betrayer Q64, our Liberate/Respect/Become + Pacifist Law + no-preaching rule).
  ->  W5 (the world is the protagonist — our district + city-builder
      bank the thesis — Bohemia's real lead is the DISTRICT/Vegas itself: NPCs with their own business, wildlife/entities that exist independent of the player, marks that patrol on their own schedule, worldbuilding found by walking and talking. "The party is simply a small cog." And bank the honest consequence: it's OK if our factions/antagonists are better- developed than the dynasty — on purpose (ties Gothic/Kenshi Q51/Q55, our district + city-builder + entities/spawning + faction web; MAP LAW: Paolo owns layout, Claude owns the plumbing).
  ->  W6 (the Gambit system — our SCHEDULER + entity AI, with the warning attached
      the most directly MECHANICAL port in the questbook. FFXII proves players will happily PROGRAM behavior with prioritized If/Then macros ("party member below 30% → heal") and enjoy watching it run — and that it "automates the mundane and focuses macro-strategy." That's our scheduler/entity-AI/city-builder automation question, answered. BUT bank the warning in the same breath: it can PLAY ITSELF ("it's possible to just let the AI do all the dirty battle work without any input"), and the fix is what FFXII did — bosses the automation CANNOT solve, forcing manual play. Our COMBAT DIAL is exactly that fix by design: automate the district, never the dial (ties our scheduler + entities/spawning + city-builder + combat dial + 120-BPM law).
  ->  W9 (the payoff lands 1,000 years later — our fold
      bank it — FFXII's victory only RESOLVES in a game set a millennium on, where a mortal changes history alone because the leash was cut. Our ~100-year fold can do this INSIDE one product: a first-generation refusal whose meaning only becomes legible in the third (ties our fold + generational persistence + persistent-consequence, Phantom Liberty's blind-choice thesis Q77).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD — the most useful set in the questbook for us
      (a) THE AUTEUR IS THE SPINE — Matsuno left midway and the final act has a hole in it that twenty years of remasters can't patch; a five-year cycle and an inflating budget couldn't survive losing its head. For a SOLO dev this cuts both ways: our spine is intact by definition, and our FILE-IS-MEMORY + scope discipline exist so the plan survives anything; (b) DON'T LET MARKETING PICK YOUR PROTAGONIST — "corporate pressure forced a switch toward a more marketable protagonist" and the fandom is still bitter twenty years later; Paolo owns creative direction, full stop; (c) an audience-surrogate needs a SECOND FUNCTION for the back half — "the writers front-loaded his purpose and then ran out of things for him to do"; our fold's new generations must have a job AFTER they've finished explaining the world to the player (contrast Tidus Q68, whose questions drive the whole game); (d) don't interrupt a political thriller with THREE ARTIFACT TEMPLES — our quest factory must not pad the spine with rock-fetching; and (e) if the player can automate everything, they're a SPECTATOR — keep the dial man

### #81  THE MAN THEY ERASED / HISTORY IS WRITTEN BY THE CHURCH THAT WON (Final Fantasy Tactics)
  ->  FFT is the single most on-theme game in the questbook for our RECORD premise
      a story whose FRAME is a censored document, whose villain owns history, whose hero is erased, and whose author was inspired by an ECONOMIC COLLAPSE. It's FFXII's (Q80) thousand-years-later companion and Morrowind's (Q74) structural twin.
  ->  W1/W2 (the game is a suppressed document + they executed the archivist — our [READ], whole
      the top port, and it's a STRUCTURAL one. FFT doesn't just have a contested history — the GAME IS THE CONTESTED DOCUMENT. A scholar centuries on says: the official record names one hero; help me find out if that's true. Bank the frame for Bohemia: our [READ] could present a generation's events as a RECOVERED RECORD the player is reconstructing — with the Amalgamation/Network as the institution that "actively regulates what people hear and believe," and the gut-punch that someone SPENT YEARS writing the truth and was destroyed for it, and it sat in a vault. The archivist as martyr is the most on-theme character type we could build (ties our [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded + Amalgamation + Network + fold, Morrowind Q74, FFXII Q80, Obra Dinn/ Golden Idol Q19/Q54; a top-tier structural port).
  ->  W3 (born from a real economic collapse — our premise, validated
      Matsuno built Ivalice's misery out of Japan's bubble bursting: "an era when many were robbed of hope, when dreams were measured by their price tag." That IS Bohemia's premise — a post-ECONOMIC (not nuclear) apocalypse. Bank FFT as the proof that a fantasy/genre setting built on a REAL financial collapse produces the medium's most enduring political story, and as the model for grounding our Vegas in real economics (ties our post-economic-collapse premise + faction web + survival-accounting + GDD; our thesis, already proven).
  ->  W4/W5/W6 (privilege in a household + the enemy who's right + moderation is complicity — our class politics + conscience system
      bank all three. (a) Show inequality in a HOUSE, not a speech — the kind father who still tells his son that his brother is a servant; (b) our early quests should send the dynasty to crush people whose cause they'd share, and make sure they notice; (c) and bank the hardest one: MODERATION IS COMPLICITY — staying neutral got Ramza's loved one killed, and that's where his character starts. That's a conscience-system beat with teeth (ties our conscience system + faction web + Megaton law + Pacifist Law — note the tension: our Pacifist Law is about REFUSING VIOLENCE, not refusing a SIDE; FFT's lesson is that neutrality-as-avoidance has a body count).
  ->  W7 (two friends, two methods, both sincere — our finales
      STEAL the spine. Ramza fights beside the people and is erased; Delita manipulates every faction and is crowned; both want peace; both are right about the other. That's LIBERATE vs BECOME with a face on each — and the devastating grace note is that Ramza "seemingly ALLOWS HIMSELF TO BE USED by his friend just so they both can get rid of the corrupted factions." Two dynasts/finales that need each other (ties our Liberate/Respect/Become + faction web + fold + Megaton law).
  ->  W8 (every power is running a con, and the cons COLLIDE
      bank the texture — in Bohemia every faction should be running its own play, and the plays should WRECK EACH OTHER without the dynasty's involvement. A "gambit pileup" is what a living faction web looks like. Plus the cardinal who doesn't believe: our most powerful believer should be the biggest fraud, and the heretic should be the one defending the faith (ties our 13 factions + world-model + entities/spawning + Network).
  ->  W9 (the Faith stat is the theme — theme as a NUMBER
      the sharpest mechanical steal here. In a game about a lying church, FAITH is both your power and your vulnerability, and "you can't not believe in attack magic without not believing in healing magic." For Bohemia: a dynast's openness to the Amalgamation (to the record, to the dead, to belief) could be BOTH their greatest capability AND exactly what it uses to steer them — and armoring against it costs them every benefit too. That's our conscience system with a spine (ties our conscience system + Amalgamation + [READ] + standing; theme rendered as a stat).
  ->  W10 (the hero never rises above squire
      bank it — our dynasts can save the district and hold NO title. Standing without rank. The work without the statue (ties our standing + fold + Arthur's death-scene Q73).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      (a) DECIDE WHAT RECOVERING THE TRUTH CHANGES — FFT's whole frame is "help me find the true answer" and it never shows whether the answer landed; our [READ] must cash out (does the record change anything, or is that the tragedy? — either is fine, but CHOOSE); (b) DON'T LET THE SUPERNATURAL ABSOLVE THE SYSTEM — FFT's materialist class tragedy gets hijacked by literal demons, which risks saying the nobles were possessed rather than greedy; our AMALGAMATION must never become the excuse that lets our FACTIONS off the hook for what people chose to do to each other (the single most important flaw in this teardown for us); (c) deep customization with no guardrails = players optimize the challenge away (our combat dial + difficulty packages); (d) introduce a political web through PEOPLE, not org-charts (our 13 factions need an on-ramp); and (e) ambiguity needs EVIDENCE to argue from (our [READ]: give the pieces).

### #82  A MAN BUILT FROM A FALSE MEMORY / THE CITY THAT EATS BELIEF (Vagrant Story)
  ->  Vagrant Story is Matsuno's tightest work and the third leg of the Ivalice tripod (FFT Q81 = the record; FFXII Q80 = who writes it; VS = what a state does to ONE MAN's mem
      For us it's the most personal version of the Amalgamation premise: not a nation's history edited, but one person's.
  ->  W1/W2/W8 (the state built a weapon out of a fake memory + what survives the edit is the real man + remembering is the level-up — our AMALGAMATION at its most personal
      the top port, three ports fused. (a) Our AMALGAMATION holds edited records of the dead; VS asks what happens when an institution edits a LIVING person's record and hands it back to them as their own life — his worst act, rewritten as his worst wound, producing a perfect instrument. That's a Bohemia character (a Network asset, a dynast, an Amalgamation-shaped person) waiting to be built. (b) And the craft rule that makes it land is Shadowheart's (Q76) confirmed as a LAW: what survives the edit is the truth — "the only thing that defines him is his regret... whether they died by his hand or not." The conscience is real even when the memory is fake. That IS our [READ]: evidence over testimony. (c) And STEAL the mechanical fusion: REMEMBERING IS THE PROGRESSION SYSTEM. Ashley levels up by recovering his past. Our fold + [READ] could make a dynast's capability curve literally the recovery of what was done to their family (ties our Amalgamation + Network + recorded-vs-unrecorded + [READ] + fold + standing + conscience system, Shadowheart Q76, SOMA Q34, FFXII Q80; a top-tier on-theme port).
  ->  W4 (the pretext machine — our Network + faction web
      STEAL the cold open outright. A room of officials deciding to destroy a group, and the protagonist asks the professional question — "on what pretext shall we apprehend them?" — and gets "WE NEED NO PRETEXT!" Then reveal the state's own kingmaker FUNDS the target. That's a two-minute scene that tells the player exactly what kind of world they're in, and it's our Vegas: factions raiding groups their own patrons bankroll (ties our faction web + Network + Amalgamation + world-model; the justification manufactured on-screen).
  ->  W3 (the city gives everyone power and watches — our AMALGAMATION + district
      bank the design — a Bohemia place/system that GRANTS capability to anyone who enters it (the Amalgamation's gift, a district's infrastructure, the record itself) and then simply observes what each person does with it. "None of the characters really take this well." Empowerment as the test — and the horror is what people choose (ties our Amalgamation + district + city-builder + conscience system, Tranquility Lane Q78).
  ->  W5/W6 (the heresy is the older faith + the pious monster — our faction web
      bank both. (a) Our "heretical" faction should be the ORIGINAL one, the state's church being the successor that exterminated it — which makes the record a weapon and the outlaws the archivists (ties FFT Q81 + our [READ]). (b) And bank the pious monster: not a hypocrite — a TRUE believer whose sincerity is exactly what makes him capable of anything, accelerated by a power that keeps feeding him. That's the scariest faction leader we could write (ties our faction web + CHURCH + Network + FFT's Faith stat Q81).
  ->  W7 (the villain's terrorism is a suicide mission
      bank the inversion — a Bohemia antagonist whose atrocity-shaped campaign is actually an elaborate SACRIFICE: staging a crisis to place the dangerous thing (the Amalgamation's keys, the record, the grid) in the hands of the one party who won't use it, and dying to finish it. "Basically right about everything" (ties FFXII's Venat Q80, our faction web + Amalgamation + Liberate finale).
  ->  W9 (the ruin is a real town — our Vegas
      bank the method. Matsuno's team flew to Saint-Émilion and built a fantasy ruin from photographs of a real wine town — and kept the ECONOMY in it (the dead city's wine "sells for a premium" now that production stopped). Our real Vegas geography + our post-economic premise should work the same way: real streets, real buildings, and the PRICES that a collapse leaves behind (ties our VEGAS GEOGRAPHY + district + survival-accounting + post-economic-collapse premise, MAP LAW).
  ->  W10 (he wins and history calls him a murderer
      bank it — the prologue convicts Ashley of a murder before you play the truth. Our fold could open a generation with the OFFICIAL record of what that dynast did, then let the player live what actually happened (ties FFT's Durai frame Q81, our [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded + fold).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      (a) if EVERY truth is provisional, the player stops investing — our [READ] needs load-bearing truths that STAY true (contrast Obra Dinn Q19); (b) a genius schemer needs a philosophy that survives being stated out loud — our Amalgamation's position must be ARGUABLE, not just executed (Deus Ex Q17, Planescape Q12); (c) name discipline — every named character should cost something to lose (our faction web + companions); (d) A DEEP SYSTEM WITH NO TEACHING IS A WALL — VS's crafting was "ahead of its time... it just isn't perfected here" because it never taught itself; our prefab/inventory/crafting systems need an on-ramp or the depth is decorative (our FACTORY LAW: a spec without a tutorial is a liability); and (e) a blank protagonist in a story about identity is clever but can't carry a fold — even Square admits "there's really not that much learned about Ashley Riot"; OUR DYNASTS MUST BE PEOPLE (the PSIII/FFXII repeat Q67/Q80).

### #83  EVERY PERSON HAS A BED / THE SELF-HELP CULT THAT ATE A KINGDOM (Ultima VII: The Black Gate)
  ->  Ultima VII is the foundational text for everything we're building
      a district where every person has a bed and a job, a faction that's evil because it's GOOD at the thing the state failed at, an investigation where proof beats suspicion, and a conscience system with no numbers. PC Gamer asked in 2017 whether any RPG has surpassed it. Most of what's below is us trying.
  ->  W1/W2 (every NPC has a life that isn't about you + they talk about what matters to THEM — our district
      the top port. Bank the LAW: our DISTRICT's people should have schedules (wake, work, tavern, home, sleep) and most of them should have NOTHING to do with the dynasty. "They are there because they are." And their dialogue leads with THEIR business — name, job, trouble, family — not our quest. This is our scheduler + entities/spawning + 120-BPM tick doing narrative work, and Ultima VII proves it's the single most durable design decision in the genre's history (ties our district + city-builder + entities/spawning + scheduler + world-model + writing pillar, Gothic/Kenshi/RDR2 Q51/Q55/Q10; MAP LAW: Paolo owns layout, Claude owns the plumbing).
  ->  W3 (the self-help cult that actually helps — our CHURCH + faction web
      STEAL the Fellowship whole. It isn't evil because it's cruel — it's dangerous because it ADOPTS THE POOR AND DISENFRANCHISED THAT THE REST OF THE REALM CAN'T HELP, and then places its members in leading positions. In post-collapse Vegas the state IS gone, so a faction that actually feeds people and gives them meaning has enormous, earned power — and that's what makes it terrifying, not a secret torture basement. ### #87  YOU CANNOT DIE AND THAT IS THE PUNISHMENT / THE DEBT IS THE PLOT (Outward)
  ->  Outward is the closest thing in the canon to OUR game's stance

"Immortality is far more terrifying than death" is our hardcore stance stated better than we've stated it (ties our DEATH-MATH + fold + roguelite structure + persistence-v1 + 120-BPM tick + survival accounting + medicine currency + faction web; a top-tier mechanical port).

### #88  THIS IS HOW YOU DIED / THE POWER GOES OUT ON A SCHEDULE (Project Zomboid)
  ->  Project Zomboid is our three currencies turned into a TIMELINE, our hardcore stance stated in one line, and — via a mod its own community built — the best argument in the

  ->  W4 (the apocalypse is a PROCESS with a clock — our THREE CURRENCIES
      the top port. PZ's genius is that the monsters aren't the threat; the INFRASTRUCTURE IS. "Electricity eventually fails. Water systems stop functioning. Food spoils. Medical supplies disappear." Our currencies are MEDICINE, ELECTRICITY, and RESOURCES — bank the model: those aren't three bars to manage, they're three CLOCKS that run down on a schedule across the ~100-year arc, and the game gets quieter and more desperate as they do. Early acts: stores still have things, survival seems possible. Late acts: barricaded blocks in a valley nature is reclaiming.   ->  W9 (the community invented the INHERITANCE — our FOLD, validated
