The modder's own framing — "it's like in a zombie movie where a character TEACHES ANOTHER HOW TO SHOOT OR FARM BEFORE THEY GET BITTEN... PASSING THE TORCH OF KNOWLEDGE" — is our FOLD in one sentence. Bank two things: (a) our fold is solving a REAL, demonstrated pain (players patched it in themselves); and (b) STEAL THE OBJECT — inheritance should be a THING IN THE WORLD (a notebook, a recording, a data-portrait) that the heir FINDS, not an abstract stat carryover. A player said installing it and pretending his new character found the old timer's notebook "SUDDENLY BECAME A COMPELLING NARRATIVE" (ties our FOLD + generational persistence + [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded + AMALGAMATION + death-math + persistence-v1, Dragon's Dogma's pawn knowledge Q84, Sunless Sea Q66).
  ->  W1/W2/W3 (tell them the ending + no "new game" because NEW INFERS HOPE + guaranteed death makes survival mean something — our hardcore stance + ART PHILOSOPHY
      bank all three. PZ says the quiet part in the LOADING SCREEN and it's the most confident design decision in this teardown. For us: our post-economic-collapse Vegas can state its terms up front, and W2 is the detail to steal — THEME IN THE UI ITSELF. They removed the word "new" from a menu because it implies hope. What does our menu refuse to say? And the payoff is the paradox: certainty of loss is what makes a day survived MEAN something (ties our ART PHILOSOPHY + death-math + fold + survival accounting + despair-with-a-thread-of-hope).
  ->  W5 (emotional conditions are survival STATS — our medicine currency
      STEAL it. Boredom, anxiety, and panic are tracked like hunger: panic cuts your melee damage and crit, and UNHAPPINESS MAKES EVERY ACTION TAKE LONGER (a debuff on TIME — brutal and elegant in a 120-BPM tick game). And the cures are looted: a cigarette, beta blockers. That's our MEDICINE currency doing double duty — physical AND psychological — and it's exactly the kind of accounting our hardcore stance wants (ties our medicine currency + survival accounting + 120-BPM tick + combat dial + district + companions).
  ->  W6/W7 (the deaths are domestic + the player supplies the narrative — our death-math + district
      bank both. (a) PZ's deaths are: a burglar alarm on your first window, wet clothes → cough → noise → horde, a zombie in a toilet. Our death-math should kill people with ORDINARY CHAINS, not bosses — three mundane facts in a row. (b) And the storytelling model: "THE APOCALYPSE PROVIDES CONSTRAINT; THE PLAYER SUPPLIES NARRATIVE." A game with no plot generates better stories than most games with one, because the systems "DO NOT PRESCRIBE IDENTITY. THEY ALLOW IT TO EMERGE THROUGH BEHAVIOR." That's the Dwarf Fortress bar (Q45) and it's what our scheduler + district are for (ties our death-math + survival accounting + district + scheduler + entities/spawning + fold, Dwarf Fortress Q45, RimWorld Q44).
  ->  W8 (the world explains itself through its own dying media — our [READ]
      bank it. PZ has no exposition; it has TV and RADIO that broadcast the outbreak until the stations go dark and the power fails. You learn the apocalypse's timeline by watching television until the electricity dies. For us that's the ELECTRICITY currency carrying the [READ]: the record is legible while the grid holds, and goes dark with it (ties our [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded + AMALGAMATION + electricity currency + district; deeply on-theme — our Amalgamation IS a broadcast that needs power).
  ->  W10 (the mascot is a cartoon raccoon — our ART PHILOSOPHY
      bank the tonal law. The single bleakest survival game ever made ships with SPIFFO, a cheerful fast-food raccoon, and its own founder says he's there "TO COUNTERACT THE BLEAKNESS." The levity doesn't undercut the dread, it SHARPENS it — and it's why the game is beloved instead of merely admired. That's our despair-with-a-thread-of-hope stance and our Stardew-adjacent pixel warmth doing the same job (ties our ART PHILOSOPHY + music repo + tone).
  ->  THE STUDIO NOTE (bank it
      October 2011, they moved into a "nice secure apartment," got BURGLED before the internet was connected, and lost the DEV BUILDS AND THE ON-SITE BACKUPS because they had no reliable connection. They rebuilt from scratch. That is our NEVER-LOSE-FILES LAW as a horror story — and their "ready when it's ready... THAT BASICALLY ELIMINATES ALL CRUNCH" is the pace note.
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      (a) A DEEP SYSTEM WITH NO TEACHING IS A WALL — fourth confirmation (Arcanum Q86, Vagrant Story Q82, Dragon's Dogma Q84); PZ's "guidance shouldn't be restricted to a wiki" and "the main issue with the game is actually its selling point" are the warnings; our on-ramp is not optional; (b) hardcore must TEACH on the way down — "the systems lean toward PUNISHING RATHER THAN INSTRUCTIVE" (our difficulty packages exist for this); (c) PERMADEATH WITHOUT AN INHERITANCE PATH PUNISHES LONG PLAY — the community built the fix themselves; our fold is the answer, and it must be REAL, not cosmetic; (d) a sim's combat still has to feel right (our combat dial); (e) 15 years in early access — "ready when it's ready" bought depth and cost a release date; and (f) a bleak sim self-selects a small audience, and the counterweight (Spiffo, warmth, humor, music) is REQUIRED, not decoration.

### #89  THE ROPE, NOT THE STICK / STRANGERS BUILT THE BRIDGE YOU'RE STANDING ON (Death Stranding)
  ->  Death Stranding is the canon's purest statement of our PACIFIST LAW's philosophy (the rope, not the stick), the best-executed asynchronous-help system ever shipped, and —
      For a single-file iPhone game whose whole subject is CONNECTION TO THE DEAD, this teardown is unusually close to home.
  ->  W1 (the rope, not the stick — our PACIFIST LAW's philosophy, stated
      the top thematic port. Kobo Abe's metaphor is the best articulation of our stance we've found: early humans used STICKS to ward off threats and ROPES to bring things closer, and MOST GAMES ARE STICKS. Our Pacifist Law is currently a RULE ("you can finish without killing"). Death Stranding makes it a PHILOSOPHY WITH A VERB: the game's actions are ropes — carrying, connecting, building, delivering. Bank it: Bohemia's core verbs should be rope-verbs (rebuild, supply, connect, remember, carry) and the stick should be the exception that feels wrong. That also directly answers Arcanum's XP-curve flaw (Q86) — if the game's VERBS aren't violence, the progression can't reward it (ties our PACIFIST LAW + city-builder + logistics + conscience system + ART PHILOSOPHY + combat dial, Arcanum Q86, Undertale Q28).
  ->  W2/W7 (asynchronous help with no server + help arrives as OBJECTS — our FOLD
      the standout mechanical port, and it pairs exactly with Dragon's Dogma's Pawns (Q84) and PZ's Skill Journal (Q88). Three separate teardowns now converge on the same answer for us: OUR FOLD'S INHERITANCE SHOULD BE PHYSICAL THINGS LEFT IN THE WORLD. Not a stat carryover — a LADDER. Generation one's dynast bolts a walkway across a gap, caches medicine in a wall, leaves a note, wires a generator. Generation three FINDS IT and doesn't know who left it (or does, and that's the emotion). And the Dark Souls contrast is the design rule: a MESSAGE says "try jumping"; an OBJECT lets you jump. Ours should be objects. Zero server cost, fits the single HTML file, and it's our whole theme — the dead helping the living (ties our FOLD + generational persistence + persistence-v1 + city-builder + district + prefab factory + [READ] + AMALGAMATION + single-file-carry, Dragon's Dogma Q84, Project Zomboid Q88; a top-tier port).
  ->  W3/W4 (the only reward is a LIKE + the crowdfunded highway — our city-builder
      STEAL the psychology. No material payoff exists for helping, and players fund bridges they'll never use because "EVEN IF YOU CONSTRUCT THINGS JUST FOR YOURSELF, THEY WILL HELP OTHERS." In our fold, that's literal and free: what the first dynasty builds, the third inherits. Bank the structural version — SOME infrastructure should be UNAFFORDABLE TO ONE GENERATION, so it's paid for in pieces across a hundred years by people who never see it finished. That is Bohemia's premise as a construction mechanic (ties our city-builder + fold + generational persistence + logistics + life-support buildings + survival accounting + THREE CURRENCIES; a top-tier port).
  ->  W6 (paths smooth as people walk them — our district + street generation
      bank it. Desire paths, simulated: a route walked enough becomes a ROAD, easing traversal for everyone after. Across our fold that's gorgeous and cheap — the routes generation one used become generation three's streets, and the CITY'S SHAPE IS AN ACCUMULATED RECORD OF WHAT PEOPLE ACTUALLY DID. Our street generation + tile pipeline could carry this natively (ties our district + street generation + city-builder + fold + scheduler + MAP LAW: Paolo owns layout, this is emergent plumbing).
  ->  W5 (the terrain is the boss — our 120-BPM movement law
      bank the nerve. Kojima made WALKING the skill: balance on the triggers, every step considered, "took something we never even think about in games and turned it into something that requires our attention." We already made movement a first-class system (the 120-BPM request law, the grid tick, hold-to-run). That's the same bet. The warning comes with it: half the audience expected Skyrim and bounced (ties our 120-BPM law + movement + district + difficulty packages).
  ->  W8 (the death screen is a SOCIAL SPACE — our AMALGAMATION + death-math
      bank it, because it's nearly our premise already. When Sam dies he enters THE SEAM and drifts among THE FLOATING SOULS OF OTHER PLAYERS, and can TOUCH THEM to strengthen a connection before returning. Our AMALGAMATION is an entity made of the uploaded dead. What is our death screen? If a dynast dies, do they pass THROUGH the Amalgamation — meet what's in there — and get sent back changed? That's a death-math + Amalgamation + fold fusion sitting right there (ties our AMALGAMATION + death-math + fold + [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded, SOMA Q34, Citizen Sleeper Q65).
  ->  W10 (the premise aged into prophecy — our logistics
      bank the encouragement. A game about a delivery driver, mocked at reveal as "a glorified Amazon driver," shipped four months before 2020 made delivery drivers the most important people alive. Our post-ECONOMIC collapse + logistics + supply chains are the same bet on the same unglamorous truth: the people who MOVE THINGS are the ones holding it together (ties our logistics + post-economic-collapse premise + survival accounting + faction web (CARAVANS, TRADES) + district).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      (a) AN ASYNCHRONOUS SOCIAL SYSTEM IS EMPTY AT THE START — DS's first 5-10 hours are an "Amazon Delivery Simulator" because nobody's built anything yet; our fold has the identical problem in GENERATION ONE and must seed itself (pre-place a predecessor's leavings, or make gen-one's loneliness the POINT); (b) SHARED/INHERITED CONTENT NEEDS CURATION — IGN flagged "incomplete or poorly placed player objects" misleading players and donated gear TRIVIALIZING BOSSES; our fold's inheritance needs a quality gate and a difficulty-integrity check (our FACTORY LAW + regression gates); (c) obliqueness costs audience — fifth confirmation ("any attempt to summarize it will be for naught"; "drank a little too much of his own kool-aid"); (d) if your core verb is unusual, TEACH IT LOUDLY AND EARLY or the wrong audience arrives and leaves angry (our on-ramp, fifth confirmation); (e) the altruism is still driven by a NUMBER — players admit they wanted the likes; design so the selfish path IS the generous one; and (f) OUR PACIFIST LAW CANNOT MEAN OUR DIAL IS BAD — DS's combat "feels a bit out of place" by

### #90  WE ACCIDENTALLY MADE A HORROR GAME / THE ENEMY IS A FEELING (Subnautica)
  ->  Subnautica is our PACIFIST LAW's best real-world case study (they removed the gun and the world got SCARIER), our HD-tile-repo bet validated by a studio that nearly went 
  ->  W1/W2 (they removed the gun and accidentally built horror + they held the line when players demanded weapons — our PACIFIST LAW + Paolo-decides law
      the top port, and the most reassuring thing in this teardown. Unknown Worlds set out to make "an open-world underwater game WHERE YOU DIDN'T KILL CREATURES" and produced one of the scariest games ever made BY ACCIDENT — because a threat you cannot kill has no ceiling. Our Pacifist Law isn't a limitation, it's a horror engine: the AMALGAMATION, the NETWORK, the factions are all scarier if the dynasty's answer can't be "shoot it." And W2 is the craft lesson for Paolo directly: when players demanded guns, Unknown Worlds KEPT THE RULE and fixed the real problem (fauna behaviour was irritating, not under-lethal). Feedback is DATA, not instructions — that's our verdict workflow's whole spine (ties our PACIFIST LAW + AMALGAMATION + faction web + combat dial + verdict workflow + Paolo-decides law + ART PHILOSOPHY, Undertale Q28, Death Stranding Q89; a top-tier port).
  ->  W3/W9/W10 (name the feeling then engineer it + music makes silence worse + terror → competence → love — our ART PHILOSOPHY + music repo
      bank all three as a tonal package. (a) Unknown Worlds wrote down the SIX FEARS and built systems to produce them; our ART PHILOSOPHY should be that explicit about what emotion each system exists to make. (b) Their sound thesis is directly usable for our 103-song repo and our master volume-balance pass: "THE MUSIC SERVES NOTHING MORE THAN TO MAKE THOSE SILENT MOMENTS MORE DREAD-INDUCING." Music as the thing that makes silence LOUDER. (c) And the arc is our despair-with-a-thread-of-hope stated as a player journey: terror, then competence, then AFFECTION — a player finished it and "didn't want to leave... IT WAS STARTING TO FEEL LIKE HOME." Our Vegas should end up feeling like home (ties our ART PHILOSOPHY + music repo + master volume-balance pass + district + despair-with-a-thread-of-hope + fold).
  ->  W4/W8 (oxygen taxes curiosity + progression is DEPTH, not power — our survival accounting + standing
      STEAL the oxygen structure. It's the best survival clock in the genre because it's a HALFWAY RULE: every meter down costs two, so curiosity is mathematically taxed and every discovery shrinks your margin. Our MEDICINE/ELECTRICITY/RESOURCES should have at least one clock with that shape — a run into the valley that costs you double, so going further is always a calculation you can lose. And pair it with W8: our progression should be ACCESS, not power — every upgrade unlocks a DEPTH (a district, a tier, a distance), which fits our standing-as-spine, our city-builder, and answers Arcanum's XP-curve flaw (Q86) the same way Outward (Q87) does (ties our THREE CURRENCIES + survival accounting + standing + city-builder + district + logistics + fold + Pacifist Law).
  ->  W6 (hand-crafted world, procedural CONTENTS — our HD tile repo, validated
      the production port. In a genre that procedurally generates everything, Unknown Worlds hand-built the entire seabed because "YOU CAN'T TEACH AN ALGORITHM ART DIRECTION" — and shipped the best-looking survival game ever made, at the cost of five years, $10M, and multiple near-bankruptcies. But note the SPLIT they used: the WORLD is hardcoded, the RESOURCE NODES AND ITEMS AREN'T. That's exactly our architecture — Paolo authors the map (MAP LAW), the FACTORY generates the contents (tiles, props, prefabs, events). Our 8,674-tile HD repo IS this bet, and our FACTORY LAW is how we afford what nearly killed them (ties our HD tile repo + prefab factory + street generation + district + MAP LAW + FACTORY LAW + ART PHILOSOPHY).
  ->  W5 (no map, and a burning ship for a compass — our tile repo + landmark discipline
      bank it, with the warning attached. Subnautica has NO MAP: you navigate by landmarks and positional audio, and the wrecked AURORA burns on the horizon as both the plot and the compass. That's the third teardown in a row (Outward Q87, Ultima VII Q83) saying the same thing: NO-MARKER NAVIGATION REQUIRES LANDMARK DISCIPLINE. If we ever go Morrowind-style directions (Q37), our tile repo + variation pipeline has to produce places that look like THEMSELVES — and our Vegas has real landmarks built in (ties our HD tile repo + variation + district + VEGAS GEOGRAPHY + MAP LAW + Morrowind Q37).
  ->  W7 (the story arrives by radio, exactly when you're lost — our quest factory + [READ]
      STEAL the device. Subnautica's entire quest system is ONE OBJECT: a radio in your escape pod that pings with distress calls from people who crashed before you, drip-feeding a story into a game that has none, and "JUST WHEN YOU MIGHT BE LOST FOR THINGS TO DO, IT'LL START PINGING OFF." Investigating them yields DATA ENTRIES that "REINTRODUCE THE HUMAN ELEMENT INTO AN OTHERWISE LONELY GAME" by "LEARNING ABOUT THE FATE OF THOSE WHO CAME BEFORE." Punk — that is our AMALGAMATION and our [READ] with the serial numbers filed off: the dead talking to you through infrastructure, and the mystery IS their fate. And mechanically it's a pacing valve for our quest factory: an idle-detector that pushes a thread when the player stalls (ties our AMALGAMATION + [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded + quest factory + electricity currency + district + Network, Project Zomboid's dying broadcasts Q88).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      (a) a progression built on ACCESS still needs its late game to stop taxing you with early-game chores — SN's back half "requires a lot of construction and GRINDING... NO MATTER HOW ADVANCED YOU GET, YOU CANNOT ESCAPE THE NEED FOR BASIC RESOURCES" (our survival accounting + act pacing); (b) WHATEVER ISN'T YOUR CORE LOOP WILL SHOW ITS SEAMS BRUTALLY — SN's land sections drop "almost to Steam shovelware quality"; polish it or cut it (our frame-locked building set + scope discipline); (c) hand-crafting is a REAL cost that nearly killed a studio — and it's still the right call, which is why FACTORY LAW exists; (d) a fear-of-the-unknown design has a REPLAY PROBLEM ("SN2 is just more of SN1... is that enough to justify a new work of art?") — directly relevant to our roguelite fold: our second run can't rely on mystery, it has to rely on the WORLD REMEMBERING (Nemesis Q48, our persistent consequence); and (e) total commitment to one idea is why it works AND why it's not for everyone ("could there perhaps be less water?") — the Outward lesson (Q87) again, and Paolo's already made that call.

### #91  THE FIRE HAS TO BE FED WITH PEOPLE / GWYN WAS AFRAID OF US (Dark Souls)
  ->  Dark Souls is our AMALGAMATION's structure in mythic form
      a system that keeps a world running by consuming people, a religion that exists to supply it, a founding myth authored by its beneficiary, and an ending where the only way out is to not participate. Its final boss is literally called an amalgamation of everyone who volunteered.
  ->  W1/W2/W9 (the fire eats people + the plague is the symptom + the final boss is everyone who said yes — our AMALGAMATION
      the top port, three fused. (a) Our AMALGAMATION is made of the uploaded dead and the NETWORK maintains it — bank the FUEL ECONOMY: what does it CONSUME to keep running, and who decides who gets burned? Dark Souls' answer is the most powerful person available, every era, forever. Ours could be electricity, medicine, or PEOPLE'S RECORDS. (b) And steal the diagnostic inversion: the Undead Curse isn't the enemy, it's what a world LOOKS LIKE when it's held past its time — people who can't finish dying, decaying into Hollows "AFTER HOPE AND MEMORY HAVE FADED ENTIRELY." That is our premise: the dead who are still in the record and can't be done. (c) And DS3's SOUL OF CINDER is our Amalgamation's boss form already written: a composite person assembled from every champion who volunteered, fighting with the moves of every player who ever did (ties our AMALGAMATION + Network + death-math + recorded-vs-unrecorded + [READ] + electricity/medicine currencies + life-support buildings + LIBERATE finale; a top-tier port).
  ->  W3/W4/W6 (the god's sacrifice was FEAR + the religion recruits + the prophecy was written by the beneficiary — our CHURCH + Network + [READ]
      the antagonist port. Gwyn didn't save the world; he was TERRIFIED of what came after him, so he burned himself to delay his own successors, then had his children "shepherd the humans" — i.e. CONVINCE US TO DO IT TOO. The Way of White is a church whose one doctrine is volunteering for the furnace. And the prophecy that drives the whole game is a vague employment ad, backed by a goddess who's an illusion. For us: our founding myth (who saved Vegas, who built the Amalgamation, what the Network is FOR) should be authored by the party that benefits, and the faction that preaches sacrifice should be the recruiter. That's our [READ]'s whole job — the record versus what happened (ties our CHURCH + NETWORK + AMALGAMATION + faction web + [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded + standing, Ultima VII's Fellowship Q83, FFT Q81, Dragon's Dogma Q84).
  ->  W5 (both advisors are kingseekers — our faction web
      STEAL it. Frampt says burn; Kaathe says refuse and rule. Players trust Kaathe because he's anti-establishment. But "BOTH OF THE PRIMORDIAL SERPENTS ARE KINGSEEKERS" — one wants you in the fire, one wants you on a throne, and neither is on your side. In a 13-faction game where the dynasty is constantly being courted, that's the shape: the rebel recruiting you against the system is ALSO recruiting you (ties our faction web + Network + standing + Megaton law, Phantom Liberty Q77, FFXII Q80).
  ->  W8 (the refusal is walking out of the room — our LIBERATE finale
      bank it WITH its flaw. The most radical choice in the medium is implemented as "don't press the button, leave." No cutscene, no dialogue tree. That's beautiful and it belongs in our finale vocabulary — a Bohemia ending you reach by NOT doing the thing everyone has spent 100 years telling you to do. BUT see the flaw below: players triggered it BY ACCIDENT (ties our LIBERATE/Respect/Become + Megaton law + fold, Dragon's Dogma's Godsbane Q84, Ranni Q71).
  ->  W7 (the opening tells you everything except the WHY — our [READ] + ART PHILOSOPHY
      bank the technique. DS's cutscene "SPELLS IT ALL OUT" — the ages, the lords, the war, the fading. The ONLY thing withheld is WHY it's ending and WHAT TO DO. Everyone remembers it as cryptic; it isn't. It's generous with FACT and silent on MEANING. That's exactly the register our [READ] should run in: hand the player the record freely, withhold the interpretation (ties our [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded + ART PHILOSOPHY + quest factory, Project Zomboid's "this is how you died" Q88).
  ->  W10 (the only Lord still at his post has no legs
      bank the image. Every other Lord of Cinder was supposed to return and burn again, and they ALL walked away — "ALL THE LORDS HAVE SHIRKED THEIR DUTY, BUT MAYBE THEY'RE ON TO SOMETHING." The one still sitting there is a commoner who's MISSING HIS LEGS: "either he's so devoted that he crawled here… OR HE SIMPLY NEVER LEFT." One prop, and it asks whether the last loyal man is a saint or just stuck. Our faction web + fold should have one of those (ties our faction web + fold + persistent consequence + district).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      (a) A CHOICE WITH NO CONFIRMATION MEANS SOME PLAYERS NEVER KNOWINGLY MADE IT — real players: "I unintentionally lit the fire again"; "I literally just killed Gwyn, walked around for 5 seconds then SUDDENLY I HAVE ACCIDENTALLY PICKED AN ENDING." Our Megaton law requires the player to KNOW they're choosing; elegance can't cost comprehension; (b) THE STRUCTURE MUST NOT CONTRADICT THE THEME — DS's thesis is "break the cycle" and BOTH endings dump you into New Game Plus; our roguelite fold has this exact risk, and Hades (Q47) is the fix (make the loop diegetic); (c) sixth confirmation that ambiguity generates community AND makes the theme optional (Vagrant Story Q82, Arcanum Q86); (d) a masterpiece can ship with a visibly rushed third act and stay a masterpiece — but everyone notices FOREVER (our act structure + regression gates); and (e) sequels that re-explain your mystery flatten it retroactively (our GDD canon discipline).

### #92  THE CURE IS THE DISEASE / EVERY FACTION IS A CHARACTER (Bloodborne)
  ->  Bloodborne is our MEDICINE CURRENCY's darkest possible reading, the best faction-web writing in the medium, and — under the tentacles — a game about INHERITANCE that pair
  ->  W1/W2/W6 (the cure is the disease + the institution is the monster + they sell you both — our MEDICINE CURRENCY + CHURCH/NETWORK
      the top port, three fused, and it's aimed straight at a currency we already have. Our three currencies are MEDICINE, electricity, resources. Bloodborne asks the question we should be asking: WHO CONTROLS THE MEDICINE, AND WHAT DOES CONTROLLING IT DO TO THEM? Yharnam's answer: an institution that discovered a miracle, monopolized the supply, KNEW it caused the plague, kept distributing it because "the common people were expendable," and then sold the ARMED RESPONSE to the consequences it created. And the definitive description of it — "'HEALTH' FOR THE CHURCH IS SIMPLY PROLONGING THE DAMAGE TO KEEP THE DESPERATE DEPENDENT ON 'TREATMENT' ANOTHER DAY" — is a faction thesis we could write tomorrow. In post-collapse Vegas, whoever holds the medicine holds everything (ties our MEDICINE currency + survival accounting + CHURCH + NETWORK + faction web (13 factions) + AMALGAMATION + death-math + logistics + district + post-economic-collapse premise; a top-tier port).
  ->  W3 (factions ARE the characters — our 13 factions, validated
      the writing-method port. Miyazaki wrote a game whose CHARACTERS ARE INSTITUTIONS: Byrgenwerth, the Healing Church, the Choir, the School of Mensis, the Vilebloods, the Executioners. Each is a POSITION on one question (what do we do with the blood?), and their disagreements ARE the plot. We have THIRTEEN factions and a central question (what do we do with the Amalgamation / the dead / the record?). Bank the law: each faction should be a coherent ANSWER to that question, with a founding, a schism, a doctrine, and a body count — and their argument should BE our story (ties our faction web (13 factions) + AMALGAMATION + Network + Church + [READ] + GDD structure).
  ->  W7/W9 (the cosmic horror is BABIES + the whole game was an interview — our FOLD
      the port nobody would predict. And the Hunter's Dream itself was "created by the Moon Presence IN ORDER TO SELECT AND NURTURE POTENTIAL CANDIDATES CAPABLE OF BECOMING ITS CHILD" — the whole game was an audition to be someone's baby. Punk: our FOLD is three generations and our AMALGAMATION is made of the dead. Bloodborne is the horror version of our premise — what if the thing that outlives you is a child you didn't choose, shaped by something that was selecting for it the whole time? (ties our FOLD + generational persistence + AMALGAMATION + Network + death-math + Liberate/Respect/Become, Dragon's Dogma Q84, Dark Souls Q91).
  ->  W4 (the apocalypse is a lab-ethics dispute with a customer base — our AMALGAMATION's origin
      STEAL the schism. Byrgenwerth's founder said BE CAREFUL WITH THE BLOOD. His students heard "stop testing on OURSELVES," so they took the samples, left, and "**OUTSOURCED THEIR GUINEA PIGS**" — to the public, as a paid treatment. That's a better origin than any evil plan: the AMALGAMATION/NETWORK founded by people who split from a cautious institution and needed test subjects, so they made the public an OFFER (ties our AMALGAMATION + Network + faction web + recorded-vs-unrecorded + post-economic-collapse premise, STALKER's C-Consciousness Q85).
  ->  W5 (the doctrine is printed on the uniform — our [READ] + inventory
      bank the technique WITH its flaw. The Healing Church's entire medical ethic ("MEDICINE IS NOT A MEANS OF TREATMENT BUT RATHER A METHOD FOR RESEARCH, AND SOME KNOWLEDGE CAN ONLY BE OBTAINED BY EXPOSING ONESELF TO SICKNESS") is a CLOTHING ITEM DESCRIPTION. Our garment system, our prefab props, our inventory — every object can carry a faction's position. But see the flaw: most players never read it (ties our [READ] + inventory macro/micro + garment system + prefab factory + faction web + recorded-vs-unrecorded).
  ->  W8 (the victim is PROUD — our CHURCH + conscience system
      bank the line. The false doctor, forcibly impregnated by a god, in agony, says: "**IT FEELS AWFUL… BUT, IT PROVES THAT I'M CHOSEN. DON'T YOU SEE?**" That's the most disturbing thing in the teardown and it's a CHARACTER BEAT our Church/Network could carry — someone whose suffering is the evidence of their election (ties our CHURCH + NETWORK + AMALGAMATION + conscience system + faction web, Dark Souls' Way of White Q91).
  ->  W10 (every faction that reached for the gods died of it, and the gods aren't evil — our AMALGAMATION

### #93  NO MORAL SYSTEM MEANS REAL MORAL DILEMMAS / TRUST IS THE RAREST RESOURCE (Rust)
  ->  Rust is the control experiment for our CONSCIENCE SYSTEM
      remove the karma bar entirely and watch people build their own. It's also the clearest proof that TRUST is a resource, and the sharpest warning about what we can't have (a hundred real strangers) and what we must therefore MANUFACTURE.
  ->  W1 (no moral system means REAL moral dilemmas — our CONSCIENCE SYSTEM, at the limit
      the top port, and the third confirmation of the answer. Ultima VII (Q83) showed consequence-as-relationships beats a karma bar. Arcanum (Q86) showed reputation that names your specific deeds beats a number. Rust is the extreme case: **NO SYSTEM AT ALL**, and it produces the most agonized moral behavior in the medium — a man walking around with stolen goods trying to find the guy he stole them from, because nothing in the game told him to. "There is no moral system in the game aside from the system you take into it. **SO YOU END UP WITH REAL ACTUAL MORAL DILEMMAS.**" Our conscience system's job is not to SCORE the dynasty. It's to make sure the world NOTICES, and then get out of the way (ties our conscience system + Megaton law + standing + faction web + district + Pacifist Law, Ultima VII Q83, Arcanum Q86, Tranquility Lane Q78).
  ->  W2/W3 (trust is the only resource with no node + every stranger is Schrödinger's threat — our faction web + THREE CURRENCIES
      STEAL the economics. In Rust wood is common, metal is findable, and TRUST CANNOT BE FARMED — it's built slowly through repeated positive interactions and destroyed instantly, which makes it the most valuable thing on the map. Our currencies are medicine, electricity, resources. Bank the fourth, uncounted one: in a 13-faction post-collapse Vegas, TRUST should behave like a resource with no node — slow to accumulate, impossible to buy, catastrophic to lose. And W3 is the mechanic that gives it teeth: every stranger must be genuinely ambiguous. "Nobody takes the risk" only works if the risk is real (ties our faction web (13 factions) + standing + THREE CURRENCIES + survival accounting + district + entities + conscience system).
  ->  W6 (the base is a HOSTAGE — our city-builder
      the port aimed straight at our genre. Rust's buildings aren't a construction mechanic; they're the thing you LOVE BECAUSE IT CAN BE TAKEN. Our city-builder + fold has this available for free and should USE it: what the dynasty builds must be losable, and the fear on the walk home is the feature (ties our city-builder + district + fold + persistent consequence + survival accounting + death-math + faction web, Outward Q87's "your town gets sacked").
  ->  W7/W8/W9 (the five-minute revenge story + invented diplomacy + governments nobody coded — our quest factory + district + 13 factions
      bank all three as the emergent-content target. (a) A stranger killed a guy, a friend hunted him down shouting "**THIS IS A MESSAGE FROM MRZERO!**", and a professional game developer called it one of his most memorable experiences — five minutes, zero script. That's what our scheduler + entities + persistent consequence should be capable of, and it's the Nemesis lesson (Q48) reachable without a Nemesis system. (b) Players invented a DIPLOMATIC RITUAL from nothing — the sideways strafe, the shouted "I'm friendly." Our district's NPCs should have protocols like that, and they should sometimes be lies. (b) And the observation that "**you DO FEEL more powerful, and dominating of others, once you possess more powerful weapons**" while a rock still killed a bowman — gear changes how people ACT more than how they win. For our dial + difficulty packages, that's a real design note: arming the dynasty changes its DIPLOMACY, not just its odds (ties our death-math + survival accounting + inventory + combat dial + difficulty packages + conscience system).
  ->  W5 (they kill you BECAUSE you have nothing
      bank the ugly truth — "you had nothing. But in Rust, KILLING = VALIDATION... **YOU'RE A MOVING STRESS BALL.**" Violence with no loot incentive, purely for the feeling. ### #94  THE WAR STARTED WITH AN UNPAID BILL / TEN MONTHS TO EARN ONE BETRAYAL (EVE Online)
  ->  EVE is the largest emergent-politics experiment ever run, and its two most famous events are both DIRECTLY our game
      a war caused by a bookkeeping failure (our survival accounting) and a betrayal that took ten months of genuine friendship to set up (our faction web). It's also the clearest statement of the four conditions that make stakes real.
  ->  W1 (the biggest war in history started with an UNPAID BILL — our survival accounting + city-builder
      the top port, and it's almost too on-the-nose for us. A corporation forgot to check an autopay box. Sovereignty dropped INSTANTLY. Two coalitions converged. 21 hours, 7,548 people, 75 Titans, $330,000. CCP's own line — "**MISSED BILL PAYMENTS ARE CERTAINLY NOT NEW TO THE HUMAN EXPERIENCE**" — is the funniest and most useful sentence in this teardown. Our post-ECONOMIC apocalypse runs on MEDICINE, ELECTRICITY, RESOURCES, and our city-builder has upkeep. Bank the law: A MISSED PAYMENT SHOULD BE ABLE TO START A WAR. Not a dramatic betrayal — a lapse. The most consequential thing in a resource game should be forgetting to pay for something (ties our survival accounting + THREE CURRENCIES + city-builder + logistics + faction web + district + fold + post-economic-collapse premise, Outward's Blood Price Q87; a top-tier port).

(b) THE CONTRACT WAS A BODY — the fee was symbolic; the client wanted "the cold corpse." A job whose payment isn't the point is a fantastic quest hook, and in our world the AMALGAMATION makes it deeper: what does someone want with a DEAD PERSON'S BODY when the record already has their mind? (c) And the aftermath is the conscience system: ONE betrayal made "**EVERY CEO IN EVERY CORPORATION THINK TWICE ABOUT WHO THEY TRUSTED**" — a single act permanently changing a whole society's trust baseline (ties our faction web + companions + conscience system + standing + death-math + AMALGAMATION + fold + persistent consequence, Rust Q93, Nemesis Q48).
  ->  W7 (the developers built a permanent MONUMENT from the wreckage — our district + persistent consequence
      STEAL it outright, and it's cheap. (b) And EVE's players built a single-transferable-vote parliament with NDAs and an annual summit because governance is an emergent NEED (second confirmation with Rust Q93). Our factions exist because the vacuum demands them (ties our faction web (13 factions) + city-builder + survival accounting + logistics + standing + persistent consequence, Rust Q93, CK3 Q46).
  ->  W9 (the four conditions for real stakes — our death-math + Megaton law
      bank the formula. Peer-reviewed: B-R5RB happened because of "**ANARCHIC STRUCTURE** [no referee], **PLAYER COMMITMENT TO THEIR RESPECTIVE CORPORATIONS** [real belonging], **MEASURABLE ECONOMIC VALUE** [a price tag], **AND RISK ASSOCIATED WITH PERMANENT LOSS**." That's a checklist we can audit our own systems against: does our district have no referee, real belonging, legible value, and permanent loss? Where a system is flat, one of those four is missing (ties our death-math + Megaton law + faction web + standing + survival accounting + fold + conscience system).
  ->  W5/W10 (espionage is legitimate play + the bank was a con — our Network + premise
      bank both. (a) CCP permits spying "**ABSENT EXPLOITS, VIEWING [IT] AS INTEGRAL TO EMERGENT CONFLICT RATHER THAN ABERRATIONS**" — infiltration, leaked retreat orders, years-long embedded agents. Our post-ECONOMIC-collapse premise has a financial-con-artist faction slot with its name on it (ties our NETWORK + faction web + [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded + post-economic-collapse premise + survival accounting, Arcanum Q86, FFT Q81).

  ->  This is the quest to steal for the AMALGAMATION's most personal scene

### #96  HAD TO BE ME / SOMEONE ELSE MIGHT HAVE GOTTEN IT WRONG (Priority: Tuchanka, Mass Effect 3)
  ->  This is the single best "good people did this" quest in the medium, and it's aimed straight at our AMALGAMATION and our MEDICINE currency
      It's also the cleanest demonstration that a persuasion check should require EVIDENCE, not a stat.

      the top port. Mordin maintained it and can justify every step. Our AMALGAMATION is the same shape — built to help, defended with real numbers, and the harm is structural rather than malicious. Steal the CHARACTER too: the Network's Mordin, the person who helped build the thing and is the only one who could unbuild it, who is not sorry the way the player wants him to be, and who is RIGHT about most of it (ties our AMALGAMATION + Amalgamation threat logic + NETWORK + faction web + MEDICINE currency + death-math + [READ] + Liberate/Respect/Become; a top-tier port).

      STEAL this outright, it's our whole [READ] thesis in one scene. You cannot talk Mordin out of curing the genophage with charisma. You can ONLY do it when the argument is literally true — "**with Eve dead and Wreav in charge, this won't lead to a renaissance, it will lead to war**" — and he responds by DOING WHAT A SCIENTIST DOES: "**Mordin, relying on logic, will pause. HE WILL LOOK AT THE DATA. He will realize you are right.**" Then: "**I MADE A MISTAKE. FOCUSED ON BIG PICTURE. BIG PICTURE MADE OF LITTLE PICTURES. TOO MANY VARIABLES. I... I AM NOT SURE.**" Punk — our [READ] system should gate persuasion on RECOVERED EVIDENCE, not a stat: you can only change a faction's mind if you're holding something true.       bank all three as the complicity package. (a) The Dalatrass offers A FLEET during an extinction war. ### #97  THE CURSE IS THE ECONOMY / THE MALIGNANT ENTITY IS A WOMAN MAKING DICE (Investigate Doomed Comm
  ->  This is the best short quest ever written about our exact premise
      an ECONOMIC apocalypse, experienced from the inside, by people who can only understand it as a haunting. It's 70 XP, one building, and it's the whole thesis.
  ->  W1/W2 (the curse IS the economy + the supernatural resolves into real estate — our POST-ECONOMIC-COLLAPSE PREMISE + [READ]
      the top port, and it's the most direct hit in the whole questbook. Plaisance is not stupid. She has real data: every business in that building fails, every time, for years. That IS an anomaly and there IS a malignant entity destroying these people — it's just a MARKET, and markets are invisible, so the mind reaches for a ghost. Then the whole mystery collapses on one Shivers check: why hasn't NEHA's business failed? "**Because it's not in the same building as the others.**" A property line. Punk — our Vegas died of an ECONOMIC collapse. Our districts should be full of people who have folk explanations for structural forces: the cursed block, the unlucky corner, the building that eats businesses. And our [READ] should be the thing that turns a curse back into a cause (ties our post-economic-collapse premise + [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded + district + city-builder + faction web + survival accounting + AMALGAMATION; a top-tier port).
  ->  W9/W10 (you choose whether she keeps the ghost + truth and lie pay the same — our conscience system + Megaton law
      STEAL this exactly. You can tell Plaisance the truth (economics; it will happen again; there is nothing to exorcise) or you can tell her the curse is real (it's not your fault; it's a monster; a monster can theoretically be beaten). One is TRUE. **The other is KINDER.** And the game pays **70 XP** either way — it has no mechanical opinion. That's the Ultima VII/Rust answer (Q83/Q93) at quest scale: no karma, no reward differential, just you and what you decided to say to a frightened woman. Our conscience system should have dozens of these (ties our conscience system + Megaton law + no-clean-answer + standing + [READ] + district + faction web).
  ->  W5/W6/W7 (the netherworld is an abandoned gym + you summon the ghost by yelling into a furnace + the entity asks if you're here for your dice — our district + prefab fact
      bank all three as the staging package. (a) Harry says "**IT'S THE NETHERWORLD...**" and it's a failed gym: a shot put ball, a 60kg barbell, abandoned offices, a planning board. Somebody's business, stopped mid-sentence. That's EXACTLY what our HD tile repo and prefab factory are for — the horror is that it's just a room where something ended. (b) The chimney/furnace route is our district's best trick available for free: the building has a voice in it because a PERSON is in it, and sound travels through infrastructure. (c) And the anticlimax — "**the workshop of Neha, the Novelty Dicemaker, who asks whether you are here to pick up some dice**" — is the tone we want: post-apocalyptic Vegas full of people just trying to run their small business inside the catastrophe (ties our district + HD tile repo + prefab factory + entities/spawning + scheduler + [READ] + ART PHILOSOPHY + despair-with-a-thread-of-hope).
  ->  W3/W4 (you lie to get the job + the hook is ignoring a woman begging you to stop — our standing + conscience system
      bank both. (a) To be ALLOWED to help her, Harry passes a **DRAMA (11)** check to convince her he's a **psychic investigator.** He fabricates the exact credential her worldview requires. Our standing system should let the dynasty claim expertise it doesn't have, and the check should be a PERFORMANCE skill, not a knowledge one. (b) And the quest OPENS by ignoring a woman pleading with you to leave her curtains alone. The content costs a small unkindness to unlock. That's a real design position most games are too polite to take (ties our standing + conscience system + entities + quest factory + faction web).
  ->  W8 (the reward for solving it is an IDEA — our perks
      bank the mechanic. You don't get a gun. You get **THE PRECARIOUS WORLD** installed permanently in your head. Our PERKS system is a known gap (never fully documented) and this is a shape for it: perks earned by DEDUCTION, not by combat — an idea you understood becomes a permanent modifier. Fits [READ] natively (ties our perks + [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded + standing + conscience system, Caves of Qud Q56, Golden Idol Q54).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      (a) ~9TH CONFIRMATION — THE THESIS CANNOT LIVE BEHIND A CHECK; the entire point of this quest is one Shivers 14 roll in an optional sub-conversation, and failing it leaves you with "haha the ghost was a lady"; if our [READ] gates the conclusion behind a roll, most players get the setup and never the punchline; (b) ritual absurdity is characterful but the PATH has to stay legible (flashlight in a specific car → specific basement → shout into a furnace); (c) NOTHING CHANGES — the building stays doomed either way, which is thematically correct and mechanically inert; our persistent consequence should let the WORLD register what the dynasty learned even when it can't fix it; (d) comedy without consequence is a bit, not a quest; and (e) the least-played great quest in the game is the one carrying its thesis — put the thesis on the critical path. --- # V2 PAYLOAD — BACKFILLED 7/16/26 (FORMAT LAW v2). ### #98  THE EARTH WILL NOT ACCEPT HIM / YOUR FATHER LET THE PLAGUE IN ON PURPOSE (Isidor's Body, Pathol
  ->  This is the single most important quest in the book for our FOLD
      It is the inheritance quest, written by the people who understood that an inheritance is a DEBT, a REPUTATION, an ACCUSATION, and a corpse that won't go in the ground.
  ->  W1/W2 (you miss it by hours and get blamed + the inheritance is the only thing that makes you mean anything — our FOLD + generational persistence + standing
      the top port. Artemy's own words are our fold's thesis: "**THE INHERITANCE OF MY FATHER WILL NOURISH MY MIND AND MY BODY ALIKE. IT IS A QUESTION OF LIFE AND DEATH FOR ME TO CLAIM IT, FOR IT WILL IMBUE MY DISSOLUTE EXISTENCE WITH REASON... WHO WILL I BECOME IF I WILL FAIL TO BIND MY DESTINY WITH MY FATHER'S CALLING?**" Our generation-two dynast should arrive to a Vegas that has ALREADY DECIDED something about them, and the inheritance should be a claim they have to prosecute, not a stat that transfers. And STEAL the opening: he misses his father by HOURS, and the town's first act is to blame him for it. Our fold's handoff should be a MESS the heir walks into (ties our FOLD + generational persistence + standing + conscience system + district + faction web + persistent consequence + death-math; a top-tier port).
  ->  W10/W9 (your father dug up the plague and carried it home + the prophecy was accurate and the misreading killed him — our AMALGAMATION + [READ]
      the antagonist port, and it's brutal. Isidor — the town's only doctor, your teacher, the man whose letters called you home — went into the steppe with Simon Kain, DUG A HOLE, and deliberately infected himself to carry the plague back, because they'd decided "**THE PLAGUE WAS A NECESSARY STEP IN THE EVOLUTION OF THE TOWN.**" He'd already sealed a neighborhood and let it die once; the orphans you spend the whole game trying to save are the children he made. Our AMALGAMATION's founder should have that shape: the atrocity committed by the person the dynasty most loved, for a reason he can articulate, in a dream, before handing the decision to you — "**HE LEAVES THE FINAL CHOICE TO HIS SON, SAYING HE TRUSTS IN HIS JUDGMENT.**" And W9 is our [READ] in one beat: the prophecy was CORRECT and the powerful men MISREAD it, and their misreading is the murder (ties our AMALGAMATION + Amalgamation threat logic + NETWORK + [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded + fold + district + MEDICINE currency + Liberate/Respect/Become, Mordin Q96, Dark Souls' Gwyn Q91).
  ->  W3/W4 (the Earth refuses the body + three clues and the third answers a different question — our death-math + [READ]
      STEAL both. (a) "**THE EARTH WILL NOT ACCEPT ISIDOR'S REMAINS, AS IT IS SAID THAT A DEBT IS STILL OWED**" — a corpse that will not go in the ground because business is unfinished. Our death-math and our AMALGAMATION are built on the dead who aren't done; that's the image, and it's free. (b) And the autopsy is the best [READ] design in the medium: a horn-wound (who), dry skin (he was sick), and **DIRT UNDER HIS NAILS** (he'd been digging). Two clues answer the question you asked. The third answers the question you didn't know to ask, and it's the only one that matters. Every [READ] scene should have that third clue (ties our death-math + [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded + AMALGAMATION + fold + district, Obra Dinn Q19, Golden Idol Q54).
  ->  W5/W6 (the séance costs a child's lifespan and gives you nothing + "nothing would have changed" — our conscience system + no-clean-answer
      bank both, they're the cruelest pair in the book. (a) You can speak to your dead father — **at the cost of Grace's lifespan**, a little girl who tends graves — and he doesn't answer, because "**ISIDOR SEEMS TO BE SPEAKING WITH SOMEONE ELSE.**" You burn a child's years to overhear your dad talking to somebody else. No karma bar. No stat. Just the cost. That is our conscience system's target. (b) And Grace's finding — "**NOTHING WOULD HAVE CHANGED EVEN IF ARTEMY HAD ARRIVED ON TIME**" — is the answer to the player's guilt, and it's not comfort, it's worse (ties our conscience system + Megaton law + no-clean-answer + death-math + companions + AMALGAMATION + fold).
  ->  W7/W8 (the town invents a clay monster + the man who clears your name is wrong — our district + [READ]
      bank both. (a) The shabnak-adyr, "**A CREATURE MADE OF CLAY WITH BONE LEGS... BROUGHT UP BY A GRIEVING TOWN AS AN EXPLANATION FOR THE ATROCITIES,**" is the Doomed Commercial Area's curse (Q97) at murder scale: when the truth is unbearable, people build a monster. Our district needs folk creatures. (b) And the Bachelor CLEARS YOUR NAME BY BEING WRONG — he proves Isidor died of the disease; a child in a closet heard him killed. Being exonerated by a false theory is a better beat than being exonerated by the truth, and the letter's warning is our whole information layer: "**PEOPLE WITH A CERTAIN BIAS ARE LIKELY TO DELIBERATELY IGNORE THE FACTS. THEN, THERE ARE THE SIMPLETONS WHO WILL DISREGARD THE FACTS OUT OF STUPIDITY**" (ties our district + entities + [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded + faction web + standing + post-collapse premise).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      (a) ~10TH CONFIRMATION — IF THE THESIS REQUIRES A FULL COLLECTION SET, MOST PLAYERS NEVER LEARN WHAT HAPPENED: the truth here needs three autopsy clues + a séance + a late dream + a confession; our [READ] needs a FLOOR (a minimum truth everyone gets) as well as a ceiling; (b) the emotional scene has a combat tax in front of it (three guards, 30% health, bad melee) — our Dead Eye Dial must earn its place; (c) be careful about answering the question your premise is built on ("nothing would have changed"); (d) a low-standing start is great narrative and brutal onboarding — "**you won't be able to buy anything at shops with such reputation**" — gate the shops OR the content, not both (our standing + on-ramp); and (e) if you build a witness, build the scene where the testimony LANDS. --- # V2 PAYLOAD — BACKFILLED 7/16/26 (FORMAT LAW v2). ### #99  THE LEVEL WITH NO ENEMY / A VAMPIRE, TERRIFIED (The Ghost Haunts at Midnight, Vampire: The Masq
  ->  This is our PACIFIST LAW's proof-of-concept from 2004, our HD tile repo's best argument, and the cleanest demonstration in the medium that an ERRAND plus an ATMOSPHERE is
  ->  W1/W9 (there is no enemy + the hazards are the building — our PACIFIST LAW + combat dial
      the top port. You are a VAMPIRE — immortal, superhumanly strong, already dead — and the Ocean House is the scariest thing in your game, because **there is nothing to fight.** Critics noticed the irony: "**AN AREA HAUNTED BY GHOSTS WOULD BE SCARIER THAN THE VAMPIRES POPULATING BLOODLINES.**" The only things that can hurt you are **purple fire and steam** — the building's own systems. This is Subnautica's lesson (Q90) eleven years earlier, and it's the argument for building at least one Bohemia sequence where the Dead Eye Dial simply **does not come up**: no target, no dial, just a structure that wants you out (ties our PACIFIST LAW + combat dial + district + HD tile repo + prefab factory + death-math + AMALGAMATION; a top-tier port).
  ->  W2/W3 (built by researching professional haunted houses + the rule was stated and obeyed — our FACTORY LAW + ART PHILOSOPHY
      the method port, and it's a direct instruction for us. Mitsoda didn't invent a horror system. He identified that his level was LINEAR, decided that meant it was a **THEME PARK RIDE**, and then went and **researched how professional haunted house operators actually work**, plus ghost-movie pacing. Then he wrote his rule down — "**DREADFUL ANTICIPATION IS SCARIER THAN JUMP SCARES AND GORE**," citing **Jaws and Alien** — and obeyed it for an entire level with zero exceptions. That's our FACTORY LAW's spirit applied to a MOOD: name the discipline that already solved this, port it, state the law, gate against violations (ties our FACTORY LAW + ART PHILOSOPHY + district + quest factory + despair-with-a-thread-of-hope + prefab factory).
  ->  W7 (the fetch item IS the murder motive — our [READ] + inventory
      STEAL this structure exactly. Therese sends you to fetch a pendant. **2 XP.** And the optional diary reveals that Ed murdered his family in this building because he thought that locket was from his wife's lover — **when it was a gift from her mother.** The trinket in your quest log is the reason four people died. Our [READ] and our inventory should do this constantly: the object the dynasty is sent to retrieve carries the record of why the place is empty. And note the pattern from Q97/Q98 repeating a third time — the mundane explanation (a mother's gift) is more horrifying than the supernatural one (ties our [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded + inventory macro/micro + quest factory + district + AMALGAMATION + prefab factory).
  ->  W4/W5/W6 (the building takes your floor + attacks your light and your map + you do maintenance in a murder house — our district + HD tile repo + survival accounting + cit
      bank all four as the environment-as-antagonist package. (a) Ten seconds in, the stairs **break and drop you into the basement** — and the design is honest: whichever stairs collapse, the other set stays intact. A scripted catastrophe that can't soft-lock you. (b) The haunting attacks LIGHT and NAVIGATION, and a real player's real fear was "**I am worried I will run out of blood**" — no combat, and he's terrified of his resource bar. That's our survival accounting doing horror work. (c) And the objectives are **a washing machine, a boiler room key, a generator, and an elevator.** Building maintenance inside a murder house. Our city-builder + district can run that exact contrast: keep the lights on, in a place where something happened (ties our district + HD tile repo + prefab factory + survival accounting + THREE CURRENCIES + electricity + city-builder + life-support buildings + logistics).
  ->  W8 (the scariest figure is the only one helping you — our entities + AMALGAMATION
      bank the reversal. The woman in the bloody dress that players flee from is the **murdered wife**, and she is trying to save your life — "**HEEEEEE'S COMING!**", "**BEEEEEE CARRRRRRREEEEEFULLLLLL**" — and she physically points at the door you need. The most frightening thing in the building is a victim trying to help. Our AMALGAMATION is made of the dead; our entities should include figures that read as threats and are actually **warnings** (ties our entities/spawning + district + AMALGAMATION + [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded + companions + scheduler).
  ->  W10 (the climax is sunlight, and it's a lie — our ART PHILOSOPHY
      bank the beat, it's the best one here. "**THIS QUEST CONTAINS THE ONLY MOMENT OF TRUE DAYLIGHT IN THE ENTIRE GAME, WHEN THE PLAYER PICKS UP THE PENDANT.**" A vampire, at the end of a haunted house, walks into a warm sunlit room. It's an illusion. It vanishes the moment you take the necklace. The final scare isn't a monster — it's **grief**: showing a creature of the dark the one thing it can never have again. Punk, our game is despair with a thread of hope. That beat — the impossible good thing, briefly, then gone — is the exact tonal instrument, and our ART PHILOSOPHY should have one (ties our ART PHILOSOPHY + despair-with-a-thread-of-hope + district + fold + AMALGAMATION + music repo + HD tile repo).
  ->  FLAWS (bank HARD
      (a) YOUR BEST CONTENT CAN BE AN EXIT — real players "**WERE SO SCARED BY THE OCEAN HOUSE HOTEL AREA THAT THEY ACTUALLY STOPPED PLAYING THE GAME**," and a fan had to make a guide for getting through it "**WITH THE MINIMUM AMOUNT OF STRESS POSSIBLE**"; a mandatory intensity spike in a main chain loses people forever (our act structure + difficulty packages); (b) attacking NAVIGATION and RESOURCES simultaneously turns dread into frustration fast ("**this seems to be a maze... I am worried I will run out of blood**"); (c) if a friendly entity reads as a threat, build ONE unmissable reframing moment or the reveal never lands; (d) ~8th confirmation of the fetch-chain law, with an INVERSION worth noting — this is the one case where the errand HELPS, because banal tasks amplify horror; (e) total authorial control produces the strongest beats and contradicts everything else the genre sells (our MAP LAW: Paolo authors, we plumb); and (f) don't let your best content be your worst-paying content — **2 XP** for the best level of 2004. --- # V2 PAYLOAD — BACKFILLED 7/16/26 (FORMAT LAW v2). Origina

### #100  THE UTOPIA THAT WORKS / DON'T CALL THEM SLAVES (Vault City Citizenship, Fallout 2)
  ->  Quest 100, and it's the faction-writing masterclass
      a place that is genuinely, measurably BETTER than everywhere else, that you genuinely want to join, whose price of admission is agreeing not to notice the people outside the wall.

SAYING IT. And Lynette's psychology is the whole thing: they got a **Garden of Eden Creation Kit** — a magic box — and concluded they were better people; "**IF OTHERS CANNOT ACHIEVE THE SAME AS VAULT CITY, THAT MEANS THEY ARE NOT SMART OR STRONG ENOUGH.**" In a post-ECONOMIC collapse, that's every faction that came out of it holding something.       STEAL the three-door structure. **DOOR ONE:** the legitimate meritocratic test, which requires 10 INT and 10 LUCK — nobody passes; the front door is decoration. **DOOR TWO:** the one she actually offers — "**GET RID OF THE GHOULISH INHABITANTS OF GECKO**" — citizenship priced in bodies. **DOOR THREE:** her own assistant sells forged papers for **$200**, and they work at the government store. That is a complete satire of belonging, and it's a structure our STANDING system can run verbatim: the official path is impossible, the real path is atrocious, and the black market path is cheap and works (ties our standing + faction web + conscience system + Megaton law + no-clean-answer + district + survival accounting).

And "**BACK IN VAULT CITY LYNETTE WANTS NOTHING TO DO WITH IT**," because the reactor was never the problem. Our [READ] should do exactly this: recover the maintenance record that proves the war is a repair job, and watch the faction refuse it. And her reaction if you do what she asked — "**YOU DESTROYED THE PLANT?! THE CONTAMINATION! YOU IDIOT. AT LEAST THOSE GHOULS ARE GONE... GET OUT OF MY SIGHT**" — is the finest euphemism beat in the medium: she is angry about the mess and satisfied about the deaths, and she never gave the order.   ->  W10 (the checkpoint only searches the poor — our standing + logistics

### #101  THE ONLY WAY UP IS A FALLEN RADIO TOWER / FOUR PEOPLE ON A ROOF (Reilly's Rangers, Fallout 3)
  ->  This is the best LOGISTICS quest ever written, and it's dressed as a firefight
      Every beat is supply: a signal, a code, a battery, and bullets you hand out one person at a time. For a survival city-builder in a ruined city, it's a blueprint.
  ->  W1/W2/W5 (the building has no entrance + the route is a disaster that fell the right way + the real road network is underground — our district + HD tile repo + logistics 
      the top port, and it's aimed at our tile pipeline. The Statesman Hotel is **inaccessible from the ground.** The only way in is to enter the HOSPITAL NEXT DOOR, climb to the second floor, and walk across **a collapsed radio tower** that fell between the buildings — then drop through a hole. Nobody built that bridge; the apocalypse did. And the whole DC map works this way: "**A LOT OF MAIN STREETS ARE BLOCKED WITH DEBRIS**," so the real road network is the METRO. Punk, our Vegas is a ruined city with a real geography, and this is the lesson: the RUIN should generate the routes. Collapsed structures as bridges, blocked streets forcing underground paths, buildings enterable only from their neighbors. That's our HD tile repo + prefab factory doing navigation work, and MAP LAW holds — you place them, we build the plumbing that makes debris a road (ties our district + HD tile repo + prefab factory + street generation + logistics + VEGAS GEOGRAPHY + city-builder + MAP LAW; a top-tier port).
  ->  W6/W8/W9 (the dead quartermaster is the supply chain + you hand out ammo by the round + the siege resolves on a battery — our LOGISTICS + survival accounting + electricit
      STEAL all three. (a) **THEO.** The team's QUARTERMASTER is dead on the stairwell, next to a super mutant he killed, holding **all their ammo** in a locked box. His friends are twenty floors up, out of bullets, and **only their unconscious leader knows the code.** That is a logistics failure written as a corpse, and you can walk over him without noticing. Our [READ] + logistics should produce those constantly. (b) You resupply the Rangers **by hand, per person, in specific calibers** — 150 5mm for Brick, 50 10mm for Butcher, 50 5.56 for Donovan — and it's OPTIONAL, unmarked, and it changes who lives.       bank both. (a) An **automated distress call** playing on a loop, receivable from three different districts, from people who may already be dead. (b) And the quest-giver **CANNOT GIVE THE QUEST** — she's in a coma, and you have to pass **Medicine 60** or talk a ghoul doctor into waking her.   ->  W7/W10 (the rescue makes it worse + the climax inverts the verb — our companions + combat dial + Pacifist Law

For our Dead Eye Dial and our Pacifist Law, that's the shape of a fight worth having: the objective isn't the enemies, it's the four people behind you (ties our companions + combat dial + difficulty packages + PACIFIST LAW + district + death-math + fold).
  ->  REWARD (the geomapper — our district + persistent consequence

### #102  SEVEN DOORS ON ONE ROOF / WRONG CITY, WRONG PEOPLE (Nocturne Op. 55 N. 1, Cyberpunk 2077)
  ->  This is the finale architecture for our three endings
      Seven doors, all on one roof, each unlocked by something you did without knowing, each priced in a different person.
  ->  W2/W3 (your options are your friendships + every door costs the person who opened it — our STANDING + faction web + companions + Liberate/Respect/Become
      the top port, and it's our finale's blueprint. V's ending options are **not stats.** They're relationships: no Panam questline, no Aldecaldos door. No Rogue questline, no legend door. No specific lines in **Chippin' In**, no solo run. **THE NUMBER OF WAYS YOU'RE ALLOWED TO END YOUR STORY EQUALS THE NUMBER OF PEOPLE WHO'D SHOW UP FOR YOU.** Our LIBERATE/RESPECT/BECOME should work exactly this way — which finales are even AVAILABLE depends on our 13 factions' standing and who the dynasty actually built something with across three generations. And W3 is the Megaton law at finale scale: every door kills the person who opened it (ties our standing + faction web (13 factions) + companions + Liberate/Respect/Become + Megaton law + fold + generational persistence + conscience system; a top-tier port).
  ->  W4/W10 (the prize for winning is six months + the only cure costs everything — our death-math + FOLD + persistent consequence
      STEAL the shape. Every "good" ending in Cyberpunk hands you a **clock**: the legend has six months, the convoy has six months, the survivor is "**GOING TO LOSE MY SIGHT, MY HEARING AND MY ABILITY TO BREATHE.**" And the ONE ending that removes the clock — The Tower — costs **two years asleep, all your cyberware, and every relationship you built**: "**THEY WAKE UP AND FIND THAT TWO YEARS HAVE PASSED... EVERYONE ELSE HAD ASSUMED V WAS DEAD AND MOVED ON.**" The verdict: "**IT OFFERS LIFE, BUT AT THE COST OF EVERYTHING THAT MADE THAT LIFE WORTH LIVING.**" Punk — our FOLD is three generations and our dynasts die. That's the design: **survival is the most expensive option**, and a dynast who chooses to live long may find the city moved on without them (ties our death-math + fold + generational persistence + persistent consequence + MEDICINE currency + companions + standing + district + Liberate/Respect/Become).
  ->  W7 (the afterlife is a product with a name — our AMALGAMATION + NETWORK
      bank it hard. **MIKOSHI** is a corporate server where souls are stored. The program is called **SECURE YOUR SOUL.** The offer is: get uploaded, get shelved indefinitely, wait for "**A BODY THAT'S COMPATIBLE.**" That's our AMALGAMATION's commercial layer — the uploaded dead as INVENTORY, with a brand name, a sales pitch, and a waiting list. And The Devil's outcome is our Network's endgame: "**V EITHER BECOMES A DIGITAL GHOST, TRAPPED IN MIKOSHI WITH NO GUARANTEE OF A NEW BODY, OR RETURNS TO EARTH AS ARASAKA'S LAB RAT, ONLY TO FIND THEMSELVES ABANDONED BY ALL THEIR FRIENDS**" (ties our AMALGAMATION + Amalgamation threat logic + NETWORK + recorded-vs-unrecorded + [READ] + death-math + faction web + Liberate/Respect/Become, Bloodborne Q92, SOMA Q34).
  ->  W5/W6 (the hardest path is the one where nobody else dies + the secret is unlocked by listening — our PACIFIST LAW + [READ] + companions
      bank both. **DON'T FEAR THE REAPER** is unlocked by saying the right things in **Chippin' In** — a conversation where Johnny takes you to visit his dead friends and you either engage honestly or don't. Nothing flags it as a test. And what it unlocks is the run where **"NOBODY DIES DURING THE FINAL MISSION"** because you go alone. ### #106  THE INFORMATION IS BEHIND A HANGOVER / YOU HAVE TO PREACH TO THE PEOPLE YOU KEPT AWAKE (Mysteri
  ->  This is the best STANDING quest ever written

  ->  This is our SURVIVAL ACCOUNTING as a moral instrument, and the best "the system is the villain" quest ever built

  ->  Punk, **one man

### #125  "TALI: TREASON"
  ->  THE INHERITANCE THAT IS ALSO THE INDICTMENT [core port]
  ->  System
      THE FOLD / dynasty succession / [READ] Gen 2 inherits a sealed record from Gen 1's era. It is the only document that clears the current dynast of a charge the settlement is actually going to rule on. It is also, in the same file, the proof that the previous dynast did the thing.
  ->  One artifact. Not splittable. Not redactable
      The player cannot present half. Against **Q98 (Isidor's body)** and **Q113 (Isidor's list)**: Pathologic hands you a corpse and a list of names with no reason attached.   ->  THE VERDICT IS ANNOUNCED BY HOW SOMEONE SAYS HELLO [W2, W3]

      faction reputation / naming / the 13 factions Bohemia already has factions-as-characters. Give one of them a **naming grammar** — a title that encodes belonging. Then, at the top of a quest, have a friendly NPC greet the dynast with the wrong title, warmly, without malice, because that's what the paperwork now says. No combat. No stat. **A word changed and you're out.** And then — **W3, the better half** — if the dynast wins the trial anyway, they can **keep the wrong name.** Permanently. It shows up in every subsequent greeting, every generation, and it means *I was thrown out and I came back and I kept the receipt.* The Amalgamation, of course, files people by name. **[PENDING, Paolo's call]** — whether a dynast can choose a name the Amalgamation didn't assign, and whether that's an act of freedom or an act of deletion.
  ->  THE HEARING IS A PROXY WAR [W6, F9]
  ->  System
      the 13 factions / mayor persistence / the Amalgamation-vs-NETWORK argument A Bohemia tribunal where **four faction reps** each want a different thing and none of them care about the accused:
  ->  one wants a war footing and needs a live threat to prove
  ->  one wants the Amalgamation's dead as a *resource*, and needs research access
  ->  one wants coexistence and needs an atrocity to point at
  ->  FIX F9 IMMEDIATELY
      Mass Effect diagnoses the facade and then makes every reply noncommittal. In Bohemia the tribunal **is a governance event**: the verdict moves the actual faction war-posture number, permanently, in the direction of whoever's argument you fed. You don't just learn it's a proxy fight — **you get to pick who wins the proxy fight, and the settlement lives with it for a generation.** Cross-ref **Q107 (Frostpunk Londoners — people you saved organizing against you)** and **Q104 (Vault 11 — a community that gave its atrocity a procedure)**.
  ->  BUILD THE CUT VERSION [F10]
  ->  System
      [READ] / the tribunal The cut ME2 design: each admiral's specific claim individually refutable with a specific document found in the dungeon. **That is the quest Bohemia should build**, because Bohemia already has [READ] and already has a record system. Four claims. Four documents in the ruin. You find zero, one, two, three, or four. **The verdict is a tally, not a switch.** Find two of four and you get a hung tribunal, which is its own outcome with its own consequences. This also **fixes F1**: the evidence you gather is no longer an optional MacGuffin. It is the mechanism. The dungeon run is load-bearing. And the father's file is a **fifth** document — the one that refutes *all four at once* and detonates.
  ->  NO KARMA BAR, AND THIS QUEST IS THE PROOF [F3, F2]
  ->  System
      CONSCIENCE SYSTEM — FINAL +30 Paragon for lying under oath. +30 Renegade for submitting true evidence that frees an innocent woman.
  ->  Print it on the wall
      This is the single best argument in 125 files for Bohemia's no-karma-bar law. The moment the scene gets a score, the score contradicts the scene, and the player optimizes toward the number instead of the person. **Q121 proved the same thing with "+30 PARAGON" on a button. This is the second conviction on the same charge.** Bohemia's version: the tribunal outcome writes to **relationships and faction posture**. Nothing writes to a morality total, because there isn't one. And **F2**: no Charm gate. Which leads directly to —
  ->  THE MERCY THAT SHOWS UP IN COURT [W8]
  ->  System
      persistent consequence / PACIFIST LAW Bohemia already has the mechanism from **Q123 (Come Fly With Me)**: mercy shows up in the passenger manifest. This is the same law, aimed at a courtroom.   ->  Requirements

  ->  THE MOTIVE LANDS BEFORE THE CRIME [W4]
  ->  System
      [READ] as level design / ruin generation

  ->  NO LOOT IN A ROOM WITH A NAMED BODY [F6, F7]
  ->  System
      ART PHILOSOPHY / inventory / production law
  ->  LOCK THIS AS A PRODUCTION LAW
      Bohemia has three currencies (medicine, electricity, resources) and a scavenging loop that touches every room. The scavenge verb is removed in that room, not just unrewarded. Same family as **Q118 / Q122 / Q123: the game REMOVES THE VERB.** Q125 says do it for grief, not just for violence. And **F7**: **no points for the hug.** The comfort option exists, it is written well, and it pays nothing and is logged nowhere.

  ->  Suppression is a delay, not a deletion
      Which is the Amalgamation's thesis stated from the other side — the Amalgamation exists precisely because nothing anybody uploaded was ever really deleted. Cross-ref **Q119 (Mikhaila's father)**: truth as a two-button PLAY/DELETE decision made alone. Q125 adds: **DELETE doesn't work, and you find out from someone gloating in your inbox.** Cross-ref **Q116 / Q119** and **FLAW LAW 3**: this is a persistent-consequence flag spanning a generation boundary. **It needs a regression gate in `bohemia_tests.js` on day one.** Q116 shipped a flag bugged for twenty-five years.   ->  THE PRIVATE TRUTH [Stage 8]
  ->  System

  ->  Bohemia needs this verb
      Not "confess" — **confide**. It is not a choice with a consequence tree. It is a scene where you get to stop being a politician for ninety seconds. **[PENDING, Paolo's call]** — whether confiding creates a persistent risk (he might tell someone, later, in Gen 3) or whether it's a clean, safe, human moment that the game just gives you.   ->  BUILD THE CONSEQUENCE FIRST [F10, method]
  ->  Q123 established it: BUILD THE CONSEQUENCE BEFORE THE CONTENT
      ME2 cut four evidence-vs-admiral rebuttals and shipped a corridor shooter with the courtroom trimmed to a switch. The consequence got scoped out and the content survived, which is exactly backward. For the Bohemia tribunal: **write the four verdict states and their generational effects FIRST.** Then write the documents. Then build the ruin. If scope cuts, cut the ruin, not the tribunal. --- --- # V2 TOP-UP — 7/16/26. #125 was built v1 hours before FORMAT LAW v2 locked; this adds the missing v2 sections. # Original file untouched above. ### #126  "RAPHAEL'S DEAL / THE HOUSE OF HOPE"
  ->  THE HONEST BUYER [W1, W2, core port]
  ->  System
      the 13 factions / NETWORK / three currencies Bohemia needs a faction rep who **never lies, never cheats, and always pays first.** Not a trickster. A **counterparty.** He states what he wants, states what he'll do with it, hands over the medicine before you've delivered anything, and at the end of the generation he does exactly what he said he would. The Amalgamation's whole logic makes this land harder than it does in BG3: **it is made of people who were honest about wanting to be remembered.** Nobody was tricked into uploading. They signed. **.bq, in Bohemia's voice:** ``` @TALK offer_open speaker=buyer entry=act>=2 @SAY I want the plant. All of it. The pumps, the maps, the names of everyone who knows the pumps. @SAY I am going to use it to make sure nobody in this valley ever has to ask me for water twice. @SAY They will ask once. Then they will not have to ask again. That is what I want. I have said it. @SAY Here is the medicine. Take it. Count it. I will wait. @OPT "You're giving it to me first." [gate: none] -> offer_need @OPT "What's the catch." [gate: none] -> offer_terms @OPT
  ->  THE NOVERB IS THE PORT
      You can ask what he wants. **You cannot ask what it costs the people who are not in the room.** The externality is unpriceable and the format proves it by having no line for it.
  ->  THE REFUSAL THAT COSTS NOTHING AND NEVER EXPIRES [W3]
  ->  System
      persistent consequence / generational persistence
  ->  FIX F1 FIRST
      BG3's temptation is strictly worse than robbing him, so it isn't a temptation. **Bohemia's offer must be genuinely the better deal on the numbers.** Cheaper, safer, faster, and it works. If the player is only refusing because the wiki says the heist has better loot, the quest is a difficulty setting. Then: **refusing costs nothing and the offer never closes.** He waits. Across the act. **Across the GENERATION.** Gen 1 refuses; the offer is still open when Gen 2 inherits, and the file says who refused it and when.
  ->  The Bohemia escalation BG3 can't do
      every generation the offer stays refused, **the terms get better.** He is patient and he is compounding. By Gen 3 he is offering so much that the refusal is no longer a moral position, it's an expensive habit somebody's grandmother started. `@OPT "No." [gate: none] -> offer_refused @DO set_flag refused_gen1` and the validator fires GEN_FLAG_TEST, because a flag crossing a generation boundary needs a named test. Q116 shipped one bugged for twenty-five years.

  ->  THE COMFORT VERB THAT DOES NOT EXIST [W7]

  ->  LOCK THIS AS A WRITING LAW
      > **NO COMFORT VERBS.** Bohemia never offers a line whose only function is to let the player feel decent about a thing they are not going to do. No "I'll come back." No "I'm sorry, I have to." No "I'll fix this later." **If the player wants to be decent, the verb is the DEED. There is no line.** Every previous instance of the removed-verb law (Q118, Q122, Q123, Q125) removes a **cruelty**. Any later system may surface the gap. A blackout you can only reassemble correctly is a corridor; ours can be honestly misremembered.
  ->  PORT 3 — ONE GRIEVANCE STICKS [F2's law]
      system: faction memory / the conduct book (#143)
      Most of a blackout's harm is comic and resets; ONE grievance persists — a person who stays hurt, a debt the district remembers, a reputation dinged. The release valve earns its lightness by letting exactly one thing not be funny, and the fold carries it.
  ->  PORT 4 — CHOOSING TO NOT BE PRESENT [F3's law]
      system: the fold / the dial / conscience
      When a Bohemia quest offers a VOLUNTARY loss of control (drink to oblivion, elect a memory edit, skip a fold beat), the choosing is itself a recorded act with a cost: the dynast elected absence, and something happened while they were gone that they now own. The voluntary blackout as a moral act, not just a setup.

      If a comic quest carries a serious question underneath, ONE beat lets the ache through — a line, a pause where the delusion's cost is briefly visible — so the theme reaches even the player who came for the joke (#163's the-costume-must-crack law).
  ->  PORT 3 — BOTH PATHS FULLY IMAGINED [F2's law]
      system: factions / the Amalgamation
      If a quest offers serve-the-delusion vs shatter-it, both are fully IMAGINED — the truth-path given its own weight, not a flat punishment — so the dilemma is real rather than a preferred ending with a bad option beside it (#181's equal-outcomes law).
  ->  PORT 4 — THE DELUDED FLICKERS ONCE [F3's law]
      system: the Amalgamation / companions
      If the weight depends on a delusion being load-bearing for a person, that person flickers once — a near-doubt, a defended certainty — so the belief reads as coherence held against a crack, not a stuck subroutine (#162's the-crack-makes-it-human law).
